"yadvaitanna pashyati na tu taddvitIyamasti" ityasyArtho yaditi | "tato.anyadvibhaktaM yatpashyet" ityetadvyAkriyate || pradhAneti || anyadavatAravyatiriktamIshvareNa bhinnatayA dR^iShTatvAtpradhAnapuruShAdikaM bhinnameveshvarAdityuktam | abhinnatayA sarvaj~neneshvareNAdR^iShTatvAchcha bhinnamityupapAdakaM "pashyan vai tanna pashyati" iti | etadvAkyaM vyAkriyate || pashyanniti || pradhAnAdInAM svato bhinnatvena darshanamIshvarasya bhramaH kiM na syAdityAshaMkAparihArarUpaM-"na hi draShTurdraShTerviparilopo vidyate" ityetadvyAkriyate || na hIti || viparilopo viparItatvam | avinAshitvAditi | nityatvena nirdoShatvAdityarthaH |
"paramaM brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati" iti shrutiM vyakhyAtuM tadupayuktamAha || brahmANIti || shrutivyAkhyAnaM apIti | yadyapi paramaM brahma veda tathApi brahmaiva bhavati na paraM brahma bhavatItyarthaH | kuta itthaM kalpyate? parabrahmaj~nAnena parabrahmatvaM bhavatityevArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || yadIti || yadi jIvasya muktau parameshvaraikyaM syAttarhi saMsAre.api tathA syAt | prAgbhinnasya pashchAdabhedAnupapatternaitadyujyate | tathAtve duHkhAnupapatteriti bhAvaH | kuto na syAdduHkhitetyata Aha || duHkhIti || parameshvarabhUtasyApyaj~nAnavashAdduHkhitvamityata Aha || kuta iti || sarvaj~nasyApi bhrAntyA.aj~nAnamityata Aha || kveti || bhramasyAdhiShThAnAj~nAnamUlatvAdaj~nAnasya cha bhrAntimUlatvAN^gIkAre.anyAshrayateti bhAvaH | "ahaM brahmAsmi" tattvamasIti shrutidvayaM vyAchaShTe || aheyatvAditi || asanAnmiteriti || svasmin parimiternirAsAdityarthaH | virodhinAM nirasanAtpramitirUpatvAchcheti vA | tviT.h (tviN^) prakAshana iti dhAtostejastvAttvamitIritaH | na kevalametachChabdavAchyatvaM harerapi tu sarvashabdavAchyatvaM chetyAha || sarvairiti || sarvashabdavAchyatve.api rUpavisheShaniyamo.astItyAha || yuShmaditi ||
tattvamasIti vAkyaM nAbhedaparam | pUrvottaravAkyAnanusAritvAditi bhAvenA.adita eva prakArAntareNa vyAkriyate | tatra "sarvAn vedAnadhItya mahAmanA anUchAnamAnI stabdha eyAya" ityetadvyAkriyate || sarvAniti || "taM ha pitovAcha shvetaketo yannu khalu 
somyaivaM mahAmAnA asUchAnamAnI stabdho.asyuta tamAdeshamaprAkShyo yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matamavij~nAtaM vij~nAtaM bhavati" ityetadvyAkriyate || akR^itAchAramiti || Adishyata ityAdesho nArayaNaH | j~nAte shrute mate cha | avij~nAtaj~nAnAdInAmiti || avij~nAtAshrutAmataj~nAnashravaNamananAnAmityarthaH | avij~nAtAnyaj~nAnAdInAM yatphalaM tattadabhAve.api bhagavajj~nAnAdimAtreNApi bhavatItyarthaH | avij~nAtAnyaj~nAnAdInAM jAtAnAmapi yatphalaM tadapi bhagavajj~nAnAdau jAta eva jAtaM bhavatIti cha | paramAtmaj~nAnAdau satyanyadaj~nAtAdyapi j~nAtAdivadbhavatIti vA | evaMvidhatvAdIshvarasya tajj~nAne svAtmano.atyantAdhamatvaj~nAnasambhavena keshavo.asmItyAdyabhimAnAyogAnnAsau tvayA pR^iShTa iti bhAvaH | tatrA.adyayojanAdvaye prAdhAnyaM hetuH | tR^itIyayojanAyAM sAdR^ishyaM hetuH |
jAtamapi jagajj~nAnAdi paramAtmaj~nAnAdau satyeva saphalamiti kathamityata Aha || tadadhInamiti || bhagavajj~nAnAdi tAvadevaM bhavati | vashIkR^itavishvo jagatsR^iShTyAdikarteshvara iti | evaM cha bhagavajj~nAnAdau sati jagattadadhInamiti j~nAnAdikaM dR^iDhaM bhavati | tatashcha mokShAdiphalaM bhavatItyarthaH |
evamaj~nAtasyApi jagato j~nAnAdinA phalaM kiM na syAdityataH kA phalapratyAshA pratyutAnartha eva bhavatItyAha || svAtantryeNeti || uktarItyA bhagavajj~nAnAdyabhAve jagataH svAtantryeNaiva j~nAnAdi prApyate | tachcha mithyAj~nAnatvAdanarthakR^idityarthaH |
sAdR^ishyAdebhagavajj~nAnAdau satyanyajj~nAtAdivadbhavatItyatroktaM "yathA somyekena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt" iti dR^iShTAntaM vyAchaShTe || yathA cheti || j~nAtaM j~nAtAdi | prAdhAnyAdbhagavajj~nAnAdimAtreNAj~nAtAderapyanyasya j~nAnAdiphalaM bhavati, bhagavajj~nAnAdau satyeva j~nAtasyApyanyasya j~nAnAdeH phalaM bhavatItyubhayatroktaM "vAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam" iti dR^iShTAntaM vyAchaShTe || yatheti || yasmAtsAMketikanAmadheyasya vAchA.a.arambhaNaM kriyate atastadvikAro.ata evApradhAnam | mR^ittiketyAdisaMskR^itaj~nAnamAtreNa sAMketikAj~nAnAdAvapi tatphalaM vidvAniti vyavahAraviShayatvAdikaM bhavati | saMskR^itanAmaj~nAna eva cha sAMketikAnAmaj~nAnaM saphalaM bhavati | tanmAtreNa vidvAniti vyavahAraviShayatvAdyabhAvAdityarthaH || tanmUlamiti || tatpradhAnakatvAdityarthaH |
"evaM somya sa Adesho bhavati" iti dArShTAntikavAkyaM vyAchaShTe || evamiti|| pradhAno.atastajj~nAnAdinoktaprakAradvayenAnyaj~nAnAdisAphalyaM bhavatIti sheShaH | evaM sadR^ishashcheti draShTavyam | prAdhAnyameveshvarasya kuta ityataH sadeva somyetyAdinA svAtantryeNa jagatkAraNatvamuktam | tadevAha || svatantraH kAraNabhUta iti || Ishvaro.ahamiti bhAvAkaraNe hetutayeshvaramAhAtmyamuktam | mAhAtmyAntaraM chochyate-"sanmUlAH somyemAH sarvAH prajAH sadAyatanAH satpratiShThAH" iti | tadarthamAha || tanmUlamiti || mAhAtmyAnramuktvA abhedabuddhiM mA kurvityuchyate -"sa eSho.aNimaitadAtmyamidaM sarvaM tatsatyaM sa AtmA tattvamasi shvetaketo"iti | tadvyAchaShTe || sa iti || vyApakaH pUrNa ityAtmashabdasyArthadvayam | pUrNo guNaiH | naiva so.asIti | atattvamasIti vibhajya vyAkhyAnAntaram | 
jIveshvarabhede "sa yathA shakuniH" ityAdinoktadR^iShTAntavAkyAni vyAchaShTe || yatheti || yadapi "jIvenAtmanA.anupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi" iti, "sa eSha jIvenAtmanA.anuprabhUtaH" iti jIveshAbhedAbhidhAyakavatpratIyamAnaM vAkyadvayaM tat "ityAdishrutivirodha" ityAdipadagR^ihItaM vyAkhyAyate || na iti || "jIvApetaM vAva kiledaM mriyate | na jIvo mriyate" ityasyArthastadadhInamiti |
"prapaJNcho yadi vidyeta nivarteta na saMshayaH" ityAdishrutiH bhedamithyAtvAbhidhAyakavatpratIyamAnA prAgAdipadagR^ihItA vyAkhyAyate || jIveti || vida utpattAviti dhAtumAshritya "yadi vidyeta" ityetadutpAdyashchediti vyAkhyAtam | bhrAntikalpitatvAdbhedasya kathamanAdinityatetyAshaMkAnivartakasya "mAyAmAtramidaM dvaitam" ityasyArtho viShNoriti | bhedasya satyatve kathamadvaitaM sthAnAntare kathyata ityata uktaM advaitaM paramArthata iti | asyArtho.advaita iti | anena paramArthata iti tasiH prathamArtha ityuktaM bhavati | advaitavAkyaM paramArtho bhagavAnadvaita ityAhetyarthaH | kiM tatparamatvamityata Aha || paramatvamiti || evaM paramatvavato.advaitatvaM nAma kimityata Aha || ityAdaya iti || so.aya paramadvaite abhAvaH | tadidaM paramatvavato.advaitatvaM tadevAdvaitashrutyartha ityarthaH | sarvAdvaitamevArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || santIti ||
bAdhakAbhAvAchcha na bhedasya kalpitatvamityarthapratipAdakaM vikalpa iti vAkyam | tasyArtho vikalpa iti | "sa AtmA tattvamasi" ityAdivAkyasya bhedaparatvasiddhyarthaM "yathA somya" ityAdivAkyasya svoktamarthamanaN^gIkR^itya arthAntaratAkalpanAyAM udAhR^itashrutivirodho bAdhakaH | bAdhakAntaraM chAha || eketi || yathaikamR^itpiNDavij~nAnena sarvaM mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt, yato nAmarUpAtmakaM mR^iNmayaM vAgAlambanamAtraM na tu pAramArthikaM, mattikaiva satyA tathA paramAtmaj~nAne sati jagajj~nAnaM bhavati | tato.atirekeNAbhAvAdityanyathA vyakhyAnaM na yujyate | "mR^itA j~nAtayA sarvaM mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt | vAchArambhaNaM vikAro mR^ittikaiva satyA" ityetAvatA pUrNatvenaikAdishabdAnAM vaiyyarthyAt | sarvamR^iNmayAnAmekamR^itpiNDAtirekeNAbhAvAbhAvAt | nAmadheyasyApi vikAratvAditi bhAvaH |
kiJNcha vAchArambhaNavAkye yadi IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya paramAtmanyAropitatayA tato.atirekeNAbhAvo vivakShitastarhi pratij~nAnaM 
paramAtmaj~nAnna jagajj~nAnaM na syAt | satyaj~nAnena mithyAj~nAnasyAnupapatteH | virodhAttayorj~nAnayorityAha || na cheti || nanu paramAtmaj~nAnena Daganmithyeti j~nAyata eva | ्taH kathamuchyate brahmaNyAropitatve DagataH tajj~nAnena DagaDj~nAnAnupapattirityata Aha || na hIti || evaM chetparamAtmaj~nAnena prapaJNchAbhAvaj~nAnaM bhavatIti vaktavyam | na tu prapaJNchaj~nAnaM brahmaj~nAnena bhavatIti | tathA loke vyavahArAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | ito.api nAtra prapaJNchasya paramAtmAtirekeNAbhAvo vivakShita ityAha || navakR^itva iti || kimato yadyevaM vAchArambhaNashrutirbhedapakShe yuktetyata Aha || tasmAditi || tasmAtpUrvavAkyAnAM bhedaparatvAdityarthaH |
atattvamasIti bhedaparatayA yojanAyAM "aitadAtmyamidaM sarvam" iti pUrvavAkyavirodhaH syAdityatastasya shrutyoktamarthaM smArayati || aitadAtmyamiti || astvevamAtmasambandhIti yojanA | sambandhashcha tAdAtmyamityataH svasvAmibhAvasambandha eveti bhAvenAha || taditi || tattvamasIti padavibhAgamabhyupetyApi pUrvottaravAkyAnAM bhedaparatvAt bhedaparatayA shrutisiddhamarthAntaraM chAha || tvamapIti || na so.asIti vyAvR^ittikathanamAtram | ito़.apyaitadAtmyaparAmarsho.ayamityAha || taditi || aitadAtmyaparAmarshe taditipadasyaikaliN^gatvaM guNaH syAt | tatashchaitadAtmyaparAmarsho.ayamityarthaH | prAchInapakShepi tasmAdanyadataditi na liN^gavaiShamyam | 
bhavedayamaitadAtmyaparAmarsho bhavatAmanuguNo yadyaitadAtmyapadena tatsambandhyuchyate | na cha tannishchitam | sarvo.api IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchaH paramAtmAtmaka ityapyarthasambhavAditi chet | tatkimatra IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya sAkShAtparamAtmAbhedo.abhidhIyata iti te matam uta IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNcha eva paramAtmAtirikto nAstIti svarUpato niShidhyate? nAdyaH | mithyAsatyayorabhedAyogAt | dvitIyaM dUShayati || avidyamAnamiti || yadyeShA shrutirIsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchaM paramAtmAtirekeNa pratiShedhati tadonmattavAkyavadapramANaM syAt | avidyamAnasyaivesheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya svayameva tadaikShatetyAdau paramAtmAtirekeNa vihitatvAt | na cha vAchyamatra niSheddhuM tadaikShatetyAdAvIsheshitavyAdiprapaJNcho.anUdyata eva, ato na doSha iti | IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya shrutiM vinA.atmano bhinnatvenAprAptatayA.anuvAdAyogAditi bhAvaH |
ito.api niShedhAya tadaikShatetyAdau prapaJNcho.anUdyata iti na yujyate | "yadidaM vadanti tanna yujyate" iti vAkyena, niShedhe visheShayuktyA cha hInatvAt | tadvinA.anuvAdasya kvApyadR^iShTatvAdityAha || anuvAdo.apIti || tAdR^ishavAkyAdyabhAve.api niShedhAyAtrAnuvAdaH prapaJNchasyetyaN^gIkAre ko doSha iti chet adR^iShTakalpanetyekaM dUShaNam | aparaM chAha || atiprasaN^gashcheti || kathamityata Aha || abhedeti || anyatheti sambadhyate | yadyetAdR^ishavAkyAdyabhAve.apyaitadAtmyamityAdau niSheddhuM tadaikShatetyAdinA paramAtmAtiriktatayA prapaJNcho.anUdyata iti kalpyate tarhi tadaikShatetyAdau prapaJNchasya paramAtmAtirekeNAbhAvaM niShidhyAtiriktatvena bhAvaM vidhAtumaitadAtmyamityAdinA prapaJNchasya paramAtmAtirekeNAbhAvo.anUdyata ityapi syAdavisheShAdityarthaH |
itashcha niShedhAyAyaM prapaJNchasya paramAtmAtiriktatayA sadbhAvAnuvAdo na bhavatItyetadeva yuktamityAha || sarveti || anuvAdo bhavan shAkhAdAveva bhavet | tadante tu niShedhaH | na chAtra tadasti | bhedasyaiva shAkhAnteShUktatvAt | ato.api na bhedasya niShedhAya shrutAvanuvAda ityarthaH | shAkhAnteShu kAstA bhedoktaya ityata Aha || neti ||
yaduktamabhedAnuvAdena bhedopadeshaH syAditi na tadyujyate | abhedasya shrutiM vinA.aprAptatvAt | kiM nAmesheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya paramAtmabhinnatayA.anuvAdena tanniShedha eva yuktaH | IsheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya paramAtmabhinnatAyAH pratyakShAdipraptatvAdityata Aha || na cheti || atreshvarapadena paramAtmochyate | paramAtmana eva pratyakShAdyasiddhatvena tatpratiyogikesheshitavyAdiprapaJNchasya bhedaH sutarAM pratyakShAdinA gR^ihyata iti tanna | tathAsati prapaJNchabhinnatayA shrutAvapi paramAtmanirUpaNaprasaN^gAt | anyathA pratyakShAdinA.api tadbhedasya viShayIkartumashkyatvAt | tathA chonmattavAkyameveti bhAvaH | Ishvarasyaiva pratyakShAdinA.asiddherIsheshitavyasya cha tadAkAreNAsiddheH paramAtmanaH sakAshAdIshvarAdirUpaprapaJNchasya bhedaH sutarAM tenAsiddha iti vA |
ito.api na paramAtmAtiriktaprapaJNchaniShedho yujyata ityata Aha || tatpakSha iti || yadi paramAtmAtiriktaH sarvo.api prapaJNcho mithyA syAt tadA sarvashrutInAM vaiyarthyaM syAt | tathAhi | "ekamevAdvitIyam" "yaH sarvaj~naH" ityAdishrutiraikyAdidharmapratipAdikA uta AtmAsvarUpapratipAdikA | Adye.apyaikyasArvaj~nAdidharmAH kiM svarUpAtiriktAH svarUpaM vA | nAdyaH | tathAtve mithyAtvApAtAt | dvitIyastu tR^itIyo.antarbhavati | nApyasau yuktaH | svarUpasya svataH siddhatvena pratipAdanabaiyarthyAditi bhAvaH |
shuddhasvarUpasyApratipAdyatve.api bhedAbhAvasArvaj~nAdyupalakShitasvarUpasya pratipAdyaratvAnna shrutivaiyarthyamityata Aha || lakShiteti || lakShitasyApi shuddhAdvisheShAbhAvena tadvadasyApyapratipAdyatvAnna tatpratipAdakatvaM shruteryuktamityarthaH | kutaH shuddhAdvisheShAbhAvo lakShitasyetyata Aha || nirvisheShatveti || lakShitamiti  yadoktaM tadaiva tasya nirvisheShatvamapyuktameva | anyathA vishiShTatvApattyA mithyAtvApAtAt | atastasya na shuddhAdvisheSha iti bhAvaH | nanu bhavatu dharmANAM mithyAtvam | tathApi shrutestatpratipAdakatve ko doSha ityata Aha || mithyeti ||
ito.api nA.atmAtiriktasya sarvasya mithyAtvaM yuktamityAha || mithyAtvamiti || AtmAtiriktasya sarvasya mithyAtve tanmithyAtvaM 
satyaM mithyA vA | nAdyaH | AtmAtiriktaM sarvaM mithyeti pakShakShateH | ato mithyetyevAN^gIkAryamiti bhAvaH | kimato yadyevamityata Aha || ata iti || itashcha nAtmavisheShANAM mithyAtvamiti vA.a.aha || mithyeti ||
na sArvaj~nAdivisheShA asanto yena shruteraprAmANyaM syAt | nApi shuddhaM lakShyaM j~nAnasvarUpaM shrutivedyamityuchyate | yenoktadoShaH syAt | kiM nAmaikasminnevAtmani 	upAdhibhedabhinnetannimittasArvaj~nAdivisheShAshcha 	bhavanti | tadupAdhibhedabhinnamaupAdhikavisheShavishiShTasvarUpaM shrutipratipAdyamiti chet, kimasAvupAdhiH mithyA satyo vA || Adye doShamAha || upAdhIti || upAdhikR^ita evAtmani bhedo visheShAshchetyaN^gIkR^ityopAdhermithyAtvAN^gIkAre tadbhinnasvarUpasya tannimittavisheShANAM cha mithyAtvaM syAt | tathAcha tadabhidhAyakashruteraprAmANyaM syAt | neha nAnetyAdau niShedhAya mithyAbhUtamapi taduchyate shrutAviti chettarhi svayameva mithyAbhUtamupAdhibhedabhinnasvarUpaM tannimittavisheShAMshcha vidhAya punastanniShedhe shruterunmattavAkyatvameva syAt | niShedhAya tadanUdyata iti chenna | upAdhibhedabhinnasvarUpasya tannimittavisheShANAM cha pratyakShAdyaprAptatvenAnuvAdAnupapatteriti bhAvaH | dvitIyaM dUShayati | satyeti || yadyapyatrApasiddhAnto vaktuM shakyaH | tathApi tasyAtisphuTatvena doShAntaramevoktam | brahmAtiriktasya satyatvamaN^gIkR^ityApi brahmaNyupAdhibhedamaN^gIkurvatAM dUShaNAya cha | AdipadenopAdherapyekadeshasambandha ityAdivakShyamANasaN^grahaH | satyopAdhipakShe.api doShAH samA ityanena mithyopAdhipakShe.apyeti bhavantIti sUchayati |
nanvekatve.apyAkAshasya tathA mahAnasAkAshagadadhUmAnubhavastasyaiva na sarvAkAshasyopAdhibhedAt | tathA.atrApi syAdityata Aha || achetanAnAmiti || kiM mahAnasAkAshasambandhavattve.api dhUmasya sarvAkAshasambandhAbhAvavadduHkhAshrayatvAbhAvo.astvityuchyate uta tadanubhAvabhAvavadanubhAvabhAvaH | nAdyaH | asmAkamaniShTAbhAvAt | na dvitIyaH | AkAshasyAchetanatvena anubhavaprApterevAbhAvena dR^iShTAntavaiShamyAditi bhAvaH | ayaM chAbhyupagamavAdaH | AkAshasyAntarbhedavattvAt | upasaMharati || ata iti || 18 ||
yaduktaM sarvaprakAreNAvinAshitvAdIshvaraH svatantra iti | tadayuktam | "ayamasya dehaviyogakartA", "anenAyaM dehAdviyojitaH" iti jIvasyApi svatantryapratIterityAshaMkAparihArAyochyate "ya enamiti" | tatra jIvasya dehaviyogAdau kathamapi kartR^itvaM nAstItyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || ya enamiti || ya enaM jIvaM svAtantryeNa dehaviyogakartAraM pashyati, yashchainaM jIvaM jIvAntareNa svAtantryeNa dehAdviyojitaM pashyati tau na vijAnIta ityevaM vyakhyAyam | na tu pAratantryeNamApi jIvasya hantR^itvAdikaM pashyan na jAnAtItyarthaH | kuto.anyo.artho na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || jIvasya pAratantryeNApi hantR^itvAbhAve "mayA hatAMstvaM jahi" itIshvarAdhInatayA jIvasya hantR^itvoktivirodhaH syAdityarthaH |
yaduktaM jIvo nitya iti na tadyuktam | "ayaM jIvasya hantA", "anenAyaM jIvo hataH" iti vyavahAreNa chetanasyAnityatvAvagamAdityAshaMkA parihArAyapyayameva shlokaH | tatra prathamapakShe ya enamiti padaM jIvaviShayatayA vyAkhyAtam | neshvaraviShayatayA | tatra dehaviyogarUpahananasya vivakShitatvAt | tatra jIvasyaiva svAtantryAbhAvAdIshvarasya tadbhAvAt | asmin pakShe tu "ya enaM chetanaM hantAraM pashyati sa na jAnAti" iti chetanaM prati hananasya vivakShitatvAt | chetanahananasya jIvavadIshvareNApyakaraNAt enamiti padamubhayorapi vAchakamityAha || chetanamiti || 19 ||
nanu jIvanityatvAdeH pUrvamevoktatvAtkimuttarashlokenetyata Aha || jIveti || nedaM bhagavadvAkyaM, yena punaruktiH syAti | kintu yaduktaM svayaM jIveshvarayorutpattivinAsharAhityam, Ishvarasya sharIrato.apyutpattyAdyabhAvena svAtantryaM, jIvasya svarUpato janmAdishUnyasyApi dehotpattyAdinA.asvAtantryaM tatra pramANatvena mantravarNo.ayamudAhriyata iti bhAvaH |
atreshvarapratipAdanApratIteH kathametadityato nAyaM bhUtvetyatra dehato.apyutpattirAhityashravaNAttasya cheshvaraliN^gatvAt pUrvArdhastatpratipAdaka iti bhAvenAha || ayamiti || etena vA shabdAdeva pUrvatra naJNo.anukarShasambhavAt kiM tadantareNeti parAstam | api chAtra "na mriyate" iti dehaviyogAbhAvashcha shrUyate | maraNashabdasya dehaviyoga eva prasiddhatvAddehaviyogAbhAvasya cheshvaraliN^gatvAt tatpratipAdakaH pUrvArdha iti bhAvenAha || maraNamiti || dehaviyoga iva svarUpanAshe.api maraNashabdasya prasiddhatvAt so.arthaH kiM na syAdityataH svarUpanAshe maraNashabdasya prasiddhireva nAstItyAha || na hIti || yadi maraNashabdasya na svarUpanAsho.arthaH tarhi IshvarasvarUpAnAshe nAyaM mantraH pramANaM syAt | tadabhidhAyakashabdAntarAbhAvAt | tathA cha maraNashabdasya svarUpanAshe.arthe grAhye naitadbalAt pUrvArdhasyeshvaraparatvasiddhirityata Aha || svarUpeti || nAtreshvarasya svarUpAnAsho vaktavyaH | yenaitatpadasya tatparatvaM kalpyate | yasya dehanAshopi nAsti tasya svarUpAnAshaH kimu vAchya iti kaimutyenaiva siddhetityarthaH |
atra jIvasyotpattyAdyabhAvAdikathanaM na shrUyata ityuttarArdhastadviShaya iti bhAvenAha || ayamiti || atrApIshvara eva pratipAdyaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || "na jAyate " "ajaH" iti paunaruktyam | nanu punaruktibhayena pUrvottarArdhayorviShayabhedakalpane shAshvatopyanya eva prasajyate | nityapadena punarukterityata Aha || neti || na shAshvatapadena nityatvamuchyate | yena punaruktiH syAt | api tu jIvopyajo nityashchettarhi IshvaravatsvAtantryAdimAnapi syAt | tathA cha na tatpUjA kAryeti shaMkAnirAsAya 
tasyAsvAtantaryAdyahAnamevochyata iti bhAvaH |
jIvasAyAsvAtantryAdikaM svarUpaM, tachcha na jahAti, tena cha shAshvata ityuchyata ityetatkuta ityata Aha || alpeti || tathApi purANa iti punaruktirityata Aha || purANIti || nAnena purANapadenAnAditvamuchyate | yena paunaruktyaM syAt | kintu jIvasyeshvaravadajatvAdisadbhAve.api kuto na svAtantryAdItyato dehotpattyAdibhAvena tadvadajatvAdyabhAva evochyata iti bhAvaH || 20 ||
yaduktaM "jIve svAtantryaM manyamAno na jAnAti" iti tatra "nAyaM hanti" iti heturuktaH | atha j~nAninAM tAdR^ishAbhimAnAbhAvashcha tatra heturuchyate "vedeti" | tatrAvinAshinityapadayoH paunaruktyaparihArAyArthabhedamAha || avinAshinamiti || jIvasya samIpoktatvAdenamityasya jIvaviShayatvapratItinirAsAyAha || enamiti || samastashlokaM shrutyaiva vyAchaShTe || kartR^itvamiti || jAnan avinAshitvAdihetuneti sheShaH | kartA kartR^itvAbhimAnI | jIvasya samIpoktatvAttadviShayo.ayaM shlokaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyashcheti || Ishvarasya sharIrApAyarahitatvAt tatparatve shakyate punaruktiparihAraH | na tu jIvaparatve | tasya dehanAshasadbhAvAt | ataH punaruktivirodhAte samIpoktamapi jIvaM vihAyeshvaragrahaNaM yuktamiti bhAvaH || 21 ||
nanvastvIshvaraviShaye shokAbhAvo, jIvaviShayo tu bhaviShyati | jIvo nityastasya dehayogaviyogau kaumArAdivadityukte.api sarvalokaprasiddhajanimR^itisadbhAvAt yuddhe cha tatprApteriyAshaMkAparihAratvena shlokamavatArayita || jIvasyeti || sharIrayogaviyogayoH kaumarAdivachChokakAraNatvAbhAvo.aN^gIkR^itashchettarhi janimR^itI api na shokakAraNaM, yataH sharIrayogaviyogAveva janimR^itI ityarthaH || 22 ||
astyIshvarasya svato nAshAbhAvaH | tathApi yuddhagatashastrAdikAraNavisheSheNa chChedAdiprApteH shoka ityAshaMkAparihAratvena shlokamavatArayati || kAraNat.apIti || anyathAtvaM ChedAdi || 23 ||
jIvaviShaye.apyetadAshaMkAparihArAya shlokamavatArayati || achChedyatveti || nanu "nityaH sarvagataH" iti nityatvaM punaH kimarthamuchyate | atra sarvagatavastupratipAdanAt kathaM chAsya jIvaviShayatvam? na chAyamardha IshvaraviShayaH | jIvasya samIpoktatvAdityata Aha || nityamiti || nityaM sarvagatasthANurityarthaH | kaH sarvagataH? kiM cha tatsthatvamityata Aha || sarvagata iti || nAtra nityatvaM sarvagatatvaM chochyate | yena punaruktirIshvaraviShayatvaM chAshaMketa | kintu "jIvasyApIshvaravadachChedyatvAdisadbhAve sarvasAmyam, tathAcha kiM tatpUjayA" ityato nityaM tadadhInatvAdyevochyata iti bhAvaH | sarvagatasthANutvoktyA vaiShamyaheturdarshitaH |
nanvatra sarvagata ityeva yuktam | na tu sarvagatastha it | sarvagatasayaivAchalatvopapatteH | aNau tadanupapatterityata Aha || hetuto.apIti || nAtrAchalapadena kriyArAhityamuchyate | yena sarvagata ityeva padavibhAgashaMkA | kintvastu jIvasyeshvarAdhInatvam | tadapi kadAchinnashyati | tatashcha sarvasAmyam | tathAcha na tatpUjA kAryetyataH tadadhInatvAnAsha evochyata iti bhAvaH | nityapadenaivAsyArthasya siddheH kimannatyata uktaM hetuta iti | nityamapi sarvagatasthatvaM varAdikAraNavisheSheNa nashyatviti shaM,AnirAkaraNAnnaitadvaiyarthyamiti bhAvaH | tathApi sanAtana ita punaruktirityata Aha || nAdeneti || na sanAtanapadena nityatvamuchyate | yena punaruktiH syAt | api tu svAtantryAbhAve jIvasya vidhiniShedhabaddhatvaM hetvantaramuchyata iti bhAvaH ata evAnUktahetUpanyAsAtprAk asvAtantryoktAvapyapaunaruktyam |
nanvachChedya iti shlokaH prakR^iteshvaraviShaya eva kiM na syAt | kimanena pratItapadavibhAgatyAgAdinetyata Aha || nityamiti || smR^itisamAkhyAnAjjIvaviShaya evAyaM shloka iti bhAvaH | ito.api nAyaM shloka IshvaraviShaya ityAha || achChedya iti || "nainaM Chindanti" itIshvarasyAchChedyatvAderuktatvAt "achChedyo.ayam" ityachChedyatvAdeH punaruktiprasaN^go.asya shlokasyeshvaraviShayatAyAm | ato nAyaM tatpara ityarthaH |
jIvasya samIpoktatvAt "avyakto.ayam" ityasyApi tadviShayatvapratItinirAsAyAha || yasminniti || yasminnayaM sthita ityuktyA sarvagatapadeneshvarasyApi samIpoktatvaM sUchayati | yadyatreshvaraH pratipAdyastarhitasmAdityuttaravAkyamanupapannaM syAt | na hIshvarasyAlvaktatvAdij~nAne yuddhagatashokAbhAvo bhavati | nApyasmin pakShe tasmAditi parAmarshaviShayo.asti | yadi tasya jIvaviShayatA tadA dUroktatvadeSha ityata Aha || evamiti || nAtra yuddhagatashoko nivAryate | nApi tasmAditi parAmarshaviShayAbhAvaH | yato.atrAchChedyatvAdisAmyAjjIvasyApi svAtantryeNa kimIshvarapUjayetyataH sanAtanatvAdihetunA Ishvarasyaiva svAtantryamuktam | astvIshvarasya svAtantryaM, kiM tAvatA tatpUjayetyato yasmAdIshvara eva svatantro.astasyaiva saMsArashokanAshakatvaM yujyate | sa cha svakarmaNA.avyaktatvAdiguNayuktatvena j~nAta eva sarvasaMsAraduHkhanAshaM saMsArashokaM pariharetyevochyata iti bhAvaH |
bhavedayamatrArtho.abhipreto yadi svakarmaNA bhagavajj~nAnaM, j~nAto bhagavAn sarvaduHanAshaM karotIti gItAbhimataM syAt | tadeva kuta ityata Aha || teShAmiti || atra mAM dhyAyanta ityanenaiva j~nAnaM labhyate |
evametatprakaraNaM jIveshvaraparatayA vyAkhyAya athAsyobhayaparatve yuktiM chAha || na tveveti || teShAmiti || atra mAM dhyAyanta ityanenaiva j~nAnaM labhyate |
evametatprakaraNaM jIveshvaraparatayA vyAkhyAya athAsyobhayaparatve yuktiM chAha || na tveveti || nanvekaH prasaN^gAdevopakrAntaH | prakaraNaM tvekaviShayameva kiM na syAdityataH sarvatrobhayaliN^gasadbhAvAdubhayaviShayaM prakaraNamityAha || dehina iti || astUpakramavashAdubhayoH prAkaraNikatvaM tathApi yadvAkyaM yadviShayatayA vyAkhyAtaM tasya tadviShayatA kuta ityato yadvAkyaM yadviShayatayA vyAkhyAtaM tatra talliN^gasadbhAvAttasya tadviShayatvaM yuktamiti vA.aha || dehina iti ||
nanvastu tatra tatra jIvaH pratipAdyaH | dehitvAdivisheShaNAnAM jIvAdanyatra niravakAshatvAt | avinAshitvAdInAM tu jIve.api sambhavAt kathaM tadvAkyasyeshvaraviShayatvanishchaya ityata Aha || na hIti || Ishvaro.api tatsambhavaH kathamityata Aha || paramAtmana iti || na cha tatra tatra bhAShyavirodhaH shaMkanIyaH | atra cha mukhyayaiva vR^ittyArthamaN^gIkR^itya paunaruktyAdishaMkonmUlanaM vinA kevalAmukhyArthagrahaNe bAdhakAnAmuktatvAt | bhAShye punarmukhyArthamaparityajyaivArthAntarasyoktatvAditi ||
tathApi naiteShAM vAkyAnAmuktArthatA yuktA | asaN^gatatvAdityato "nAsataH" ityantAnAM saN^gateruktatvAt " avinAshi tu" ityAdInAM saN^gatiM darshayan "avinAshi tu"ityasya shlokasya "nAsataH" ityanena saN^gatiM sAkShAdasambhavAdavatArakrameNAha || yasmAditi || evambhUta iti || sarvaprakAreNAvinAshItyarthaH | asya shlokasyoktaprakAreNa "anAshinaH" iti vakShyamANenApi saN^gatirityAha || atastadarthamiti || athavA "nAsataH" ityetachCheShatvenApi "anAshinaH" ityasya saN^gatirityanenoktam | "antavantaH" ityanenApi saN^gatirityAha || anyeShAmiti || prAkR^itadehinashcha | jIvA iti sheShaH | anena "sharIriNaH" ityanyopayogamAchaShTe | nityatvAdityanena "nityasya" ityasya | ata evAsya "na tvevAham" , "dehino.asmin" ityanena gatArthatA.api parihR^itA bhavati | "nAyaM hanti" ityatra hetutayA prakR^itAnuvAdo.ayamityAshrayaNAt | ata evoktaM "nityasyoktAH" iti || "nAyaM hanti" ityasya "ya enam" ityanena saN^gatimAha || tasmAddhanteti || etena "nAyaM hanti" ityetatpunaruktam | jIvAsvAtantryAderuktasvAt | na cha "ya enam" ityanena saN^gatiM sAkShAdasambhavAdavatArakrameNAha || yasmAditi || evambhUta iti || sarvaprakAreNAvinAshItyarthaH | asya shlokasyoktaprakAreNa "anAshinaH" iti vakShyamANenApi saN^gatirityAha || atantadarthamiti || athavA "nAsataH " ityetachCheShatvenApi "anAshinaH" ityasya saN^gatirityanenoktam | "antavantaH" ityasyoktarItyA "anAshinaH"ityanena saN^gatau sddhAyAM "nAyaM hanti" ityanenApi saN^gatirityAha || anyeShAmiti || prAkR^itadehinashcha | jIvA iti sheShaH | anena "sharIriNaH" ityasyopayogamAchaShTe | nityatvAdityanena "nityasya" ityasya | ata evAsya "na tvevAham", ityatra hetutayA prakR^itAnuvAdo.ayamityAshrayaNAt | ata evoktaM "nityasyoktAH" iti | "nAyaM hanti" ityasya "ya enam"ityanena saN^gatimAha || tasmAddhanteti || etena "nAyaM hanti"ityetatpunaruktam | jIvAsvAtantryAderuktatvAt | na cha "ya enam"  ityetadupapAdanAyaktAnuvAdo.ayaM pramANAnupanyAsenopapAdanAyogAdityetadapi parAkR^itam | " nAyaM hanti"  ityetatprakR^itam " antavantaH" ityapekShya pravR^ittamityuktatvAt | mantravarNasya jIveshvaranityatvopapAdakatvamuktam | " nAyaM hanti" ityetadupapAdakatvenApi saN^gatirityAha || yasmAdayameveti || etena mantravarNasya jIveshvaranityatvamAtropapAdakatve.adhikavisheShaNokteranupayoga ityetadapirahR^itam | jIvavadityanena " purANaH" ityasyopayogaM darshayati | " na hanyate" ityasya pUrvArdhaprakR^itena parameshvarasyaiva svAtantryamityanena saN^gatimabhipretya tadghaTanAya tAtparyamAha || jIvastviti || anenAsya gatArthatA parihR^itA bhavati |
" vedAvinAshinam" itIshvarAvinAshitvAdeH " kathaM sa puruShaH" ityanena sAkShAtsaN^gaterabhAvAdavatArakrameNa tAmAha || ata evamiti || eteneshvarAvinAshitvAdeH prAgevoktatvAtpunaruktirityapi parAntam | " kathaM sa puruShaH" ityetadupapAdakasvatantryopapAdanAyoktAnuvAdo.ayamityAshritatvAt | " vAsAMsi" ityetasya prakR^iteneshvarasvAtantryeNApi saN^gatimAha || vAsasa iti || nainamityasya prakR^iteneshvarasvAtantryeNapi saMgatimAha || Ishvarasyeti || j~nAtavyamiti sambandhaH|
yadvA tathApi nAsya prakaraNasyobhayaviShayatvaM yuktam | ubhayapratipAdanasya prasaN^agAnanuguNatvAt | yuddhavidhAnasyaiva prakR^itatvAdato nobhayapratipAdanaM prasaN^agAnuguNam | yuddhaM kartavyaM, tachcheshvarasyaiva svatantratvena mokShapradAnasamarthatvAttatpUjAtvena kAryamityatrAbhipretam| tatreshvarasya nityatvapratipAdanaM yuddhavidhAnAya shokanivAraNArthamupayujyate | tasya sarvaprakAreNAvinAsharatvAdipratipAdanaM cha tatpUjAvidhAnArthaM tasya mokShadatvasAmarthyasamarthanAya svAtantryopapAdakatayopayujyate | jIvasya nityatvavarNanaM yuddhavidhAnAya shokanivAraNArthamupayujyate | tasya dehanAshAdivarNanamapi shokanivAraNAya parameshvarasyaiva svAtantryasiddhyarthaM jIvasyAsvAtantryapradarshanAyopayujyate-iti bhAvena sarvavAkyAnyabhipretArthe yojayati || yasmAdevambhUta iti || sarvaprakAreNAvinAshItyarthaH | yasmAdevambhUta ityavinAshitvityabhinate prameye yojyam | atantatpUjeti nAsata iti | 
atantadarthamityanAshina iti | anyeShAmityantavanta iti | prAkR^itadehina iti sharIriNa iti | ata iti nAyaM hantIti | nityanvAditi na hanyata iti | tasmAditi ya enamiti | yasmAditi na mriyata iti | tatsaMyogeti nAyaM bhUtveti | jIvastviti na hanyata iti | ata evamiti vedeti | vAsasa iti vAsAMsIti | Ishvasyeti nainamiti | yadyapyetadvyAkhyAnata eva siddhaM, tathApi viprakIrNatayoktaM na mandabuddhAvArohatIti piNDIkR^ityoktam |
atra "nainaM Chindanti " iti vartamAnaprayogaH kAlAntarachChedAdyanuj~nArtha ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || nainamiti || na kAlAntarachChedAdyanuj~nArthaM vartamAnaprayogaH | kintu mama dehe ChedAdikaM nAstIti tatra yuktitayA ChedAdiprApitisadbhAve.apIdAnIM tadabhAvasya pratyakShata eva darshayituM shakyatvasUchanArthameveti bhAvaH | atreshvarasvarUpasyaiva chedAdeyabhAvaH kathyate na tu taddehasyApi | dehasya  "nishatasharairvibhidyamAnatvachi " iti tadbhAvokteH | ataH svadehasyeti kathamuchyata ityato.abhiprAyamAha || chChedeti || mR^iShA pradarshanaM kimarthamityata Aha || Ishvara iti || kuto mR^iShA, paramArthata eva kiM na syAdityato vA.aha || Ishvara iti || svatantrasya paramArthatastadayuktamityarthaH || 24 ||
"avyakto.ayam" itIshvaraviShayamityuktam | tatreshavarasyAvyaktatvAdikathane kA saN^gatirityataH "sarvagatasthANuH"iti paramAtmanaH sarvagatatvamabhihitam | tatreshvarasya deho.asti na vA? Adye dehinaH sarvatra vartamAnasya sarvatra darshanaM syAt | dvitIye sharIrachChedAdinirAso na yukta ityAshaMkAnirAsAyAdyapadamavatArayati || sarveti || dehitve.avyaktatvaM kathaM yujyata ityAshaMkya tatparihAtatvenAchitantyapadaM vyAchaShTe || kathamiti || avintyashakteH prativandhe nAshe vA sati pratItiprasaN^ga ityAshaMkAparihArAyAvikAryapadaM vyAchaShTe || na cheti || nanvekenaiva shabdena pUrteH kimarthaM nainamityatra prati ptatyenamiti vachanam | "avyakto.ayam"ityatra prativisheShaNam "ayam"iti vachanaM cha kimarthamityata Aha || yAnIti || Adipadena naJNo grahaNam | anena prativisheShaNamapi vIpsArUpeNa "enam"ityAdibahushabdayojanAM sUchayati | evaM chejjIvasya bAhulyAbhAvAt "achChedyo.ayam"iti pR^ithagvachanaM vyarthamityata Aha || jIve tviti || jIve kR^ithagvachanamiti sheShaH |
nanvIshvarasya dehavattvaM, tasya cha dehasya ChedAdirAhityamevambhAvashcha sarvarUpANAmityetatkuta ityata uktam "uchyate"iti padaM vyAchaShTe || sarvamiti || kAstAH shrutaya ityata Aha || saditi || ChedAdidoSharahito deho yasyAsau saddehaH | sukhagandhaH | sukhAtmakagandho vA | j~nAnaj~nAna ityAderatishayitaj~nAnAdimAnityarthaH |
nanvIshvarasya dehasadbhAve shrutivipratipattestatsandeha eva syAtkuto nishchayastadbhAvasyetyataH shrutyantareNa tadvyavasthAM darshayati || adeha iti || svarUpavAn svarUpabhUtadehavAn || sukhaj~nAnAdirUpakaH || astIti saMbandhaH | tatashcha dehavAnuchyata ityanuShajyate | dehadehinoraikyamanyatrAdR^iShTaM kathaM yujyata ityata Aha || sa cheti || nanu sukhaj~nAnAdirUpakaH || astIti saMbandhaH | tatashcha deho viShNorananyashchet tadA tasya sukhAdiguNarUpatvaM prasajyate | na cha tadyujyate | "Anandabhuk" ityAdAvAnandabhoktR^itvasyoktatvAt | ekasya cha bhoktR^ibhogyabhAvAdarshanAdityata Aha || guNeti || dR^iShTopyayamabhinne bhoktR^ibhogyabhAvaH kiMnimitta upapadyata ityata Aha || abhinne.apIti || asti | tenAbhinne.api bhoktR^ibhogyabhAva upapadyata iti sheShaH | visheShasadbhAva eva kuta ityata Aha || ayamiti ||
nanvayaM visheSho visheShite.anyo.ananyo vA? Adye bhedaparamparayA.anavasthA | dvitIye visheShavisheShibhAvavyavahArAyodaH | tatrApi visheShAN^gIkAre.anavasthetyata Aha || visheSho.apIti || visheSho visheShito.ananya iti na bhedaparamparayA.anavasthA | na eva visheSho yathA.abhinne.api vastuni bhoktR^ibhogyabhAvanirvAhakaH tathA visheShito bhedarahitasyApi svasya visheShatvaM, visheShiNo visheShitvaM cha nirvahatIti na visheShaparamparayA.apyanavasthetyarthaH | itopyekasyaiva harerbhoktR^ibhogyabhAvo yukta ityAha || parameti || abhinnasyaiva svasya bhoktR^ibhogyabhAve.anupapattiM parihartuM hareraishvaryaM kuta ityata Aha || yukteti || yuktAyuktatvaM vastunoriti sheShaH | tatra Ishvare | tarhIshvare duHkhitvAdyapi kalpyatAmayuktyabhAvAdityata uktam | pramANeti || ekasyaiva bhoktR^ibhogyatvAdikaM pramANAvagatatvAdviruddhamapyaishvaryabalAdaN^gIkAryaM nAnyat | tasyAprAmANikatvAditi bhAvaH |
ekasyaiva bhoktR^ibhogyabhAvAdiguNA eveshvarasya pramANikA na duHkhAdidoShA ityatra shrutyantaraM chAha || guNA iti || kathaM na doShAH shrutAH? "janitota viShNoH"ityAdau pratIterityata Aha || aj~nairiti ||
pirakR^itaguNAnAM bhagavatA.abhede, sarvANyapi rUpANyovaMvidhAnItyatra cha shrutIrAha || ekamiti || ekam ekatvahaN^khyAyogi | evetyavahavAdibhedanirAkaraNam | advitIyaM samAbhyadhikarahitam | kiJNchana nAneti rUpAvayavaguNakarmabhedaH | tarhi bhedAbhedau syAtAmityata Aha || mR^ityoriti || mR^ityoH mR^ityuM tama Apnoti | nAneveti bhedAbhedau bhedadarshane ko.anartha ityata Aha || yatheti || yathA parvateShu durge shikhare vR^iShTamudakam adho vidhAvati evaM guNAdIn bhinnAn pashyan tAn dR^iShTAnanu teShAmeva darshanAntaramadho vidhAvatItyarthaH |
sarvAdvaitaparAH shrutaya etA ityatastAH smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || matsyeti || atyantAbhede vyavahArabhedaH kiMnimitta ityata Aha || abhede.apIti || yadyabhinnaShu guNAdivisheSheShu visheSho varitate tarhi visheShiNAM visheShasya tathAbhedavisheShayoH bhedo.abhedo vA | Adeye.anasthA | dvitIye vyavahAravisheShAyogaH | tatrApi visheShAN^gIkAre.anavasthaivetyata Aha || visheShiNAmiti || visheShiNAM visheShasya tathAbhedavisheShayoH bhedAbhAvAnna bhedaparamparayA.anavasthA | na cha vyavahAravisheShAnupapattiH | yatantatta visheSho.aN^gIkriyate | na chaivaM visheShaparamparayA.anavasthA | ya eva visheSho.abhinneShvapi guNaguNyAdiShu vyavahArabhedanirvAhakaH sa eva visheSho visheShaviSheShyAdivyavahArabhedanirvAhaka ityaN^gIkArAdityarthaH | matstAdInAmabhede.api indrArjunAdivattAratamyamapi nAstItyAha || prAdurbhAveti ||
ke te matsyAdayaH prAdurbhAvA ityata uktameva vivR^iNoti || matsyeti || brahmAdayo.api bhagavadavatAratvenAnyatrochyante | te hi kimatrAdishabdena gR^ihItA utAnavatArA evetyapekShAyAmAha || brahmeti || tarhyati || tarhyavatAratvokteH kA gatirityata Aha || viShNuneti || AveshAvisheShavattayA taduktirityAshayaH | sAkShAdavatArA eva kiM na syurityata Aha || saMsariNa iti || teShveveti || sheShasanatkumArAniruddhashakrayamAshviShu lakShmaNabharatashatrughnabalapradyumnAniruddhanarArjunayudhiShThiranakulasahadevatvena jAteShvatyarthaH | arjunAdichaturShu naikaprakArAvesha ityAha || svalpa iti || avatArANAmanavatAratvenAnavatArANAmavatAratvena j~nAnaM saN^.hkaraj~nAnam || 25 ||
evaM svayaM yuktIruktvA shoko na kArya ityuktam | tatra dehasiddham | tenaiva shoko na kArya ityuchyate "atheti"| tatra muktasyApi jananamaraNasadbhAvaM parAkarvanneva shlokaM vyAchaShTe || tiShThatviti || "atha cha" ityasyArthastiShThatviti | tathApItyanUdya tAvanmAtraj~nAnenApIti vyAkhyAnam.h | nityapadasya niyamavAchitve mAnAbhAvAtkathaM niyameneti vyAkhyetyata Aha || nityamiti || evaM nityapadasyobhayArthatve niyamArthagrahaNe ko heturityata Aha || atra tviti || etachChlokArthavivaraNAtmakottarashloke nityapadasya dhruva iti vivR^itatvAdityarthaH || 26 ||
jananamaraNaniyamo.atra shokanivAraNe hetutayoktaH sphuTaM pratIyate | prAgabhiprete jIvasyAsvAtantrye cha hetutayA.abhimata iti bhAvenA.aha || tanmAditi || tasmAjjananAdiniyamavattvAdeva | atra jIve svAtantryabuddhishcha na kAryetyarthaH || 27 ||
yadi jIve nAshcharyabuddhiH kAryA tarhi kutrAsau kAryA? Isvara ityuktamiti chetsatyam | kiM tato.anyatrApi kvachidityAshaMkya tatparihAratvenoktopasaMhArarUpaM shlokamavatArayati || kiM tarhIti || nanvatrAshcharyo.anya eva, Ishvarastu tatsadR^isha eva, na svayamAshcharya iti pratIteH kathamAshcharyo bhagavAnevetyuchyata ityata Aha || Ashcharyamiti || Ashcharyavadityanena neshvarasyAnAshcharyatvamabhipreyate kintvAshcharyasyaiva sata Ashcharyopamatvamuchyata iti bhAvaH | evamapi bhagavaditarasya svAtantryamaN^gIkAryam | tasyaiva svatantratAyAmAshcharyavadityuktyasambhavAt | svopamAyAH kvApyadarshanAt | tathAcha bhagavAnevetyavadhAraNAyoga ityata Aha || gaganamiti || itivatsvopamAbhidhAnamukhena bhagavaditarasya svAtantryAbhAve tAtparyamatreti bhAvaH | sAgaraM sAgarasamUhaH |
pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAdityataH svoktArthe smR^itisammatimAha || Ashcharya iti || tadgocharamityanena "Ashcharyavat" ityetatkriyAvisheShamityuktaM bhavati | nanu bhagavAnAshcharya eva chettarhi sarveShAmapyAshcharyatvAt "kashchit" iti visheShaNaM vyartham | na hi stambhaH kasyachideva stambha ityata Aha || anAshcharyavaditi || yadyapIshvaraH sarveShAmAshcharya eva | tathApi viparItadarshinAM bahUnAM bhAvAdyathAvaddarshinaH kasyachideva bhAvAdAshcharyatayA darshanaM vivakShya kashyiditi visheShaNaM yuktamiti bhAvaH || 29||
AkShipati || dehIti || jIvo nitya ityuktam | tatra kiM svata eva nityo.atheshvarasAmarthyena? nAdyaH | sarvaM parameshvarAdhInamityabhimatavirodhAt | na dvitIyaH | nityasya svAbhAvikatveneshvarAdhInatvAnupapatteriti bhAvaH | etatparihArAya dehIti shlokaM vyAchaShTe || yasmAditi || dehe rakShakatvena sthitashchet pralayAdau nAshaH syAdityata uktam || sUkShma iti || sUkShmadehapadena liN^gasharIraM chaitanyasharIraM chochyate | nityatvAdeH svAbhAvikatvAtkathamIshvarAdhInatvamityata Aha || dravyamiti || svAbhAvikatve.api nityatvAderIshvarAdhInatvaM yujyate | svAbhAvasyApi bhagavadadhInatayA smR^itisiddhatvAditi bhAvaH | jIvasattAyA bhagavadadhInatve cheyaM smR^itiH pramANam | tathApi jIve sthitvA tadrakShaka Ishvara iti visheShaH kuta ityata Aha || tatrate || tataH tadadhIne | tatastasmAttannintR^itvAt | bhAvAbhAvayorapi nityAnityAbahirbhAvAt || 30 ||
"yadvA jayema" ityuktasya pakShadvaye.apyahAniH parihAra uchyate "hato veti" | tatra "hato vA prApsyasi svargam" ityatreva "jitvA vA bhokShyase mahIm"ityatrApi mahImAtraM na svarga ityanyathApratInirAsAyA.aha || jitveti || "yuddhe mR^ita eva svargaM prApsyasi, jitvA mahImeva bhokShyase" iti pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || ya iti || ye shUrAH yuddheShu pirayudhyanti, ye cha tatra mriyante, ye cha sahasrasaN^khyAtadhanadakShiNAdAtAraH tAnevAyaM preto.api gachChatAditi yamaM pirati pretasya svargaprArthanAjjaye.api svargaprAptiH shrUyate | ato na pratIta evArtha iti bhAvaH || 37 ||
uktamupasaMhR^itya prakaraNAntaramArabhyate "eSheti" | tatra sAN^khyayogashabdau darshanavisheShaparAviti pratItinirAsAya tadarthaM sapramANakamAha || samyagiti || atroktayoH sAN^khyayogayorbuddhya yukta iti prashastatvAditarayorninditatvAnna tAvatroktAviti bhAvaH | ito.api na sAN^khyapadenAtra prasiddhasAN^khyaM vivakShitamityAha || sAN^khyasyeti || atira sAN^khyapadena prasiddhasAN^khyagrahaNe sAN^khyoktamabhihitamityuktaM syAt | na cha tadyuktam | atra "na jAyate"ityAdAvIshvarasyoktatvAt, sAN^khyasya nirIshvaratvAt | atashcha nAtra sAN^khyaM shAstravisheSha ityarthaH | ito.api nAtra sAN^khyayogashabdau prasiddhashAstraparAvityAha || sAN^khyairiti || atra pUrvottaraprakaraNayoH | sAN^khyAdibhiH pAratrikAnarthahetutvameva hiMsAyA aN^gIkriyate | na tvaihike | atira punA rAjyArthameva hiMsA vidhIyate | ato na virodha ityata Aha || mokSheti || sAN^khyayogashabdayoH sopapattikamarthAntaraM chAha || parameti || pUrvottaraprakaraNoktArthapratipAdakatvAdityarthaH | na virodho.atra taduktagrahaNa iti sheShaH || 39 ||
yogaH stUyate neheti | tatra yogAtikrame nAshaH pratyavAyashcha nAstItyanyathApratItinirAsAya pUrvArdhe smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || prArambheti || tameva viShNudharmaM smR^ityA darshayati || svochiteneti || pravR^ittirhitakaraNamapravR^ittirniShiddhaparityAgashchAnyaviShaye nAnuShThIyata ityarthaH | tasmin dharme.adhikArikAlapramANAnyAha || enamiti || tameva vivR^iNoti || taditi || kArtayugatve tretAdiShu na phalaprado.anadhyAyAdhItavedavadityata Aha || treteti || kArtayugatvoktistatra prAchuryeNa sambhavAbhiprAyeNeti bhAvaH | kimasya phalaM yat.htretAdiShvadhikaM syAdityata Aha || evamiti || kathaM sa eva muchyate? traividyasAyapi mokShasadbhAvAdityataH traividyadharmasvarUpamuktvA tadvato mokShAbhAvamAha || traividya iti || traividyasyApi bhagavajj~nAnAdisadbhAvAttasyaiva mokShahetutvAtkathamasau svargaM bhuktvA nivartata ityata Aha || samyagiti || kiM tasya kadApi na mokSha ityataH svargagamanAvadhikathanenaivArthataH siddhamarthaM sphuTamAha || krameNeti || ante samarpayan traividyo yadi niyamAt pratyekaM sarvANi samarpayatItyarthaH | trayyuktakarmakaraNamAtreNa traividyo bhavetkiM bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnAdinetyata Aha || paramiti || vedavAditvasya bhAgavatatraividyayorapi sAmyAdasyaiva kimuchyata ityato na vedAnusAritvaM vedavAditvamatrAbhipretamiti bhAvenAha || vAda iti || vivAdAtpaThanAditi || vivAdapUrvakapaThanAdityarthaH | astvevaM vedavAditvaM tathApi tena mokShAdisiddheH kathaM bhAgavatasyaiva mokSha ukta ityataH pAShaNDAdivattasya niShiddhatvAnna mokShasAdhanatvamiti bhAvenAha || vedeti || na kevalaM mokShanAdhanatvAbhAvo.api tu tamaHsAdhanatvaM chAstItyAha || tebhya iti || "anArambhamanantaM cha" iti tamasi duHkhAnubhavAnuvR^itterAdyantashUnyatvamuchyate | "yasmAnnaivotthitiH" iti tatpraptAnAmapunarAvR^ittiruchyate | tamasaH punarAvR^ittirAhityaM kuta ityata Aha || vavramiti || svagatAnAM gamanaM vArayatIti vA, sadA vR^iNotIti vA varamAnandaM vArayatIti vA vavram | "ityAdivedamaditam || 40 ||
evaMvidhashchedayaM vaiShNavo dharmaH tarhi kimiti kaishchidevaikamatyenAnuShThIyate, parasparaviruddhatayA bahubhirnAnuShThIyata ityata Aha || buddhiriti || keShAJNchideva buddhernirNItatvAttAvanta evaikamatyena viShNuparAyaNAH | bahUnAmanirNItabuddhitvAtparasparavirodhena na viShNuparatvamiti bhAvaH | anena vyavasAyeti shlokopi vyAkhyAto bhavati || 41 ||
yadyavyavasAyAtmakabuddhitvameva vaiShNavadharmarAhitye nimittaM tarhyavyavasAyabuddhistyAjyA syAt | tyagashcha kAraNaparityagena syAt | kena kAraNenAvyavasAyabuddhirbhavatIti pR^ichChati || avyavasAyeti || tatparihArAya "yAm"iti shlokAn yojayati || yAmiti || samAdhAna iti nishchayasya tattvaviShayatayA dArDhyamuchyate | samAdhAnAbhAve cha na viShNudharmAnuShThAnamiti vAkyasheShaH |
smR^ityaiva shlokAn vyAchaShTe || yatheti || tathA tathAviShayIkAri | tatsAmyAditi || vastadusAmyAdityarthaH | asatAM vAkyaM kuto vaiShamyaheturityata Aha || svargeti || yadyasmAt | nAnyadastItyasyArthadvayamAha || na manyanta iti || anugatiH prAptiH | kriyAbAhulyasantatAm etatpratipAdakAm | janmetyasyArtho bahviti | anta ityabhiprAyamAtram | nAnyadastItyAdyarthe shrutiM yAha || iShTeti || anyachChreyo bhagavajj~nAnAdi | sukR^ite sukR^itaprApye | anubhUtvA | bhogAniti sheShaH | vedavAdaratatvamuktArthatayA niShiddhamityatra pramANAntaraM chAha || vedeti || iShTApUrtaM variShThaM manyamAnAH kechana svargabhogAnantaramimaM lokaM vishanti | kechana hInataraM vishantItyuktam | tatsmR^ityA vivR^iNoti || ya iti || saMshayAt saMshayena | viShayIkurvantIti sheShaH | shraddhAdisadbhAvave kathaM tattvaj~nAnAbhAvaH? "shraddhAvAn labhate j~nAnam" ityAderityata Aha || nirNetR^iNAmiti || tattvaj~nAnarahitashraddhAdikamevaitatphalapradaM chettarhi kiyAn visheShastattvaj~nAninAM bhavadityata Aha || yairiti || Adhikye chiraM neti || brahmahatyAderapyadhikapApAcharaNe.apyalpakAlaM yAtanAM yAnti || na tu chiramityarthaH | yaj~nAdimAtreNa bhagavad.hdveShiNAmapi svargasiddheH kiM jij~nAsAdinetyata Aha || tadanyeShAmiti || viparItanishchayAnAmashvamedhAdibhirapi na svargaM ityarthaH | duryodhanAdInAM dveShiNAmeva svargAdidarshanAt kathametadityata Aha || ye tviti || tathApi dveShiNAM svargaprAptisadbhAvAt kathaM tadanyeShAM viparyaya ityuktamityata Aha || tadanya iti || bhAgavatAchAryavarjitad.hdveShyabhiprAyeNa taduktamiti bhAvaH | anena "imaM lokam" ityaj~naviShayam | pramUDhatvamaj~natvameva | hInataramiti tvavaiShNavAchAryavadbhagavaddveShiviShayam | teShAM pramUDhatvaM mithyAj~nAnitvamityuktaM bhavati || 42-44 
||
pratij~nAto j~nAnopAya uchyate || "traiguNyeti" || tatra vedAnAM traiguNyaviShayatvAt tAn parityajya nistraiguNyo bhavetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || traiguNyeti || yApayantItyasya prApayantItyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || apagamayantIti || pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAdityataH svoktArthe smR^itisammatimAha || Ashrityeti || sattvasthatvaM sAttvikatvaM, AtmavattvaM manasvitvamityanyathApratItinirAsAya tattvAtmashabdArthe smR^ityaivA.aha || sattvamiti || santatiH samyagvyAptiH | sattvaM viShNushchet tatsthatvaM svabhAvikaM kiM vidhiyata ityata Aha || santateti || na tadAdhAratayA.avasthAnamAtramatra vivakShitamiti bhAvaH | AtmA viShNushchettadvattvaM svabhAvikaM na vidheyamityata Aha || paramAtmeti || na tu tatsambandhamAtramiti bhAvaH | sattvasthapadenaivAsyArthataH prAptatvAtkiM punaruchyata ityata Aha || teneti || satataM viShNusmaraNamAtravidhAvaikyenApi tatsmaraNaM prApyate | ata Atmavattvakathanena tannivArya yathAvatsmaraNaprakAra uchyata iti bhAvaH | aprAptaprAptiryogaH | prAptaparirakShaNaM kShemaH | tadubhayaM sarvathA tyAjyamityanyathApratItinirAsAyA.aha || viruddheti || na kevalaM shAstraviruddhaviShayayogakShemaparityAgamAtramatra vivakShitam | api tu tadichChAtyAgo.apIti bhAvenechChetyuktam | pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyetheti || utthAnAdInAmapyaprAptaprAptirUpatvena yogatvAt | tatashcha "yogamAtiShThottiShTha" ityAdivirodha iti bhAvaH || 45 ||
traiguNyanivR^ittyarthaH vedAshrayaNaM kAryamityatra yuktiruchyate "yAvAniti" | tatrodapAnashabdaM, sarvataH saMplutodakashabdaM cha smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || udrekAditi || sarvakAryANAM pralaye lInatvAt kathaM sarvataH saMplutodakashabdArthatayA pralayo gR^ihyata ityata Aha || prakR^itiriti ||
samastashlokaM smR^ityA vyAchaShTe || yAvaditi || sAdhakasya sambhavatIti sheShaH | vedaj~nAnena kuto viShNuH phalaM dadAtItyata Aha || vedeti || astu vedArthaj~nAnaM nAma viShNuj~nAnam | tathApi kuto bhAgavAn phalaM dadAtItyata Aha || j~nAnAditi ||
vAkyadvayasiddhaM shlokArthamekIkR^itya darshayati || sarvata iti || nanvatra kashchidudriktatvAdiguNaH shrUyate | sa viShNuriti kutaH? anyopi kiM na syAdityata Aha || sarve hIti || muktAnAM ramAyAshchodriktatvAt kathamudriktatvena viShNutvanishchaya ityata Aha || ye cheti || muktAnAmudriktatve.api pAlakavarjitatvAbhAvenodapAnatvAsambhava iti bhAvaH | muktAnAmudapAnatvAsambhave hetvantaraM chAha || na cheti || ramAyAH sarvAbhimInitvena kAlAdicheShTakatvAdasaN^grahaH | kiJNchodriktatvaM teShAmaN^gIkR^itameva na tu mukhyatostyato na teShAmudapAnatvamityAha || na cheti || anena ramAyA api cheShTakatvamanumatameveti j~nAyate | udriktatvAderanyatrAsambhave.api kimityata Aha || ata iti || kiJNchodriktatvAdyevAnyatra na sambhavati | kimuta sarvataH samplutodake | ato.apyudapAno viShNurevetyAha || pralaya iti ||
mAstvanyeShAmasambhavAt sarvataH samplutodake.apyudapAnatvam | viShNorapi tatsambhavaH kuta iti chetparisheShAditi brUmaH | shrutibhyashchetyAha || AnIditi || tadekaM brahma vAyupreraNAM vinA svasAmarthyenaiva kAlAdikaM prerayati sma | tasmAdanyaduttamaM vastu kiJNchana nA.asa | api tu tadevodriktamAsa | aparaM tamaH prakR^itirasmin sarvasmin deshe.avij~nAtaM salilaM bhUtvA.asIt | tena salilena pralaye sarvaM gUDhamAsIdityarthaH | asyAgre salile samantAtpAlakavarjito bhagavAnAsIdityarthaH | advaitaH sarvodriktaH || 46 ||
aikyabhAvanaM na kAryamityatra heturuchyate "karmaNIti" | tatrArjunasya karmakaraNe kiJNchitsAmarthyamasti, na tu phalApAdana ityevochyate | tatkathamanena sarvajIvAnAmIshvarAbhedAbhAvaH sAdhyata ityata ityata Aha || karmeti || nAtra ta ityurjuna eva gR^ihyate | api tu sarvajIvAH | teShAM phalApAdanAsAmarthyamuktvA Ishvare tatsAmarthyamabhipreyate | tenAtroktaivAbhedAbhAve yuktiriti bhAvaH | nanvatrAstvetAvadabhipretam | tathApi pratij~nAyA abhAvAdabhedAbhAve yuktiriyamukteti kathaM j~nAyata ityata Aha || mA karmeti || phalaheturIshvaraH sa mA bhUrmanasetyarthaH | atra shrutiM chAha || eSha iti || svayaM jIvaH || 47 ||
karmAkaraNe sneho mA.astvityuktam | kiM tarhItyata uchyate "yogasthaH" iti | tatra karmasaN^gaM tyaktvA karmANi kurviti vyAhatamityata Aha || saN^gamiti || na saN^gapadena karmasambandho.abhidhIyate | yena vyAhatiH | api tu phalasneha eveti bhAvaH || 48 ||
j~nAnAtkarmAdhamamityuktam | tarhi j~nAnasyottamatvAt j~nAnAvAsthAyAmIshvaraikyabhAvanaM yuktamityAshaMkAparihArAyochyate buddhAviti | tatraitachChaMkAparihAraH kathamukta ityata Aha || buddhAviti || asminnevArthe smR^itisammatiM darshayaMstayaivottarapAdamapi vyAchaShTe || aj~nAnAmiti || phalahetupadavyAkhyAnaM "taM ye svaikyena" ityAdi pUrvavat | kR^ipaNAH kR^ipAviShayAH | tatra hetumAha || tamasIti || 49 ||
nanvastu j~nAnasyAdhikyaM, tatashcha kimityataH "tasmAt"iti j~nAnasAdhanamApAdyamityuktam | tatrAstu j~nAnasAdhanApAdanam | kiM phalasneharahitakarmaNetyAshaMkAyAM phalasneharahitakarmaiva j~nAnasAdhanamiti vaktavyam | kimarthamatra karmakaushalasya j~nanasAdhanatvamuchyata ityataH phalasneharAhityAdiyuktakarmaiva karmakaushalapadenochyata iti bhAvenAha || yathAvaditi || "yogasthaH" ityatra 
bhagavajj~nAnasyAparigR^ihItatvAdatrApi na tadabhipretamityata Aha || bhagavaditi || etachChlokArthavivaraNAtmakottarashloke "buddhiyuktaH"iti bhagavajj~nAnasyAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanatvena gR^ihItatvAdatra pUrvatrApi tadabhimatamiti bhAvaH || 50 || 51 ||
kiyatparyantamavashyaM kartavyAni mumukShuNaivaM karmANItyata uchyate yadeti | tatra nirvedapadena vairAgyamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || nirvedamiti || etachChlokadvayaM smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || buddhIti || shrotavyashrutapadaM sarvakarmopalakShakam | samAdhAnena shrutyarthaj~nAnanishchalatvenAparokShaj~nAnaM bhavati | anena "namAdhAvachalA" iti samAdhau satyaparokShaj~nAnaM tena viShNAvachaleti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tadyogaM bhagavadyogam  | bhagavadyogasya sarveShAmapi vidyamAnatvAt ko visheSha ityuktaM vivR^iNoti || mukti iti || tadashrnute brahmApnotItyarthaH | atrApi yadA tadeti sambadhyate | nanvatra "shrutiviprapatipannA" iti shrutiviruddhatvamuchyate | tatkathaM shrutimArgaM prapanneti vyAkhyotyata Aha || shrutAviti || 52 || 53 ||
prakR^itaj~nAnilakShaNAdiprashnaH kriyate sthiteti || tatra "kA bhAShA" ityetadanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || keti || nanu j~nAnIti bhAShyata iti siddhatvAtkiM prashnenetyata Aha || kairiti || "samAdhisthasya"ityasya samAdhiM kurvato j~nAnino lakShaNAdi pR^ichChatItyanyathApratItinirAsArthamAha || samAdhIti || 54 ||
j~nAnilakShaNamuchyate prajahAtIti || tatra j~nAninaH sarvakAmaprahANaM nAma niShiddhAniShiddhasarvakAmaprahANamityanyathApratItinirAsAya tatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || sarveti || kuto na j~nAninaH sarvakAmanivR^ittiH, yataH sarvashabdasaN^.hkochaR^i kriyata ityata Aha || aparokShati || j~nAninaH kadAchinniShiddhamamanivR^ittirapi nAsti | kutaH sarvakAmanivR^ittirityarthaH | tarhi j~nAnasyAbhibhavakAle j~nAnilakShaNAbhAvAjj~nAnitvAbhAvaH prasajyata ityataH satyamityAha || ata iti || niShiddhakAmarAhityasya j~nAnAnabhibhavakAla eva sattvAdityarthaH | nanu yadi kadAyid dR^ishirabhibhUyate tarhi sA na mokShasAdhanaM syAt | kAdAchitkatayA daurbalyAdityata Aha || tathApIti || yogyA svabimbaviShayA | "AtmanyevAtmanA"ityAtmashabdau jIvamanaHparAvityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || AtmanIti || kuto na jIvAdiparovityata Aha || tuShTa iti || atrAtmasthityAdinA tuShTyabhidhAnAjjIvasthityAdinA tadasambhavAnna tatparAvAtmashabdAviti bhAvaH || 55 ||
etAdR^ishaM chejj~nAnaM tatkiM sarve na sAdhayantItyato nirAhAratvenendriyajayastenaiva j~nAnamityatiduHsaMpAdatvaM j~nAnasyochyate "viShayA" iti | tatra rasashabdasyApUrvamarthamAha || rasa iti || 59 ||
vItarAgetyAdinA rAgAdirAhityaM j~nAnilakShaNamuktam | jij~nAsunA cha tatsAdhyam | kAraNaphalaparij~nAne cha rAgAdityAgo bhavati | ato rAgAdiparihArAya tatkAraNaphale uchyeti "dhyAyata" iti | tatra saMmohasmR^itivibhramapadAbhyAM viparItaj~nAnamevochyate | ataH kathaM hetuhetumadbhAva ityata Aha || saMmohAditi || atra saMmohapadena paravittApaharaNAdyadharme dharmabuddhirityAdimithyAj~nAnamuchyate | smR^itivibhramapadena cha paravittApaharaNAderadharmatvAbhidhAyakashrutyAdyarthasya pUrvaM svayaM j~nAtasyApyanyathAsmaraNamuchyate | tayoshcha hetuhetumadbhAvassambhavatIti bhAvaH | smR^itibhraMshAdbuddhinAsha iti durghaTam | chetanasya buddhyavinAbhAvitvena buddhernAshAyogAdityata uktaM vivR^ishvannAha || vAkyeti || nirNItaM kevalavAkyasApekShatAM vinApi nishchitam | na tu j~nAnamAtramiti bhAvaH || 63 ||
indriyajaye jAte manasaH svato.api prAyo viShayAgatilakShaNena prasAdena mokShalAbhAdasAvApAdya ityuktam | tadanApAdane doShashchochyate nAstIti | tatra bhAvanAyAH shAntisAdhyatvAt "na chAbhAvayataH shAntiH " iti kathamuchyata ityato na shAntipadenatra chittanirodha uchyate | api tu bhagavanniShThabuddhitvam | tachcha bhAvanAsAdhyaM bhavatIti bhAvena shAntishabdArthaM sapramANakamAha || shAntiriti || 66 ||
piNDIkR^ityoktalakShamuchyate yA nisheti | tatra sarvaprerakANAM devAnAmapi j~nAnitvAjj~nAninAM paramAtmetarAdarshane lokayAtrochChedaH syAdityatastadvAkyaM devetaraj~nAniviShayatayA smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || devebhya iti ||  "yathA.anyaiH " ityanena pUrvArdhatAtparyamuktaM bhavati | yathAj~nairbR^ihma na j~nAyata ityarthaH || sUryavaditi || sUryo yathA svatejasA sarvaM prakAshayatyevaM svaj~nAnena sarvaM viShayIkurvantItyarthaH || 69 ||
evaM j~nAnI sarvatrodAsInashchetkathaM viShayabho,stasyetyata uchyate ApUryamANamiti | tatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || bhuJNjAna iti || dharmamayIM dharmAkhyAm | viShayabhoktA na kAmI kathamuchyata ityata uktasya  "na kAmakAmI " ityasyArtho nAsAviti | nanu kAmAbhAve viShayabhogAsambhavAt kathaM j~nAninaH kAmAbhAvo mokShasiddhyarthamuchyata ityato.atra kAmapadena niShiddhechChaivAbhipretA | tasyA eva mokShavirodhitvAt | nechChAmAtraM tasya mokShAvirodhitvAdityAha || keti || kutsiteyamiti mAnaM yadviShaye saivechChA kAma ityarthaH | itashcha  "na kAmakAmI " ityatra nechChAmAtraniShedha ityAha || na cheti || nanu shAntishabdasya bhagavanniShThAvAchitvAt kathaM sa muchyata iti vyAkhyetyato bhagavanniShThAsambandhAdeva mokSho.api shAntishabdAbhidheya iti smR^ityaivAha || shAntiriti || 70 ||
pUrvashlokoktaM prapaJNchyate vihAyeti | tatra kAmapadena yadIchChA gR^ihyate tarhi niHspR^iha iti puraruktiH | yadi viShayAntarhi viShayatyAge 
kiM bhakShayati | niHspR^ihatvaM cha kathaM yujyate | sarvakAmanivR^ittiriti vachanavirodhAt | jIvanAdyabhAvaprasaN^gAchchetyata Aha || niShiddheti || sarvakAmapadena viShayANAM grahaNAnna puraruktidoShaH | nApi charaNAsambhavaH | atra niHspR^iha ityanena viShayANAM svarUpato hAnamantareNa spR^ihAbhAvamAtreNa hAnasyAbhipretatvAt | nApi smR^itivachanAdivirodhaH | niHspR^iha iti niShiddhaviShayaspR^ihAbhAvasya vivakShitatvAditi bhAvaH || nanu j~nAninAmapyahaM mameti pratyayaprayogadarshanAt kathaM tasyochyate nirahaN^.hkAratvAdItyato nAhamityAdij~nAnAdimAtramahaN^.hkArAdIti bhAvena smR^ityaivAhaN^.hkArAdishabdarthAmAha || asvarUpa iti || mamatA madadhInamiti bhAvanA || 71 ||
uktalakShaNamupasaMhriyate eSheti | tatra brAhmIti brahmadharmabhUteti pratItinirAsAyAha || brAhmIti || nanu  "kShIyante chAsya karmANi tasmin dR^iShTe parAvare " ityAderj~nAnamAtreNa sarvakarmaNAM kShayAjj~nAnAnantarameva mokShasadbhAvena  "sthitvA.asyAm " ityantakAle bhagavatsmR^ityAdividhAnaM brahmaprAptyarthaM kimiti kriyata ityata Aha || j~nAninAmiti || j~nAninAmapi yadyantakAle bhagavatsmaraNAdi nAsti tarhi janmAntarameva bhavati | na brahmaprAptiratastadarthamantakAle tatsmaraNAdividhAnaM yuktameva | na cha j~nAninaH kShINakarmatvAjjanmAntarAyogaH | j~nAnamAtreNAprArabdhakarmanAshe.api yeShAmantakAle.api na bhagavatsmaraNaM teShAM prArabdhakarmabhAvAditi bhAvaH |
yadi mokSharthaM sAkShAdantakAla eva bhagavatmR^ityAdyapekShitaM tarhi tasya duHsampAdatvena kasyApi mokSho na syAt | ataH sAkShAdantakAlasmaraNaM sAtra bhagavato.abhipretamityata Aha || prArabdheti || na mokSharthamantakAlasmaraNApekShAyAM kasyApi mokShaprasaN^gaH | prArabdhakarmaNa evAntakAlasmaraNapratibandhakatvena tannAshe.antakAle smaraNaniyamAt | tadbhAve cha mokShaniyamAditi bhAvaH | nanvantakAlasmaraNAdeva mokSho nAnyatheti bhagavadabhimatamiti nishchayo yadi bhavettadaivamarthakalpanA bhavet | na eva kuta ityata Aha || yaM yamiti ||  "shAntirmokSho.atha nirvANam " ityAdernirvANashabdasya mokShe.api prasiddherbrahma nirvANamiti kathaM sAmAsAdhikaraNam | na cha brahma nirvANaM cheti yojanA | brahmaprAptyatiriktamokShAnirUpaNAdityata Aha || bANamiti || bANashabdasya sharIravAchitvAnnirvANapadena kAryabrahmavyAvR^ittyarthaM brahmaNo.asharIratvamevochyate | na mokSha iti bhAvaH | nanu kathamasharIratvaM brahmaNaH | sahasrashIrShetyAdivirodhAdityAshaN^.hkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || abhAvAditi || 72 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM dvitIyo.adhyAyaH || 2 ||
 
pUrvAdhyAyasaN^gatatvenaitadadhyArthaM harshayituM pUrvAdhyAyapratipAdyamAha || j~nAnamiti ||  "eShA te.abhihitA " ityantena j~nAyata iti j~nAnamIshvarAdisvarUpaM nirUpitam | tato.adhyAyaparisamAptiparyantaM tatsvarUpaj~nAnopayashchoktaH pUrvAdhyAya ityarthaH tatsaN^gatatvenaitadadhyAyArthamAha || tatreti || tayorj~nAnayogayormadhye yogo.api dvividho bhavati | karmadhyAnayogabhedAt | tatra prAguktameva karmayogaM prapaJNachayatyanenAdhyAyena bhagavAnityarthaH | nanu  "karmajaM buddhiyuktA hi phalaM tyaktvA " ityAdinA pUrvatrApi karmayogasya prapaJNchitatvAt kimannAdhyAyenetyata uktam || visheShata iti || nanvatrApi  "indriyANi parANi " ityAdinA j~nAnasyApyukteH kathaM karmayogaM prapaJNchayatItyuchyata ityato vA.aha || visheShata iti || prAchuryeNetyarthaH |
nanu karmaNaH sakAshAdbuddherjyAyastvaM prAk kutroktam? yadbIjo.ayaM  "jyAyasI chetkarmaNaH " ityarjunaprashna ityata Aha || dUreNeti || 1-2 ||
 "loke.asmin " iti parihAravAkye keShAJNchidadhikAriNAM j~nAnameva keShAJNchit karmaivAnuShTheyamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || j~nAneti || nAtra j~nAnayogapadena j~nAnamAtraM vivakShitaM, karmayogapadena cha karmamAtramuchyate | kintu pratyekamubhayam | rhyubhAvapi j~nAnakarmayogAviti baktavyau | kathaM kashchijj~nAnayogaH kashchitkarmayoga uchyata iti chenna | ekaikatra j~nAnakarmaNoH prachuryAbhiprAyeNAlpajalamishre.apikShIre kShIrashabdaprayogavat prayogopapatteriti bhAvaH |
sAN^khyAnAM j~nAnameva yoginAM karmaiveti pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAditi chettathA.aN^gIkAre smR^itivirodhaH syAditi bhAvenAha || sAN^khyAiti || devAnAM bahukarmasadbhAvAtkathaM mukhyahAN^khyatvamityata Aha || bahviti || tato.api karmaNo.api | gR^ihasthAdInAmapi kiM kevalakarmaivetyapekShAyAmAha || j~nAnino.apIti || tarhi kathaM karmayogina ityata Aha || atIti || sAN^khyAnAM kevalaM j~nAnameva yoginAM kevalaM karmaiveti tiM na syAdityata Aha || nobhayamiti || sAN^khyAnAM j~nAnena yoginAM karmaNApuruShArtho bhavatIti shrutyAdau shrUyate | na chaikaikena puruShArtho yujyate | ato naikaikagrahaNaM yuktamiti bhAvaH | karmAbhAve kuto na puruShArtha iti chetkiM karmapadena karmamAtraM vivakShyate atha yaj~nAdikarma vA | AdyaM dUShayati || na hIti || dvitIyaM dUShayati || na cheti || j~nAnamAtraM karma vinA saMsAranivR^ittisAdhanamapi na sampUrNapuruShArthakaramiti bhAvaH | tarhyastu kevalaM karmaiva puruShArthakaramityata Aha || na cheti 
||  "na karmaNA na prajayA " ityAdishrutivirodhAditi bhAvaH | anena  "na karmaNAmanArambhAt " ityAdeshcha tAtparyamuktaM bhavati | bhavedatra j~nAnakarmaNoH samuchchayakalpanaM, yadyatra sAN^khyayogAdeH puruShArthahetutvamuchyeta | ekaikasya puruShArthasAdhanatvAbhAvokteH na cha tadatrochyata ityata Aha || niShTheti || ShThA gatinivR^ittAvityato niShThA paryavasitiH | gateriti sheShaH | kathamanena chodyaparihAra ityata Aha || muktiriti || atra niShThApadena gatiparyavasitivAchinA saMsAragatiparyavasAnaM muktirabhipretetyarthaH | nanvevaM j~nAnakarmabhyAM mokSha ityaN^gIkAre  "na karmaNA na prajayA dhanena tyAgenaike amR^itatvamAnashuH " ityAdishrutivirodhaH syAdityata Aha || j~nAnina iti || j~nAnakarmabhyAM mokShasiddhyaN^gIkAre.api naitachChrutivirodhaH | karmarahitaj~nAnamAtrasya mokShasAdhanatvAbhidhAnAt | asmAbhirapi tadaN^gIkArAt | karmaNastu j~nAnamAtreNaiva siddhe mokShe sukhAdhikyahetutvenAN^gIkArAt | j~nAnAdeva mokShaH karmaNA AnandavR^iddhirityetat kuta it chet j~nAnina iti shrutereveti bhAvaH |
itashcha  "j~nAnayogena " ityatra karmApi saMyojyam | na j~nAnamAtramityAha || anyatheti || anyathA j~nAnamAtreNaiva puruShArthAN^gIkAre | karmayoginAmapi prakR^itatvAtteShAM karmAnArambhe puruShArthAsambhavAbhidhAyakametadvAkyaM kiM na syAdityata uktam || ubhayeti || na kevalametatkarmayogiviShayamapi tUbhayaviShayamityarthaH kut.asyobhayaviShayatvaM j~nAyata ityata Aha || samatvaM cheti || mokShe karmaNA AnandavR^iddhirbhavatItyayuktam |  "nAnyaH panthA " iti shrutau karmaNo mokShasambandhasyaiva nirAkaraNAdityata Aha || nAnya iti || j~nAnAyogameveyaM shrutirvyavachChinatti | na tu karmasambandhaM nirAkaroti | tathAtve  "j~nAnino mokShaniyamaH " iti shrutivirodhAditi bhAvaH || 3 || 4 ||
kAryata ityatra svatantrakarturanyasyApratIteH prakR^itiguNAnAmeva svatantrakartutvamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || kartR^itvamiti || atra guNAnAM vikArakartR^itvamevochyate | na tu svatantrakartR^itvam | avasha iti viShNoH svatantrakartR^itvokteH | avashapadena svAnadhInatvaM gR^itItvA guNAnAM svatantrakartR^itvameva kiM na gR^ihyata iti chenna |  "kartR^itvam " iti shrutivirodhAditi bhAvaH | shrutiriti kutrachitpAThaH | tatrAnyathApratItinirAsAya shrutyaiva vyAkhyAtaM viShNoH svatantrakartR^itvamatra na pratIyata ityata uktam || avasha iti || avashapadaM kathaM viShNuvashatvaM vaktItyata Aha || aH iti || 5-8 ||

uktArthasaN^gatatvena etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || uktayoriti || j~nAnakarmaNormadhye.anyatarasyeti pratItinirAsAya ubhayorityuktam | karmaNo.atItAdhyAye vivR^itatvAt kimanenetyato visheShetyuktam | uktakarmayoge ruchijananAya pUrvAnuShThito.ayaM dharma ityuchyate  " imamiti " tattAtparyaM smR^ityaivAha || brahmeti || gItA paJNcharAtrasaN^kShepashchettarhi tasyAH sarvottamashAstratvahAnirityataH shabdata eva saMkShepo sArthata ityAha || yatheti || sarvapaJNcharAtrArthatve gItAyAH paJNcharAtrAdadhamatvamAtraM mAstu | tAvatA sarvashAstrottamatvaM kathamityata Aha || vedeti || sarvashAstrebhyo.atishayena vedArthapUrakapaJNcharAtrAsheShArthatvena gItAyAH sarvashAstrottamatvaM yuktamiti bhAvaH || 1 || 3 ||
idAnIntanatvAdbhagavato vivasvataH prAchInatvAt kathaM tadupadeShTratvamiti pR^ichChati  " aparamiti " | tatrArjunasya bhagavadaj~nAnitvapratIteH prAguktAnupapattirityata Aha || jAnanto.apIti || naivaM prashnenArjuno bhagavantamanAdinityaM na jAnAtIti kalpyam | jAnanto.apIti vachanAt prashnasya visheShaj~nAnAdyarthatvopapatteriti bhAvaH | sthApanAya j~nAtasya dR^iDhIkaraNAya || 4 || 5 ||
janmAnyatItAni chettarhi na jananamaraNarAhityaM bhavataH | tathAcha  " avinAshi tu  " ityuktavirodha ityata uchyate  " ajo.api " iti | tatra  " AtmamAyayA " ityetadaj~nAnavashAdityanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || Atmeti || nAtrAtmamAyayetyaj~nAnavashAdityuchyate | sarvamAnavirodhAt | api tu avatAre parapreraNAnivAraNAya mahAmAyetyAdinA mAyApadoditasvechChAnibandhanatvamevochyata ityarthaH |  " prakR^itiM svAmadhiShThAya " ityetat prAkR^itasharIralAbhenetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAnudya prakR^itipadaM vyAchaShTe || prakR^itimiti || nAtra prAkR^itasharIralAbho.abhidhIyate | shrutyAdivirodhasyoktatvAt | kintu  " avatarasi chet prayojanena bhAvyam | tathAcha nAnavAptamityuktavirodhaH " ityAshaMkAparihArAya prayojanAbhAve.apyavatArAdikaM tAdR^ishasvabhAvatvAdyujyata ityevochyata iti bhAvaH | bhavedayamartho yadi hareravatArAdi prayojanaM vinA svabhAvAdeveti siddhaM syAttadeva kuta ityata Aha || devasyeti || sa svabhAvashcha ayaM deva eva na tu tato bhinna ityarthaH |
astu viShNoH svabhAvAdeva vyApAraH | tathApyatra prakR^itipadaM kutaH svabhAvavAchItyata Aha || ata eveti || yato.atra prakR^itipadaM sAvabhAvavAchyata eva svAmiti visheShaNaM prayuktam | kevalamanyArthatve svAdhInatvasya mametyasAdhAraNashabdenAbhidhAnaM vinobhayasAdhAraNametanna syAdityarthaH | etameva nyAyamasyatrApyatidishati || prakR^itimiti || ityAdiShu cha svashabdena visheShaNamata evetyarthaH | yadi prakR^itipadaM svabhAvavAchi tarhi  " mayA.adhyakSheNa prakR^itiH " ,  " prakR^itiM viddhi " ityatrApi kiM svabhAvavAchItyapekShAyAmAha || mayeti || ataH svabhAvAdanyaiva tatra prakR^itiriti sheShaH | anyatve hetvantaraM chAha || prakR^itimiti 
|| atrA.adipadena  " mayA " ityasya saN^grahaH |  " mayA.adhyakSheNa " ityatrAdhInatyA sambandhitvapratIteH " prakR^itiM " ityatra " me " iti ShThyA sambandhitvapratIteshcheti yojyam | sambandhitvena pratIteranyA chedatrApi svAmiti sambandhitvena pratIteranyA syAdityata Aha || atreti || bhavedidaM yadi svashabdaH sambandhasavAchyeva syAt | na chaivam | atra svashabdasya mukhyataH svarUpavAchitvAditi | bAdhakAbhAvat svarUpavAchyeva na tu sambandhavAchIti bhAvaH | svashabdasya svarUpavAchitvaM kutra dR^iShTamityataH svabhAvapadagatasvashabdasya tadR^iShTamiti bhAvenAha || svabhAva iti || svabhAvapadagatasvashabdasya sveti shabdasyAnyatvamAtrApAdane nAniShTam | arthadvayAN^gIkArAt | anyaivetyApAdanamayuktam | svashabdasya svarUpavAchitvasyApi bhAvena  " me " itivaditarAvyAvartakatvAditi bhAvaH | svabhAvapadagatasvashabdasya svarUpavAchitve tenaiva pUrteH bhAvashabdo vyartha ityata Aha || bhAveti || yadi svashabdamAtraM prayujye tadA svashabdasya svIyo.api prayogAt tadAshaMkA syAt | tAM nivArayituM bhAvashabdaH prayujyate | bhAvashabdayuktasvashabdasya svarUpa eva pratItijanakatvAditi bhAvaH |
nanvatra prakR^itipadaM svabhAvavAchakaM chettarhi prakR^itimityukte svasvabhAvamityuktaM bhavati | svashabdadvayaM cha svarUpavAchItyuktam | tathAcha punaruktirityata Aha || svati || yathA asvarUpe.apyupachAreNa svarUpapadapravR^ittestatpariharAya svasvarUpamityuchyate | na cha tatra svarUpavAchisvashabdadvayasadbhAve.api punaruktidoShaH | evamasvabhAve.apyupachAreNa svabhAvapadapravR^ittestadAshaMkAnivAraNAya svasvabhAva ityuchyate | ato na punaruktidoSha ityarthaH |    
ajo.apIti shlokatrayaM shrutyaiva vyAchaShTe || 6 || 7 || 8 ||
evaM svabhAvAdevAvatArAdivyApAramuktvA tajj~nAnaphalamuchyate "janmeti " | tatreshvarajanmakarmaj~nAnamAtreNa mokSho bhavatItyanyathApratItiM nirAchaShTe || yeShAmiti || samuchchayAdeva bhavatIti j~nAtavyamiti sheShaH | shamAdInAM samuchchayAdeva j~nAnaM bhavatIti j~nAtavyam | pR^ithak.hpR^ithagj~nAnasAdhanatvoktAvapItyarthaH | ukto grAhya iti sheShaH || 9 ||
etajj~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvaM kuta ityata uchyate  "vIteti " | tatra  "manmayAH ",  "madbhAvamAgatAH " ityetadanyathApratItinirAsAya smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || mayamiti || yadyapi bhagavAn pradhAno yeShAM te bhagavanmayA iti sAkShAdarthaH tathApi sarveShAM bhagavAn pradhAno bhavati | j~nAninAM ko visheSha ityataH  "prAdhAnyaM yairharermatam " ityuktam |  "madbhAvamAgatAH "ityasyArtha  "te muchyante " iti | madbhAvapadaM kathaM mokShavAchakamityata Aha || mayIti || mayi bhAvaH sAyujyAdiH || 10 ||
traividyAnAmapi mokShasadbhAvAt ko visheShastvAmupAshritAnAmityata uchyate  "iti | tatra namantaM namatItyAdyanyathApratItinirAsAyA.aha || tathaiveti || na j~nAninAM traividyAnAM cha phalasAmyam | sevAnusAreNaiva mama phaladatvAt | sevAyAshcha vaiShamyAditi bhAvaH | traividyAnAmanyadevatAyAjitvAt kathamuchyate tAM prapadyanta itItyato devatA yajanto yadi karmaNAM siddhimAkAN^kShanto bhavanti tarhi mama vartmAnuvartanta eva | anyathA karmaphalAbhAvAdityuchyate  "mama "iti | tatra traividyA api chedbhagavadvartmAnuvartante tarha bhAgavatatraividyabhedo na syAdityataH shlokaM vyAchaShTe || anyeti || matsamarpaNena anta iti sheShaH | atra smR^itisaMmatiM chAha || anyeti || 11 || 12 ||
bhagavadbhajanaM vinA kuto na phalamityatastasya pitR^itvAdyujyata ityuchyate  "chAturvaNyaM " iti | atra guNAnAM tritvAt kathaM chAturvarNyasya guNavibhAga ityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || sattveti || rAjananAttvikeShu sAttviko brAhmaNaH | sattvamadhikaM yato rajasastadvAn kShatriyaH | samasattvarajovAn vaishyaH | sajopekShayA.adhikatamovAn shUdra ityarthaH | anena sattvapradhAnatvaM brAhmaNAdInAmuktam | tasyApavAdamAha || sAttvikA eveti || vaiShNavA eva sAttvikAH sattvapradhAnAH | na brAhmaNatvAdiprayuktaM sAttvikatvAdItyarthaH |
karmavibhAgaH kIdR^isha ityata Aha || karmeti || yadi vaiShNavA eva sAttvikAstarhi brAhmaNAH sAttvikAH ityAdyuktiH kiMnimittetyAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharita || vaiShNavA iti || apare dveShiNaH | vaiShNavAnAM shUdrAdiShu daurlabhyAt brAhmaNA eva sAttvikA ityAdirUpeNa sAttvikatvAdInAM varNAshramabhedena bhinnatochyata ityarthaH | yathA sAttvikatvAdikaM na varNAmAtralakShaNaM tathA shamAdikamapi na varNamAtralakShaNam | kintu svAbhAvikavarNalakShaNamityat smR^itimAha || svAbhAvika iti || nanvasvAbhAvikaM brAhmaNatvAdikaM kIdR^ishamityata Aha || yonIti || ayamiti prasiddhaH |
svAbhAvikabrAhmaNasyaiva shamAdikam | svAbhAvikakShatriyasyaiva shauryAdItyAdyuktam | tatrApavAdamAha || viShNviti || shamapadoditA viShNubhaktiH na kevalaM brAhmaNasyaiva, api tu sarvavarNeShvanugatetyarthaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat | damAdikamapyevaM draShTavyam | kShatriye shamavati rAShTraviplavaH syAdityato nAyaM shamaH prasiddhaH | api tu viShNubhaktiriti shama iti vaktavye tadartha evoktaH | shamAdInAM kShatriyAdiShvapi sadbhAve kathamayaM brAhmaNo.ayaM neti svAbhAvikavarNabhedaj~nAnamityata Aha || vishvapatimiti || brAhmaNe shamAdInAM bAhulyAt kShatriyAdiShu krameNAbahulatvAt shamAdInAM bAhulyAbAhulyato.ayaM brAhmaNo.ayaM neti svAbhAviko varNabhedo j~nAtavya ityarthaH
