sarvakartR^itve bhagavataH karmalepaH syAdityata uchyate  "na mAmiti " | tatra mAmityasya siddhatvAt  "iti mAm " iti punarasmachChabdaH kimartha ityata Aha || jIveti || svasyeshvarAbhedAbhiprAyeNa svAtmAnamuddishya  "na mAM karmANi lampanti " ityAdi yo jAnAtItyanyathapratItiH syAt | tannirAkaraNArtham iti mAM yo.abhijAnAti, na svAtmAnamiti bhAvena mAmiti visheShaNaM prayuktamityarthaH || 13-16 ||
 "tatte karma pravakShyAmi " iti pratij~nAtamuchyate  "karmaNaH " iti | taddavargamArthatvAdvyAchaShTe || karmeti|| matta eva bhavatIti boddhavyam | asamAnapadasthasya rephottarasya nasya NatvaM dR^iShTaM  "brahma Na indra upayAhi vidvAn " ityAdau | Adipadena  "boddhavyaM cha " ityAderapi pUrvavadyojanAM sUchayati || 17 ||
etadbodhanaM stUyate  "karmaNi " iti | tatra pUrvArdhaM durgamArthatvAdvyAchaShTe || karmaNIti || karmavidhiphalayorabhAvAt akarmetyanena tadbhAvAjjIvaH karmeti sUchitam | jIveshvarayorevaM vyutpattyA vyutpattyA karmAkarmapadavAchyatvaM kuta ityata Aha || kara iti || amitatvAdaviShayIkR^itatvAdityarthaH | ko.ayaM karo nAmetyata Aha || kara iti || karashabdasya hastAdivAchitvameva dR^iShTaM, nAgR^iShTAdivAchitvamityata uktam | sakArAnta iti || hantAdivAchino.ayaM sakArAnto.anya eveti bhAvaH | karmavidhivAchI cheti draShTavyam | ata eva karmavidhItyAdyuktam | anena vidhishabdenAmitvam akarmapadena kathamuchyata iti parAstam | akartari jIve kathaM karo mIyata ityata Aha || taditi || nAkartari kriyAdarshanaM viruddhaM, svAtantryeNAkartR^itve.api bhagavadadhInakartR^itvAditi bhAvaH | ata eva pUrvamasvAtantryAdityAdyuktam | karmashabdasya jIve vidvadrUDhiM cha dshayati || prasiddhashcheti || nanu j~nAninaH svAtantryeNa pAratantryeNa vA kR^itsnakarmAkaraNAt kathaM kR^itsnakarmakR^ittvamuchyata ityata Aha || kR^itsneti || svayogyAsheShakarmaphalamokShasya niyatatvAditi bhAvaH || 18 ||
na kevalaM kartR^itvAbhimAnaparityAgena kR^itsnakarmakR^ittvAdi | api tu kAmAdiparityAgenApi bhAvyamityuchyate -yasyetyAdishlokapaJNchakena | tatra nirAshraya ityanyathA padavibhAgapratItinirAsAyAha || anirAshraya iti || pratItaprakAreNaiva padavibhAgaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || bhagavaditi || j~nAnino.api bhagavadAshrayatvena  "aj~nAnAM chaiva " ityAdAvuktatvAt nirAshrayatvAnupapatterna pratItaprakAreNa padavibhAga ityarthaH | nanvatra j~nAninaH sharIrasambandhasadbhAvAt kathaM muktatvamuchyata ityata Aha || muktasyeti || 19-23 ||
nanu kutra svAtantryAbhimAnatyAgo vivakShitaH? kiJNcha yaj~narthatvamiti pR^ichChati  "kathamiti " | tatparihArAyottarapraghaTTakamavatArayati || brahmeti || atrArpaNAdInAM brahmaikyamuchyate, nAbhimAnaparityAgaprakAra ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || brahmaNIti || pratItArtha eva kiM na syAdityataH svoktArthe smR^itisammatimAha || eka iti || anena havirAdiShu svasya svAtantryamanirUpya brahmAdhInatAM j~nAtvA homAdikaraNaM svAtantryAbhimAnaparityAgaH | brahmArpaNaM tu yaj~nArthatvamityuktaM bhavati || 24 ||
tatprapaJNchyate  "daivam " ityAdinA || tatra pUrvArdhe kasyachiddevasyopAsanamevochyate na tu brahmArphaNabuddhyA yajanam | ato nAyamardhaH pUrvasaN^gata ityata Aha || daivamiti || bhagavantaM yaj~na ityupAsata ityanena bhagavAneva yaj~naH tasya tathopAsanameva yaj~nakaraNamityuktaM bhavati | kathaM bhagavato yaj~natvam? yena tathopAsanaM yaj~nakaraNaM syAdityata Aha || sveti || svarUpamevAnandAdihaviH svayamevAgnirbhagavAn bhuN^kte, ato.ayaM yaj~na ityarthaH |  "brahmAgnau " ityetaddurgamArthatvAt pUrvasaN^gatatvena vyAchaShTe || brahmeti || yaj~nAkhyenetyasya sarvaM tadadhInaM j~nAtvetyarthaH || 25 ||
nanu  "shrotrAdIni " ityAdau shrotrAdihaviShaH saMyamAkhyAgnyAdau homa evochyate, na tu tasya brahmarpaNam | ato naitatpUrvasaN^gatamityata Aha || taditi || atrApi brahmArpaNasya  "evaM bahuvidhAH " iti vakShyamANaparyAlochanayA vivakShitatvAvagamAt nAsaN^gatiriti bhAvaH || 26 ||
|| indriyAdisaMyamamiti || karmendriyANAM prANApAnAdInAM cha saMyamamityarthaH | nanvatra kriyAyaj~na eva yaj~nenaivetyabhimAnatyAgokteH kathaM daivamityAdi pUrvasaN^gatamityata Aha || yaj~nenaiveti || svayameva yaj~na ityAdyapUrvArtho.ayaM kuta ityata Aha tenaiveti || 27-31 ||
 "brahmaNo mukhe " ityasya vedAdAvityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || shrotreti || iti shaMkA syAt tAmiti sheShaH | pratIta evarthaH kiM na syAdityata uktArthe smR^itisammatimAha || sarveti || 32 ||
dravyamayAdyaj~nAt j~nAnayaj~nasyottamatve heturuchyate  " sarvamiti " | tatra sarvAkhilashabdayorekArthatvapratIteH j~nAnAnantaraM karma nAstInyathApratIteshcha nirAsAyAha || sarvamiti || pUryate saphalaM bhavatItyAshayaH | samAptishabdasya pUrtivAchitvAdarshanAt kathamatra lUrtavAchitvamityata Aha || samApteti || dhanurvidyAviShaye sampUrNavidyAn kR^iShNasAtyakiyuktapaJNchayavachanam | astu pUrtAvapi samAptishabdaprayogaH | tathApyatra pUrtivAchitvaM kutaH? pratItArtha eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || j~nAneti || punaryogakathanAt j~nAnAnantaramapi karmAnuShThAnakathanAt || 33 ||
j~nAnasya karmaNo.adhikatvamuktvA tadApAdanaM vidhIyate  "taditi " tatra svayaM j~nAnopadeshAyaiva pravR^ittatvAt  "na tvevAham " iti j~nAnasyopadiShTatvAchcha katham  "upadekShyanti  te j~nAnam " ityuchyata ityata Aha || j~nAnamiti || upadekShyantIti nishchitatvAbhiprAyeNa | parokShatayopadekShyAma ityevochyamAnatvAt na j~nAnopadeshArthaM pravR^ittatvavirodhaH | na cha j~nAnasyopadiShTatvavirodhaH saN^kShepeNopadiShTatve.api  "j~nAnaM te.ahaM " ityAdinA punarupadekShyamANatvAditi bhAvaH || 34 ||
j~nAnaM stUyate  "yat iti | tatra svasmin, mayi chetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || AtmanIti || IshvaramantareNa sarvabhUtAdhAratvasyAnyatrAnupapatterna pratIta evArtha ityarthaH | evaM chet  "atho " iti samuchchayavAchI shabdo vyartha ityata Aha || atho iti || 35-40 ||
j~nAnaphalamuchyate  "yoga " iti | tatra  "AtmavantaM " ityAtmA jIvashchet svasambandhoktirayuktA.anupayuktA cha | paramAtmA chetsarveShAmapi tadvattvasAmyAt ko visheSho j~nAnina ityata Aha || Atmeti || 41-43 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM chaturtho.adhyAyaH || 4 ||
hariH OM || etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || yogeti || pUrvaM samuchchitaH karmayogo nirUpitaH | sacha yogasaMnyAsabhedena dvividhaH | dvividhayoshcha svarUpaM saN^kShepeNa  "kuru karmaNi ",   "saN^gaM tyaktvA " ityAdAvuktam | tadevAnenAdhyAyena spaShTayatItyarthaH |
prashnavAkyaM sAbhiprAyamavatArayati || yogeti ||  "yogasaMnyastakarmANam " ityAdau paThito nyAsashabdo yatyAshramaviShayo  "yogamAtiShTha " ityAdau shruto yogashabdo gR^ihasthAshramaviShaya iti kalpayitvA yatInAM sarvakarmatyAgena j~nAnamAtrAdhikAritvAt gR^ihiNAM j~nAnaparityAgena karmamAtrAdhikAritvAt tayorekapunniShThatvaM na yujyata iti bhAvena yogasaMnyAsayormadhye shreyaH pR^ichChati | ubhayasyApi kartavyatayA vihitatvAdekenaivAnuShThAtumashakyatvAt anyataraparityAgenAnyataragrahaNe shreyasa eva grAhyatvAditi bhAvaH || 1 ||
nanu yogasaMnyAsayormadhye shreyomAtra evAyaM prashno, na tUktarItyA virodhAbhiprAyeNa | tathAtve parihArAbhAvAdityataH parihAravAkyAbhiprAyamAha || eketi || ubhayorekapuMyogyatvAt niHshreyasakaratvAchcha anuShTheyatvAdanyatarasya shreShThatve prashno vyartha eva | atha svarUpaj~nAnamAtrArthaH prashnashchedyoga eva vishiShTa iti bhAvaH | yogasaMnyAsayorekapuMyogyatvAbhidhAyakaM padamatra na shrUyata ityatastatpaThitvA vyAchaShTe || ubhAviti || dvAvapi pratyekaM shreyaskarAvityarthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || saMnyAsastviti || yogarahitasaMnyAsasya anarthakaratvokteH saMnyAsarahitayogasyaivAsambhavAt samuchchitayoreva niHshreyasakaratvamuchyate na pratyekamiti bhAvaH || 2 ||
kathaM yogasaMnyAsayoH samuchchayo yujyate? yatigR^isthayoradhikArabhedAdityAshaMkAparihArAya shlokamavatArayati || dveShAdIti || atra  "saMnyastakarmANam " ityAdau | evaM  "yogamAtiShTha "ityAdau bhagavadarpaNAdIyoga evAbhipreto na gR^ihasthAshrama ityapi draShTavyam | nanu kathaM dveShAdivarjanasya saMnyAsatvamatrochyate?  "kAmyAnAM karmaNAM nyAsaM saMnyAsaM kavayo viduH " iti kAmyakarmaparityAgasya saMnyAsatvAbhidhAyakavAkyavirodhAdityata Aha || na cheti || bhavettadvirodho yadyatra dveShAdivarjanamAtraM saMnyAsatvena vivakShitaM syAt | naitadasti | kAmyakarmaparityAgenApi sahitasya dveShAdivarjanasya saMnyAsatvenAbhipretatvAdityarthaH | kathamatra kAN^kShAdivarjanasya saMnyAsatvamuchyate?  "sarvakarmaphalatyAgaM prAhustyAgaM vichakShaNaH " iti tasya tyAgatvenoktatvAt | na cha saMnyAsatyAgayoraikyAdavirodhaH |  "kAmyAnAM " iti shloke nyAsAttyAgasya pR^ithaktvenoktestadvirodhAdityata Aha || na cheti || bhavatyevAkAN^kShAdivarjanaM nyAsaH | na cha tasya tyAgatvoktivarodhaH | nyAsatyAgayoraikyAt | na cha pR^ithaktvoktivirodhaH | yathA khalu pANDavAnAM kurutve.api  "santAnabIjaM kurupANDavAnAm " iti pR^ithaguktiryujyate, pANDavAnAM kurvavAntarabhedatvena kurupANDavAnAM sAkShAdaikyAbhAvAt, evaM tyAgasya nyAsatve.api nyAsAvAntarabhedatvena tyAganyAsayoH sAkShAdaikyAbhAvAt pR^ithag vachanopapatteriti bhAvaH | nyasAdishabdasya yatyAdyAshramArthatvaM gR^ihItvA tayoradhikArabhedAt samAveshAyogo yashchodito.asau nyAsAdishabdasya tadarthatvAnaN^gIkAreNa parihR^itaH || 3 ||
athAsAvadhikArabhedo.api na yujyata ityuchyate  "sAN^khya "iti | durgamArthatvAt shlokaM vyAchaShTe || bAlA iti || j~nAnamArgaM samyagAsthita eva j~nAnaphalaM prApnoti | karmakArgaM cha samyagAsthita eva karmaphalaM prApnotItyarthaH |  
j~nAnaikagamyayatiprApyasthAnaprAptisadbhAvAchcha gR^idiNAM j~nAnAdhikAro.astItyuktvA upasaMhriyate  "yat " iti | tatra " ekaM sAN^khyaM " ityupasaMhAravAkye j~nAnakarmaNoraikyaM kimarthamuchyata ityato yathAvadvyAchaShTe || tasmAditi || j~nAninAM yatInAmiti sheShaH | samyakkarmAnuShThAnenaiva karmI karmaphalaM prApnoti chettathApi kutastasya j~nAnamityata Aha || na hIti || evaM samyagj~nAnamArgAnuShThAnainaiva j~nAnaphalaM prApnoti chettathApi kuto j~naninaH karmeti shaN^.hkAyAM na hi karma vinA j~nAnamArgastha samyaganuShThAnaM bhavati | saMpUrNaphalasAdhanatvAbhAvAditi parihAro draShTavyaH | atra smR^itisammatiM chAha || niShkAmamiti || anena karmiNAM j~nAnamuchyate |  " buddhyA " iti j~nAnasadbhAve hetvantaramAha || etasmAditi ||  " muktiH " ityubhayam |
karmiNAM j~nAnasadbhAvAdevetyarthaH | anena  " yatsAN^khyaiH " iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | ubhayorapi j~nAnakarmasadbhAve kathamAshramabheda ityata Aha || tasmAditi || ubhayorapyubhayasadbhAvasya yuktyAdisiddhatvAditi bhAvaH | saN^.hkochavikAsa sambhavaH || 4 || 5 ||
samuchchitayoreva yogasaMnyAsayorniHshreyasakaratvamuktam | asamuchchaye bAdhakamuchyate  " saMnyAsastu " iti | tatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || mokSheti || yoga iti || uchyata iti sheShaH | viShNvarpitatayA tadrUpa iti sambandhaH | pAdatrayam uttarArdhavyAkhyAtam |  " nAnyaH " iti pUrvArdhasya | tadvivR^iNoti || viShNviti || Adipadena svochitakarmaNAM viShNvarpaNAdikaM na kAryamiti buddhyA kR^ito narakaphala iti j~nAtavyam |  " ayogataH " iti yogarUpatvaM vineti kimarthamuchyate | yogaM vinetyeva kiM na syAdityata Aha || yamiti || yaM saMnyAsam " iti yogasaMnyAsayoraikyasya vakShyamANatvAt saMnyAsasya yogarUpatvameva vAchyamityarthaH | yogasaMnyAsayoraikye  " saMnyAsaH karmayogashya " iti pR^ithaguktiH kathamityata Aha || yogeti || yogo nyAsashchetyeka evArthaH | api tu nyAso yogAvAntarabhedaH | ataH kurupANDavavat pR^ithaguktirupapannetyarthaH || 6 ||
yogarUpatAM vinA nyAsasyAnarthasAdhanatvamuktvA |  " yogayuktaH " ityanena yogarUpasaMnyAsasyoktaM mokShasAdhanatvaM prapaJNchyate || yogayukta iti || tatra yogasaMnyAsayoreva vaktavyatvAt tayoshcha yogayuktAdipadairuktatvAt  " sarvabhUtAtmabhUtAtmA " iti kimuchyata ityata Aha || rarveti || anenApi yoga evochyata iti nAsaN^gatiH | nApi yogayuktapadena yogasyoktatvAdvaiyyarthyam | yogayuktapadena karmayogasyoktatvAt , anena dhyAnayogasyoktatvAditi bhAvaH |
atrAdhikAriNaH sarvabhUtaikyamuchyate | ataH kathamiyaM dhyAnayogokitirityuchyata ityataH smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || AdAnAditi || bhUtamanAH sthitamanAH || 7 ||
yogarUpasaMnyAsasya mokShahetutvamuktam | tatra saMnyAsasya yogarUpatvaM kena prakAreNetyatantatparihAratvena shlokadvayamavatArayati || yatheti || tatrendriyANAmeva svatantryeNa kartR^itvamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAya smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || viShNunati || 8 || 9 ||
yogarUpasaMnyAsavato muktirbhavatIti nopachAramAtramiti bhAvena punaH phalamuchyate  " brahmaNi " iti | tatra karmaNAM brahmaNyAdhAnaM nAmAkaraNamevetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || tatpUjeti || AdhAnaM karmaNAmiti sheShaH | anyathA karotItyasya vyAghAtAditi bhAvaH | bhavatpakShe.api yadi karmANi bhagavatkR^itAni tarhi jIvasyAkatrR^itvaM syAt | tathAcha karotIti vyAhataM syAt | mama shubhArthamiti chAsambhavItyata Aha || svAtantryeti || karmaNAM bhagavatkR^itatve jIvasyAkartR^itvaM syAditi satyameva | na cha tAvatA jIvasya kartR^itvaphalasambandhAnupapattiH | svatantryAbhAvavivakShayaiva akartR^itvasyAbhyupagatatvena bhagavadadhInatayA kartR^itvopapatteriti bhAvaH | asvatantratve cha jIvasya bhagavatpUjAkartR^itvaM shubhayogashcha na yujyate | asvatantre kartR^ishabdaprayogasya phalasambandhasya chAdarshanAdityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || svavandanamiti || kAritaM shishuneti sheShaH | shishukartR^ikaM bhavediti sambandhaH || 10-12 ||
itashcha karmaNAM brahmaNyAdhAnaM nAma tatra svasya svAtantryAbhimAnatyAga eva | na tu svarUpaparityAga ityAha || ata iti ||  " brahmaNyAdhAya karmANi " iti saMnyAso hyuchyeta | tallakShaNaM cha  " sarvakarmANi " ityanena prapaJNchyate | tatra karmaNAM svarUpaparityAgAbhAvAdeva hi manasaiva tyAgo.abhihitaH | atashcha nAtrApi karmaNAM svarUpatyAgo.artha iti bhAvaH | manasaiva tyAgAbhidhAne kathaM svarUpatyAgAbhAva ityaha Aha || asvAtantryeti || manasaiva karmanyAso nAma svAtantryAbhimAnaparityAga eva | na tu svarUpatyAgaH | tathAtve manaseti visheShaNavaiyyarthyAditi bhAvaH || 10-13 ||
yaduktaM jIvAnAM svAtantryAbhAvApekShayaivAkartR^itvaM, paratantrakartR^itvaM tvastyeveti na tadyuktam |  " na kartR^itvaM " ityuttaravAkyavirodhAdityata Aha || yatheti || svato jIvAnAM svatantrakartR^itvAdyabhAve.api paramAtmadattaM tadasti | ataH kathaM brahmaNyAdhAnamuchyata ityAshaMkAmevAtra pariharati | na tu jIvAnAM sarvAtmanA kartR^itvAbhAvaM vaktIti bhAvaH | karmaphalasaMyoge cha svAtantryamityapi saMyojyam | anena  " na kartR^itvaM na karmANi " iti paunaruktyaM cha paridR^itam | nanvatra kartR^itvAdyabhAva evochyate, na tu tatrAsvAtantryam | ataH kathamanenaiShA shaMkA parihriyata ityata Aha kriyAyAmiti || kartR^itvAdikaM na sR^ijatItyasya tatra 
svAtantryaM na sR^ijatItyevArthaH | ato bhavatyetadAshaMkAparihAra ityarthaH | nanvatreshvarasyaiva kartR^itvAdyabhAva uchyata iti kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || yadyatreshvarasyaiva kartR^itvAdyabhava uchyate tadA lokasya kartR^itvAdikaM na sR^ijatIti vyarthaM syAdityarthaH |
yaduktaM jIvasya pAratantryeNa kartR^itavAdyastIti na tadyuktam | kartR^itvAdi Ishvaro lokasya na sR^ijatItyuktatvAt | na cha tra tasya svAtantryaM na sR^ijatItyarthaH | kartR^itvAdisadbhAve.api svAtantryApradAnAbhiprAyeNa kartR^itvAdikaM na sR^ijatItyevaMjAtIyaprayogAdarshanAdityata Aha || janapada iti || yadyatra jIvAnAM sarvAtmaneshvarasya cha kartR^itvaM na niShidhyeta tarhi  " svabhAvastu pravartate " iti svabhAvadeva pravR^ittikathanaM na yujyata ityata Aha || svayameveti || nAtra svabhAvapadena prasiddhasvabhAvo.abhidhIyate | yonoktavirodhaH | kintu svasthitAvanyakaraNe cha paranirapekShatvAdbhagavAnevetyarthaH | prasiddhapadaparityAgenAprasiddhapadaprayogaH kimarthamityato hetusUchanArthamiti bhAvena vAkyArthamAha || svabhAvatvAditi || 
nanu kimarthamevamarthAntaraM kalpanIyam? jIvasyeveshvarasya cha kartR^itvAdikaM nAstyeva | vishvapravR^ittistu svabhAvAdevetyarthaH kiM na syAt? lokasyetyasya lokaviShaya ityarthopapatterityataH svoktArthe smR^itisammatimAha || svAtantryAditi || nAsyasya sR^ijati | api tu svayameva pravartata iti sheShaH | Ishvarasyaiva kartR^itve karmalepaH syAdityata Aha || svAtantryAdeveti || anena  " nAdatte " ityasyArtho.apyukto bhavati | evaM sarveShu sthitvA svAtantreNa kartA Ishvaro.asti chet kathaM na dR^ishyata ityata Aha || aj~nAneti || etenAj~nAneti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati |
yaduktamIshvaraH svayameva bhAvayatIti na tadyuktam | tasya kartR^itvAbhAvAt | tasya kartR^itvasadbhAve.api tasyAsvAbhAvavikatvAdityata Aha || ahamiti || ahaM sarvasyeti vachanadvayaM kartR^itvasadbhAve mAnam | parAsyetyAdikaM kartR^itvasya svAbhAvikatve | tvadR^ite dUre samIpe vA kiJNchana kenApi na kriyata ityarthaH | atra bhagavaditarasya kartR^itvAbhAvoktyA IshvarakartR^itvasyAparAdhInatvasambhavena svAbhAvikatvamevochyate | lokavadityatrApi phalAdyapekShA.abhAvena kartR^itvoktyA tasya svAbhAvikatvamevochyate | itashcha neshvarasya akartR^itvamasvAbhAvikaM kartR^itvaM chetyAha || viparIteti || nanvasmAbhirIshvarasya kartR^itvamasvAbhAvikapadenAnirvAchyamabhipreyate | na tu phalApekShaM parAdhInaM vA | ato nodAhR^itavachanavirodha ityata Aha || anirvAchyeti || Ishvarasya kartR^itvamanirvachanIyamiti pakSho dvitIyAdhyAye.anirvAchyavastuno nirastatvAdeva nirastaH | ato na punaratra nirasanIya iti bhAvaH |
nanu brahmaNaH sarvavisheSharahitatvAt kathaM paramArthataH kartR^itvaM syAdityata Aha || na cheti || bhavedbrahmaNaH kartR^itvasyApAramArthikatveM, yadi tasya sarvavisheSharAhityaM syAt | na cha tadyuktam | tathAtve brahmaNaH shUnyatvApattyA tadabhyupagantR^iNAM shUnyavAditvApAtAditi bhAvaH | sarvavisheSharahitatve.api na brahmaNaH shUnyatvApattiH, astitvAdityata Aha || na hIti || na bhavedbrahmaNaH shUnyatvApattiH, yadi tasyAstitvaM sidhyet | na cha tatsiddhiH | sarvavisheSharahitamityaN^gIkArAditi bhAvaH | sarvavisheSharahitatve.api kuto.astitvaM na siddhyatItyata Aha || vAchyatveti || astitve brahmaNaH astitvamastishabdavAchyatvaM vA syAt | tasya cha visheShatvAt na tatsarvavisheSharahitasya yujyata iti bhAvaH |
bhavennirvisheShatve.astitvAsiddhiH, yadyastitvaM brahmaNo visheShatayA aN^gIkrayate | naitadasti | tasya brahmasvarUpamAtratvAdityata Aha || anyatheti || yadyastitvAdikaM brahmaNaH svarUpamAtraM na tadvisheShastarhi brahma brahmetivadasti brahmetyAdishabdAnAM paryAyatvaM syAt | tatashcha  " asti brahmeti chedveda " ityAdisahaprayogAnupapattiH syAt | tathA chopaniShadAM punaruktidoSheNa unmattavAkyavadanAdaraNIyatvaM syAditi bhAvaH | brahmaNyastitvAdivisheShAbhAve.api AropitAsattvAdivisheShavyAvR^ittikathanadvArA astyAdipadAni tallakShayanti | ato na shabdAnAM paryAyatvAdItyata Aha || vyAvartyeti || bhavedastyAdipadAnAmaparyAyatvaM, yadyastyAdipadAni brahmaNo.asattvAdi vyAvartayanti | na cha tadyuktam | vyAvartyAsattvAdivisheShavyAvR^itteH vyAvR^ittatayA.aN^gIkR^itabrahmagatAstitvAdivisheShanivandhanatvAt | teShAM chAnaN^gIkArAt | brahmaNyastitvAdivisheShabhAve.api asattvAdivyAvR^ittAvasato.api tadvyAvR^ittiprasaN^gAt | gaN^gApadalakShyo.api tIre gaN^gAtvAbhAve.api agaghgAtvavyAvR^ittiprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH |
ito.apyastyAdipadAni astitvAdivisheShabodhakAni neti na yuktamityAha || anyatheti || yadyastyAdipadAni na astitvAdibrahmavisheShabodhakAni tarhi teShAM vaiyyarthyameva syAt | brahmajij~nAsuM prati brahmakathanasyaiva sArthakyAt | brahmaNashcha brahmapadAdevAvagatatvAt | na chAsattvAdivyAvR^ittiH prayojanam | tadasambhavasyoktatvAt | brahma kuto vyAvR^ittamityajij~nAsitatvAchcha | ajij~nAsitatve.api brahmaNyasattvAdibhrAntiH nivAryata iti chenna | vikalpAsahatvAt | bhrAntiH kiM pratIte.apratIte vA brahmaNi bhavet? | nAdyaH | brahmapratItau tanmAtrasya sattvAderapi pratItatvena bhrAntyanavakAshAt | brahmapratItAvapi sattvAdyapratItau tanmAtratvAnupapatteH | na dvitIyaH | adR^iShTakalpanAprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH |
itashcha na astyAdipadairasattvAdivyAvR^ittidvArA brahma lakShyam | tasya sarvashabdAvachyatvAN^gIkArAt | shabdavAchyasyaiva 
lakShyatvadsanAdityAha || na cheti | astitvAN^gIkAre brahmaNaH savisheShatvaprasaN^gAt na tatsiddhyatItyuktam | ito.api na brahmaNo.astitvaM siddhyati | tatpramANAbhAvAt | pramANaM vinA.arthasiddheH kvApyadarshanAt | pramANakathane cha sarvapramANAgocharatvAN^gIkArabhaN^ga iti bhAvaH | yadyastitve pramANAbhAvAt na tatsiddhyatItyuchyate tarhi brahmaNo nAstitvamapi na siddhyati | tatra pramANAbhAvAt | tathAcha na shUnyavAdAvisheShApAdanaM brahmavAdasya yujyata ityata Aha || nAstitvamiti || brahmaNo na nAstitve.asmAbhiH pR^ithak pramANaM vaktavyam | tasyAstitvapramANAbhAvenaiva siddheH | yathA khalu saptamarasAdyastitve pramANAbhAvAt nAstitvaM siddhyati tathaivetyarthaH | anenAnupalabdhiliN^gakamanumAnaM sUchitaM bhavati |
nanu pramANAvedyatve.api brahmaNo na nAstitvaM vAchyam | svaprakAshatayaiva tastiddheriti yenna, vikalpAnupapatteH | tathAhi-svaprakAshatve brahmaNaH pramANamasti na vA? na tAvAddvitIyaH | pramAmAbhAve tadasiddherityAha || svaprakAshatvaM cheti || Adye svaprakAshatvaM brahmAtiriktaM tatsvarUpameva vA? prathamaM dUShayati || svayaMprakAshatvAmiti || yadi brahmaNaH svatiriktaM svayaMprakAshatvaM prAmANikaM syAttadA tasya savisheShatvaM prasajyata ityarthaH | dvitIyaM dUShayiti || na chediti || yadi svayaMprakAshatvaM na brahmAtiriktaM, kintu tatsvarUpameva tarhi svayaMprakAshatve pramANasadbhAvAN^gIkAre brAhmaiva pramANagamyAmaN^gIkR^itaM syAt | tathAchAprameyatvabhaN^ga ityarthaH |
na svaprakAshapadena svaviShayaprakAshatvamuchyate | yena tasya brahmAtiriktatve brahmaNaH savisheShatvaM syAt | kintu paraprakAshatvAbhAva evetyata Aha || pareti || yadi svaprakAshapadena paraprakAshanirAsamAtramabhipreyate tarhi brahmaNaH prakAsharAhityameva syAt | paraprakAshasyAnabhimatatvAt | svaviShayaprakAshatvAkhyAsya svaprakAshatvasyoktarItyA pramAmAbhAvena, bhAve cha savisheShatvaprameyatvaprAptyA nirastatvAditi bhAvaH |
tathApi na nAstitvaM brahmaNo vaktR^iM shakyate |  " asti brahma " ityAdishrutyA asattvAdivyAvR^ittidvArA brahmaNi lakShite.arthatastasyAstitvasiddheriti chenna | dUShitatvAt | abhyupagamyApyAha || arthata iti || tatpramANata iti || asti brahmeti shrutipramANata ityarthaH | yaduktaM svaprakAshatvena brahma siddhyatIti tadvyAhataM chetyAha || svaprakAsheti || na svaprakAshapadena svaviShayaprakAshatvamaN^gIkriyate | kintu paraprakAshatvAnaN^gIkAramAtrameva | ataH svaparaprakAshUnyatayA svaprakAshatvena brahmaNo.asiddhireva syAnna tu tena tatsiddhirityarthaH |
kiJNcha bhaved brahmaNaH svaprakAshatA yadi prakAshatvameva sambhavet | na cha tatsambhavati | brahmAkhyAprakAshasya prakAshyarahitatvAt | na tAvat svayaM prakAshyam | anaN^gIkArAt | nApyanyat | tadabhAvAt | na cha prakAshyarahitaprakAsharUpaM brahmeti vAchyam | svamanyaM vA prakAshyaM vinA prakAshasyAdR^iShTatvAt | yathA bhojyarahitaM bhojanaM na dR^iShTaM tathaivetyAha || prakAsha iti || nanvekasyAM kiyAyAmekasyaiva kartR^itvaM karmatvaM cha viruddham | ataH kathaM prakAshyaM vinA prakAsho na dR^iShTa ityuchyate | svasyaiva prakAshyate svayameva prakAshayati prakAshate chetyekasyaiva kartR^itvakarmatvApatterityata Aha || kartR^ikarmeti || mAmahaM jAnAmItyekasyaivaikasyAM viruddhamiti bhAvaH |
nanu prakAsho nAma dravyam | ataH kathaM tasya bhojanAdivat karmApekShetyAshaMkAM pariharan adhikaM cha doShamAha || j~nAnaM cheti || brahmaNaH prakAshatvaM nAma j~nAnatvamabhyupagatam | na cha j~nAnatvaM brahmaNo yuktam | j~nAtR^ij~neyarahitatvAt | tadrahitaj~nAnasyAdR^iShTatvAdityarthaH | upasaMharati || ata iti || yataH sarvavisheSharahitatvenAprameyatvena cha brahmaNo na astitvaM siddhyatyata ityarthaH | bhagavataH kartR^itvAbhAvAdinirAkaraNamupasaMharati || ata iti || duShTatvAt || kartR^itvaM nAsti, sadbhAve vA.asvAbhAvikamiti matasya | punarIshvarasya svabhAvataH kartR^itve shrutiM chAha || haririti || 14 ||
 " j~nAnena " iti prakR^itataj~nAnasya sAdhanAntaramuchyate  " vidyA " iti | tatra na brAhmaNAdiviShaye samabuddhitvaM vivakShitam | kintu tadgataparabrahmaviShaya eva | brAhmaNAdInAM viShamatvAt tadgatabrahmaNa eva samatvAt viparItaj~nAnasya cha j~nAnAsAdhanatvAditi bhAvena jIvAnAM baiShamye brahmaNaH sAmye cha pramANamAha || viShameShviti || anena  " nirdoShaM hi samaM brahma " ityetadapi vyAkhyAtaM bhavati || 18-20 ||
yaduktaM yogarUpasaMnyAsasya niHshreyakaratvaM tadupapAdyate  " bAhya " iti | taddurgamArthatvAdvyAchaShTe || saMsAre.api paramAtmasmaraNAdyalpayogayuktaH saMnyAsI sukhaM vindati yadA tadA dhyAnAdimahAyogayukto mokShAdiniHshreyasaM vindatIti kimu vAyyamityarthaH || 21-23 ||
j~nAnilakShaNamuchyate  " yo.antaHsukhaH " iti | tatra brahmabhUtapadaM brahmaNaikIbhUta ityanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || brahmaNIti || manaseti sheShaH | pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAditi chenna | j~nAnino.api brahmabhedasya sAdhitatvAt | doShAntaraM chAha || anyatheti || yadyatra j~nAnino brahma bhAvo.abhidhIyate tarhi brahmAdhigachChatIti viruddhaM syAt | na hi kashchit svayaM svAtmAnaM gachChatItyarthaH | nanvatra antaHsukhatvAdikaM bhavatu j~nAnilakShaNam | antarjyotiShTvaM kathaM brahmadarshino lakShaNaM syAt | yAvatA brahmadarshitvameva tadityata Aha 
|| antaHsukhatvAdikamiti || nAtrAntarjyotiShTvaM j~nAnilakShaNamuchyate | kintu antaHsukhatvAdyeva | tatra kAraNatvenAntarjyotiShTvamuchyata iti bhAvaH || 24-27 ||
brahmayogAdipadena prAkR^itadhyAnaprakAra uchyate  " sparshAn " iti | tatra dhyAnino.amuktasya kathaM  " mukta eva saH " iti muktatvamuchyata ityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || amukta iti || muktasAdR^ishyamabhimAnAdiparityAgaH | mukta evochyata iti sheShaH | yasmAt j~nAnasAmarthyena evaM phalaM bhavati tasmAt || 28-29 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpAkAyAM paJNchamo.adhyAyaH || 5 ||
hariH OM|| etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || dhyAnamiti ||  " yoge tvimAM shrR^iNu " iti pratij~nAtam | yogashcha karmayogo dhyAnayogashcheti dvedhA bhAvati | tatra saN^kShepavistarAbhyAM karmayogo nirUpitaH | dhyAnayogaprakArashcha saN^kShepeNa paJNchamAnte nirUpito vistareNAsminnadhyAye uchyata iti bhAvaH |
prakR^itaM dhyAnamagnyAdiparityAgena nissaN^gatayA sartamAnasya bhavatItyAshaMkA nirasyate  " anAshrita " iti | tatra niragneH saMnyAsitvaM yogitvaM cha nAstItyuktaM nopapadyate | tathAsati yatyAshramasyAnanuShTheyatvaprasaN^gAt | yaterniragnitvena yogasaMnyAsAbhAvaprApteH | tayoreva shreyaHsAdhanatvAdityata Aha || sa iti || bhavedanena yatyAshramasyAnanuShTheyatvaprasaN^go yadi yaterniragnitvaM syAt | na cha tadasti | sa brahmaniShTha iti tasyApyagnishravaNAditi bhAvaH | itashcha na yateragnitvamityAha || Atmeti || yatyashramasvIkArakAle pUrvAshramasvIkR^itAgnerAtmani samAropaNAchcha na yateranagnitvamityarthaH | anena na kevalaM niragnirakriyo yatireva saMnyAsI yogI cha | kintvanAshritaH karmaphalaM kAryaM karma karoti yaH so.apItyapavyAkhyAnaM cha nirAkR^itaM bhavati || 1 ||
saMnyAsI yogI chetyuktyA prAptA saMnyAsayogayoH pR^ithaktvAshaMkA nivAryate  " saMnyAsam " iti | tatra saMnyAsayogasoraikye kathaM pR^ithaguktirityata Aha || yogeti || 2 ||
karmayogamadhye kIdR^isho yogo j~nAnArthino.avashyApekShita ityata uchyate  " ArurukShoH " iti | tatra yogarUDhapadasya durgamArthatvAdarthamAha || sampUrNeti || atra j~nAnArthinaH karma apekShitamityuktvAt j~naninaH karmopashamo.apekShita ityuchyate | tathAcha na niragnirna chAkriya ityAdivirodha ityata Aha || nAneti || nAnAjanasya uttamAdhamamadhyamasya || karavanmiteriti || rAjAdikaravadAvashyakatayA pramitatvAdityarthaH | yogasthenApi shushrUShAyAH kAryatve ko visheSho yogArthiyogasthayorityata Aha || tenApIti || anyairyogArthibhiH | yogArithiyogasthayorvisheShe vaktavye asiddhasiddhayorvisheShaH kimarthamuchyata ityata Aha || prApteti || nAnAjanasya shushrUShA kathaM j~nAnasya sAdhanamityato bhagavatprasAdadvAretyAha || tasyeti || nanvaj~nAnAmapi harau sthitatvAdyogasthena harau sthitiH kAryeti kimuchyata ityata uktaM vivR^iNoti || siddheti || anyat nAnAjanashushrUShAdi | j~nAnino mokShaniyamAt kiM dhyAnAdinetyata Aha || tasyeti || tatashcha muktAvAnandapUrtiriti bhAvaH | atra karmapadena nAnAjanashushrUShaivochyate na tu sandhyAvandanAdi | shamapadena cha nAnAjanashushrUShopashama evochyate | bhagavaddhyAnAdikaM cha | na sandhyAvandanAdikarmopashamaH | nAnAjanasyeti smR^itisamAkhyAnAt | ato nAsya pUryoktavirodha iti bhAvaH | shamapadasya viShNudhyAnAdivAchitve spaShTarthAM smR^itiM chAha || shama iti || 3 ||
yogarUDhalakShamuchyate  " yadA hi " iti | tatra na karmasvanuShajyata iti j~nAninaH karmAbhAvakathanAnna chAkriya ityAdivirodha ityata Aha || kathamiti || nAtra j~nAninaH svarUpataH karmAnuShaN^go.abhidhIyate | kintu sarvakarmasu saN^.hkalpanyAnenaiva | tathA svayameva vyAkhyAtatvAditi bhAvaH | yadi sarvakarmasu saN^.hlpanyAsastarhi karmasvarUpanyAsa eva prApnoti | svarUpAtyAge saN^.hkalpatyAgAyogAdityata Aha || mayIti || bhavetkarmasvarUpatyAgaprAptiryadi saN^.hkalpasvarUpatyAgo.abhipretaH syAt | na chAsAvasti | saN^.hkalpasaMnyAsapadena saN^.hkalpAderbhagavadadhInatAj~nAnasyaivAbhipretatvAt | mayI sarvANi karmANi saMnyasyaityatra saMnyAsapadasya bhagavadadhInatAj~nAnArthatAyAH samarthitatvAditi bhAvaH | prakANAntaraM chAha || madadhInamiti || 4 ||
yogArohasya bhagavatprasAdo mukhyasAdhanamityuchyate  " uddharet " iti | tatrA.atmapadaM jIvAdimAtraviShayaM na paramAtmaviShayamityanyathApratItinirAsAya smR^itvaiva vyAchaShTe || uddhareteti || kIdR^ishAH santaH kIdR^ishA asanta ityata uktaM vivR^iNoti || taditi || tadanyasya bhaktyA.avashIkR^itaparamAtmanaH puruShasya | ito.apyatra Atmapadena paramAtmagrahaNaM yuktamityAha || paramAtmeti || yena AtmA vashIkR^itastasyAsau bandhutayA kiM karotItyapekShAyAM vAkyasheShe vashIkR^ito.asau paramAtmA tasya hR^idi samyagAhito bhavatItyuktatvAt pUrvamapyAtmApadena paramAtmaivochyata iti j~nAyata iti bhAvaH || 5 || 6 ||
yogArUDhalaNaM prapaJNchyate  " shItoShNa " iti | tatra j~nAnavij~nAnashabdayorarthabhedaM smR^ityaivAha || sarvatreti || sarvatra vedAdau || 7 || 8 ||
nanu suhR^idAdInAM viShamatvAt kathaM teShu j~nAninaH samabuddhitvamuchyata ityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva paraharati || yasyeti || suhR^inmitrapadayoH aridveShyapadayoH udAsInamadhyasthapadayoshcha ekArthatvapratItinirAsAya smR^ityaiva tadarthamAha || animitteti || j~nAtvopakArakR^iditi || svayameva tasya kleshasthAnaM nirUpyopakArakartetyarthaH || 9-19 ||
yogasampUrtisvarUpamuchyate  " yadA " ityAdinA | tatra AtmanA.a.atmAnamityAtmashabdayorjIvAdiviShayatvapratItinirAsAyAha || AtmAnamiti || anyathA toShAyogAditi bhAvaH || 20-26 ||
yogaphalamuchyate  " prashAnta " iti | tatra brahmabhUtapadasya anyArthapratItinirAsAyArthamAha || brahmaNIti || anyathA bahupramANavirodhaditi bhAvaH || anena pUrvoktaM matsaMsthApadamapi vyAkhyAtaM bhavati || 27-28 ||
dhyeyamuchyate  " sarvabhUtastham " iti | tatrAtmapadena jIva uchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || sarveti || bhoktAramiti saN^kShepoktau paramAtmana eva dhyeyatvokteH, yo mAmityanuvAdAchcheti bhAvaH || 29-30 ||
paramAtmadhyAnaphalamuchyate  " sarvaM " iti | tatra  " NakatvamAsthitaH " ityetadanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || sarvatrate || anyathA sarvabhUtasthitamiti svavachanavirodhAditi bhAvaH || 31 ||
yogina eva itthambhAvAntaramuchyate  " AtmA " iti | tatsarvaprANiviShayamityanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || ata iti || atra bhagavadIyoShveva svas.hminniva sneho vidhIyate, na tvavaiShNaveShu | vandhurAtmeti vaiShNavAnAnameva bhagavatpriyatvasyoktatvAt , anAtmana ityavaiShNavAnAM bhagadapriyatvasyoktatvAditi bhAvaH || 32-36 ||
ayatirityarjunaprashnavAkyagatAyatipadasya gR^ihasthAdirityanyathApratItinirAsAyArthamAha || ayatiriti || gR^ihasthAdirevArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || prayatnAditi || ayatestatra shraddhAvashAt chaturthAshramI bhavatIti parihAraprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | nanu yogashabdasya j~nAnopAyArthatvAt shraddhAvAn labhate j~nAnamityAdeH shraddhAyA api j~nAnopAyatvAt shraddhayopeto yogAchchalitamAnasa iti parasparavirodha ityata Aha || yogeti || bhavedayaM virodho yadi yogashabdenAtra sAmAnyato j~nAnopayo.abhidhIyate | na cha tadasti | dhyAnasyaiva vivakShitatvAt | na cha yogashabdasya j~nAnopAyavAchitvavirodhaH | dhyAnasyApi j~nAnopAyavisheShatvAditi bhAvaH |
yogAchchalitamAnasasya  " prApya puNyakR^itAn lokAn " ityAdiphalamupapAdyate  " jij~nAsuH " iti | tatra yogajij~nAnoH vidhiniShedhAbhAvapratItinirAsAya tatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || mokSheti || tadAsthita iti || tatrAlpapravR^ittimAnityarthaH || 44-45 ||
yogaH stUyate  " tapasvibhya " iti | tatra yogasya j~nAnArthatvAt kathaM j~nAnAduttamatvamuktamityataH tatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || tapasa iti || aj~nAnidhyAnana iti || samyag dhyAnaprakArAj~nasya dhyAnato dhyAnaprakAraj~nAnamevottamam | dhyAnaprakAraj~nAnasahitaM dhyAnaM dhyAnaprakAraj~nAnamAtrato.adhikamityarthaH | dhyAniShvapi tAratamyamAha || tatrApIti || kIdR^isho.abhakta ityata Aha || anyeti || na bhaktiryeShu te.abhaktayaH | anyAn madadhInAn jAnannityanana parivAratayA anyopAsanamuchyate | madupAsakeShvapi viShuddhadhIH niShkAmo vara ityarthaH anena yoginAmiti shloko vyAkhyAto bhavati | tathAhi-sarveShAM yoginAM madhye yaH shraddhAshabdoditamadbhaktimAn sa eva yukto mataH | tatrApi yo mAM bhajate sa eva yuktataro mataH | tatrApi phalakAmanAM vinA yo mAM bhajate na yuktatamo mata iti || 46-47 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM ShaShTho.adhyAyaH || 6 ||
hariH OM|| etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || bhagavaditi || yatpUrvoktaM dhyAnaM tadbhaktipUrvakameva j~nAnasAdhanaM, nAnyathA | ato bhaktyarthaM bhagavanmahimA.asminnadhyAye.abhidhIyata ityarthaH | na tvevAhamityAdinA prAgapi bhagavanmahimno varNatatvAt kimananetyata uktam || visheShata iti || prAk saN^kShepeNokto.atra vistareNochyata ityarthaH | uparitanAdhyAyAnAmapi bhagavanmahimAbhidhAyakatvAdartetyAhi noktam |
pratij~nAte j~nAne lipsAmutpAdayituM daurlabhyaM tasyochyate "manuShyANAm " iti || tatmR^itibhirvyAchaShTe || anantAnAmiti || kechanaiva chet samyagvidustarhi kathamitareShAM mokSha ityata Aha || anyeShAmiti || anena yatatAmapi kechit siddhA bhavantIti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | jIvanmuktAnAM sarveShAmapi siddhipadoditA muktirbhavati | siddhiM gatAH sarvepi nArAyaNAyanAH, tajj~nAnAdimattvAt | nArAyaNaparAyaNastu sudurlabha ityarthaH | jIvaghano jIvasAraH | anena na kevalaM mahAj~nAnino daurlabhyamapi tu mahAbhaktyAdimAnapi durlabha ityuktaM bhavati || 3 ||
pratij~nAtaM j~nAnamuchyate  " bhUmiH " ityAdinA | tatmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || achetaneti || chetanA shrIrityanena jIvabhUtAmiti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | te ubhe ityanena me prakR^itirityasyArtha ukto bhavati | etadyonInItyasyArtho jagata iti | viShNoreva jagatkAraNatvAt kathametadityata Aha || piteti || pitR^itvenaiva viShNuH kAraNamityarthaH | anenAhaM kR^itsnasyeti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tarhi prakR^ityoH 
kIdR^ishaM kAraNatvamityatra Aha || mAteti || achetanaprakR^iterupAdAnatvashaktirapi bhagavadadhInetyuchyate || viShNubaleriteti || 4-6 ||
tvadvatsarvottamAntarasyapi pitR^itvAdyupapatteH kathaM kR^itsnasyetyAdyuktamityata uchyate  " matta " iti | tatra svavyatiriktamAtraM niShidhyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyA.aha || matta iti || nAtra svavyatiriktaniShedhaH, kintu matto.anyadvastu parataraM  na bhavati | kintvahameva parataraH | ataH  " ahaM kR^itsnasya " ityAdi yuktamevochyata iti bhAvaH | svAtiriktaniShedho.ayaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || yadyatra svAtiriktaniShedhastarhi paratarapadenaiva svAtiriktasyoktatvAdanyAditi vyarthaM syAt | anyaditi padasya svAtiriktArthatAbhyupagame cha parataramiti vyarthaM syAdityarthaH | yadi viShNureva paratarastarhi parAvarAdinA bhAvyam | tatkimityata uktArthe smR^itimAha || avarA iti || duHkhasambandhitvAnna paro, duHkhena samyagapIDitatvAchcha nAvaraH | ato madhyama ityarthaH | viShNuH paratarashchet kaH paratama ityata Aha || abhAvAditi || atra parataraparatamapadAbhyAM viShNureka evochyate | na tvasau paratama eva | parabhUtashrItattvasya paratamabhUtaviShmoshcha madhye paratarasyAnyasyAbhAvAt | nApi viShNuH paratara eva | paratamasyAnyasyAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | nanu jaDaprakR^iterapi nityanirduHkhatvAt kathaM shrIrekaiva paretyata Aha || yasyA iti || nirduHkhatve.api duHkhakAraNatvena jaDaprakR^iterasandigdhamavaratvamevetyarthaH | 
yaduktaM jIvA avarA iti tasyApavAdamAha || atheti || atrApi taraptamapAvekArthau | nanvachetanAdapi chetanasyottamatvAt IshvaravimukhAnAmavarataratve kathaM prakR^iteravaratvamityata Aha || na hIti || jIvAnAM duHkhasambandha uktastarhi mokShaH kathaM syAdityata Aha || ata iti || uktaprakAreNetyarthaH | nanu bhagavajj~nAnena duHkhamokSho bhavati chet muktasya paratvaM syAt | tathA cha shrIrekaiva paretyayuktamityata Aha || mukta iti || sunityasukhabhojanAdavaratvAbhAve.api prAk duHkhAbhAvasAmye.api na sukhAdAvapi sAmyamityAha || tatrApIti || nanu shrutyAdau j~nAnavij~nAnAbhyAM mokShokteH kathaM viShNoH parataratvaj~nAnena mokSho.abhihita ityata Aha || viShmoriti || uchyate shrutyAhAviti sheShaH | evaM shryAdInAM paratvAdij~nAnena | anena  " j~nAnaM te.ahaM savij~nAnam " ityasyApyartha ukto bhavati | j~nAnavij~nAnayordaulabhyaM lipsotpAdanAyA.aha || etachcheti || muktAnAM tAratamye vA.anena heturuchyate | anena manuShyANAmityetadapi vyAkhyAtaM bhavati || 7 ||
viShNutantratvAt sarvasyAsau paratara iti tadadhInatvapradarshanenAha || sa iti || anena vij~nAnapradarshakaM raso.ahamityAdi vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | rasayati rasamAdatte rasaM prerayati | prabhAsanAt svayaM prabhAsamAnatvAt, prabhApreraNAchcha | praNauti stauti stAvakatvaM prerayati cha | shabdayati vakti shabdaM prerayati cha || 8 ||
surabhyasurabhitayA gandhaM prerayati, svayaM surabhishcheti puNyagandhaH | svayaM puNyagandhapradatvAchcha | tejasvI vartate, tejaH prerayati cheti tejaH | jIvanapradaH tasmAjjIvanam | tapayati tapaH kurute prerayati cheti tapaH || 9 ||
vyaJNjanAd vyaJNjakatvAt prerakatvAchcha | bodhanAt boddhR^itvad buddhiprerakatvAchcha || 10 ||
viShayabhoganirapekShatayA nityapUrNabasatvAt kAmavarjitaM balam | asthAne.aprayujyamAnatvAd rAgavivarjitaM lasam | rAgiNo 
hyasthAne.api balaM prayuJNjate | kAmarAgavivarjitabaladashchati vA | arthAntaramuchyate || etAdR^isheti || etAdR^ishabalAtmetyanuvAdaH | arthAntaraM chochyate || veti || tadgateH pUrNaratitvAt | atrApi kAmarAgarAhityaM pUrvavat | dharmAviruddhechChAprerakatvAchcheti j~nAtavyam | apsu rasa ityAdivyAvasthayA.abAdisarveShAM rasAdisarvado.ato rasAdinAmetyarthaH | rasAdyabhedAttannAmA kiM na syAdityata Aha || sarvata iti || tatra svAtantryaM hetuH | rasAderasvAtantryaM prasiddhamiti bhAvaH || 11 ||
na kevalaM rasAdidharmaprerakaH kiMnAmA.abAdiprerakashchetyAha || ye cheti || yathA bhagavadadhInamidamevaM bhagavAnetadadhInostu, bhUbhUdharAdivadityata Aha || tadAyattamiti || idameva tadAyattaM na tvasAvetadAyatta iti bhAvaH | anena  " na tvahaM teShu te mayi " ityasya vailomyenArtha ukto bhavati || 12 ||
evaM sarvaprerakaH paramAtmA kuto lokena na j~nAyata ityata Aha || achetanayoti || prakR^ityeti sheShaH || tanmeyatvAditi || viShNunaiva samyak j~nAtatvAt | lakShymA chetyarthaH | anena tribhirityAderartha ukto bhavati | mametyasyArtho vashagayeti | viShNunaivetyanenAchetanaprakR^ityAdyAhitaM svaviShayamohaM bhagavAn kuto na bArayatItyAshaN^.h्kAnivArakasya nAhaM prakAsha ityasyArtha ukto bhavati | yadi sAkShAdbhagavatyA loko mohitastarhi na kasyApi j~nAnamityata Aha || ye tviti || anena mAmevetyetadvyAShyAtaM bhavati | bhagavatprapattyA kathaM mAyAtaraNamityata Aha || lakShmIriti || nanu pUrvaM lakShmyA eva bhagavadvashatvasyoktatvAt kathaM te ubhe api viShNorvashe uchyate ityata uktam || lakShmIH sA jaDamAyA yA devateti || lakShmyA bhagavadvashatvaM bhavati | achetanaprakR^iterlakShmIvashatvAt | ato mohakaprakR^ityorbhagavadvashatvAt tatprapattyA mAyAtaraNaM yuktamevAtastaM prapadyetetyarthaH | anena guNamayItyetad vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tato.ananyabhaktyetyanenaikabhaktirityAdeH tAtparyamuktaM bhavati | ananyabhaktirnAma kIdR^ishItyata 
Aha || yAdR^ishIti || tatra bhaktiviShaye | anenaikasmin bhaktiryasyeti vigrahaH sUchitaH | tena sAmAnAdhikaraNyAN^gIkAre bhaktishabdasya priyAditvena puMvadbhAvAprAptishcha parihR^itA |
viShNoH sarvottamatvamanyeShAM tadvashatvaM cha j~nAtvA bhaktiM kurvatAM kiM phalamityata Aha || evamiti || evaM jAnanniti || j~nAtvA bhajannityarthaH | anena  " j~nAnI tvAtmaiva me matam " ityAdyuktArthaM bhavati | avadhAraNArthatushabdasyArtho nAnyatheti | bhagavajj~nAninAmeva mokSho nAnyeShAmiti kuta ityata Aha || pUrNamiti || bhagavata eva purNatvena mokShadAnashaktirnAnyeShAmityarthaH | anena vAsudeva ityasyartha ukto bhavati | yadi bhagavajj~nAnena mokShastarhi sarveShAM syAdityata Aha || evaMvIditi || vAsudevaj~nAnena mokShasadbhAve.api tajj~nAnino na sarva iti na sarveShAM mokSha ityarthaH | etena sa iti vyAkR^itaM bhavati | loke bhagavajj~nAninAM bahUnAM dR^ishyamAnatvAt kathaM daurlabhyamityata Aha || yaditi || mishrayAjina iti || vaiparItyena yajanta ityarthaH | etena kAmairityAdestAtparyamuktaM bhavati | kiM teShAM phalamityata Aha || viShNumiti || tatparaM ramAdibhyaH param | aj~nAtvA viparItaM j~nAtvA cha | kAraNavisheShAjj~nAnarahitasya viparItaj~nAnAbhAvenAnyadevatArAdhanena kiM syAdityata Aha || aj~nAnAmiti || upalakShaNaM chaitat | nirNetrabhAvAdikAraNAntaraM cha draShTavyam | samarchanaM kartavyamitIti sheShaH | pR^ithak sevA parivAratAM vinaiva anyadevatAyajanaM vidyAdi tadviShayaj~nAnaM stavanAdi chetyarthaH | etachcha phalaM nAj~nAnimAtrasya, api tu j~nAnAnantaraM yaH pUrvamArgaM tyaktvA bhagavadbhajanameva kuryAttasyaiva | keShAJNchittamoyogyAnAmapi kadAchidaj~natvasambhavAditi bhAvenAha || yadIti || idaM cha tamoyogyavyAvR^ittimAtram | nityatraividyAnAmapi phalasadbhAvAt | prAjInAparAdhasadbhAvAt kathamuttarApekShayA phalamityata Aha || ajAnateti | svato bhagavata eva yadi viShNutattvaM j~nAtvA.api kAraNavisheShAt pUrvamArgaM na jahAti tasya kiM syAdityata Aha || atyAga iti || j~nApayati tyaktumiti sheShaH | janmAntara ityupalakShaNam | yadi svIya iti sambandhaH | kechana gurvAdikaM nimittIkR^itya, na tu sAkShAt | anena labhate chetyAderviShaya ukto bhavati | evaM rasAdikAraNatvAdgasAdinAmakatvaM viShNornAbhedeneti pramANavachanenoktam | upakramopasaMhArayoH sarvasya bhagavadadhInatvokteshcha tajj~nAyata ityAha || matta eveti || j~nAnI tvAtmaiva me matam " ityetat  " evaM jAnaMstamApnoti " iti pramANavachanena vyAkhyAtam | yuktyA cha taduktArthameva na tvabhedArthamiti sAdhayitumAha || ApnotIti || AtmashabdasyAptivAchitvaM kuta ityata Aha || yachcheti ||  " yachchApnoti yadAdatte yachchAtti viShayAniha | yachchAsya santato bhAvastasmAdAtmeti bhaNyate || " iti bhAratavAkyam | kuto.ayamAtmashabda AptyarthaH, svarUpArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || Asthita iti || etadarthavivaraNAtmake vAkyasheShe paramAM gatimuddishyabhagavantamupAsInasya j~nAninastatprApteruktatvAt atrApi prApyarthaM evA.atma shabdo na svarUpArtha ityarthaH | nanu j~nAnAnantaraM mokShasya karmakShayamAtrAvadhitvAd  " bahUnAM janmanAm " iti bahujanmaniyatiH kathamuchyata ityata Aha || bahUnAmiti || vAsudeva ityetat pUrNaM vastviti pramANavachanena vyAkhyAtam | yuktyA chaitamarthaM sAdhayitumAha || vAsudeva iti 
|| atra vAsudevasya pUrNatvamevochyate, na tu sarvAbheda ityarthaH | pramANavachanena bhagavajj~nAninAmevAnuttamagatirbhavatItyatra hetvabhidhAyakatayaiva etadyojitam | atha bahUnAM DanmanAmante vAsudevaH sarvamiti j~nAnavAn bhavatItyapi yojanAM sUchayati || jAnanniti || abhedArthamevedaM vAkyaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || prapadyanta iti ||  " devAn devayajo yAnti " ityetad  " viShNuM tatparamaj~nAtvA " ityAdinA vivR^itam || 21-22 ||
vAkyAntareNApi vivR^iNoti || j~nAtveti || kimaj~nAnamAtreNa tama iti, netyAha || tathApIti || yadyapyevamuchyate tathApItyarthaH | tAvaditi saMyojyam | kechana bhAgavatAH puruShAH | kechana traividyAH santi | teShAM cha mokShAdikaM phalamityuktam || 23 ||
atha kechana dveShiNo.api santItyuchyate  " avyaktam " iti || tadarthaM pUrvavadeShAM phalasyAnuktatvAt phalaM cha smR^ityaivAha || anyakta iti || evaM sarvaprerakatvAdimahimavAMshchadbhagavAn tatkathaM bhagavataH kechijjIvAbhedaM manyanta ityato vaitaduchyate | sarvAtmanA j~neyatvAj~neyatvAbhyAM jIveshvarayorvyaktAvyaktatvam || 24-25 ||
yadi mAyAvashAdaj~nAnaM lakasya bhagavadviShayaM tarhi bhavato.api lokaviShayaM tadasti kiM, kuDyobhayabhAgAvasthitayoranyonyAdarshanavadityata uchyate || vedAhamiti || tatra kasyApi bhagavajj~nAnAbhAve rvedAdivaiyyarthyApatteH kathaM  " mAM tu veda na kashchana " ityuchyata ityatastatsmR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || yatheti || 26 ||
yatkeShAJNchidadvaitaj~nAnaM tadapi madichChayetyuktaM nAhaM prakAsha iti | tadayuktam |  " aikAtmyaM nAma yadidaM kechid brUyuranaipuNAH | kAmakrodhAbhibhUtatvAdahaMkArayashaM gatAH || " ityAdAvichChAdveShAderevAdvaitaj~nAnahetutvokterityata uchyate || ichCheti || tatra mohasaMmohashabdayorarthabhedapradarshanAya dvandvamohapadamanUdya mohashabdArthamAha || dvandveti || mohashabdasya mithyAj~nAnavAchitvaM kuta ityata Aha || tama iti || sharvarIsaMbandhitamovadAvarakamaj~nAnamityarthaH | astu moho mithyAj~nAnaM, dvandvamoho nAma ka ityata Aha || jIveti || Adipadena sarvaj~natvAlpaj~natvAditaddharmagrahaNam | mohashahdAgatArthatayA saMmohashabdaM vyAchaShTe || saMmoha iti || tadAgraho 
mithyAj~nAnadArDhyamityarthaH | kuto.ayaM saMmohashabdartha ityata Aha || tadagraha iti ||  " mohashchaiva viparyayaH " iti prakR^itaviparyayaH taditi parAmR^ishyate | krodho yathArthaj~nAniShu | uktashaN^.hkAparihArAyoktaM sargapadaM tadAshaMkAparihArakaM yathA syAttathA vyAchaShTe || sarga iti || satyamichChAdveShAdinA mithyAj~nAnaM bhavatIti || tathApi tadavAntarakAraNameva | sargakAlamArabhyaiva tasya kAraNatvAt | sharIrAnutpattAvichChAdyabhAvAt | viShNostu sarvadA kAraNatvAduktaM yuktamiti bhAvaH | nanvatra jIveshvarAdi viShayadvandvamohasyechChAdyavAntarakAraNatvamuchyate | na tu jIveshvarAbhedaj~nAnasya | na hi visheShyaikyaj~nAnameva dvandvamoha iti niyAmakamastItyata Aha || jIveti || 27 ||
bhagavajj~nAnena kiM bhavatItyata uchyate-jareti | tatra bhagavatA tadbrahmetyukte.api na brahmaNo bhagavataH sakAshAdanyatvaM shaN^.hkanIyam | tadAshaN^.hkAparihArAyaiva sAdhibhUtAdhidaivaM brahmeti vaktavye mAmityuktatvAditi bhAvenAha || taditi || ityukte jAtAmiti sheShaH || 30 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpAkAyAM saptamo.adhyAyaH || 7 ||
pUrvAdhyAyasaN^gatatvenaitadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayiti || ukteti || yaduktaM"te brahma tadviduH" ityAdi tadvyAkhyAnamatrAdau kriyate || "prayANakAle.api cha mAm" ityuktavyAkhyAnaprasaN^gena antakAlasmaraNaphalaM, tadupAyaprakAro, brahmaprAptimArgashchetyetaduchyata ityarthaH | antakAlasmaraNAdInAM brahma prApyate ebhiriti brahmaprAptishabdAbhidheyatvaM j~nAtavyam |
nanvarjunasya j~nAnitvAjjAnAtyevAsau bhagavAneva brahmeti | ataH "kiM tadbrahma" it prashnaH kathaM yujyate, kAraNAbhAvAdityata Aha || taditi || arjunasya j~nAnitve.api yukto.ayaM prashnaH | tadbrahmetyatra brahmaNo bhagavatA taditi pArokShyeNoktatvAd bhagavato.anyadevatA.a.atroktaM brahmeti pratIyate | vAsudevAtmakaM brahmetyAderbhagavAn brahmeti pratIyate | evamubhayathApratItijanitasaMshayasya prashnakAraNasya sadbhAvAditi bhAvaH | nanu brahmashabdasya bhagavanmAtravR^ittitvAt kathaM taditi visheShitatve.apyanyatvapratItirityata uktam || prakR^itIti || brahmashabdasya bhagavati mukhyatve.api prakR^itivedAderapyamukhyatayA tadarthatvAttaditi visheShitatvena mukhyArthAsambhave.apyamukhyArthaH prakR^ityAdInAM madhye yatkiJNchidatra syAditi pratItiryukteti bhAvaH | nanu taditi visheShaNena prAptA visheShaNena prAptA brahmaNo bhagavadanyatvashaMkA "sAdhibhUtAdhidaivaM mAm" ityuparitanavAkye bhagavataiva parihR^itA | brahmeti vaktavye mAmityuktatvAt | ataH kathaM brahmaNo bhagavadanyatvapratItirityata uktam || uparIti || yadyapyeShA pratItiruparitanavAkye parihR^itA, tathApi punarbhavatyeva | tatra "sAdhiyaj~naM cha" chashabdasya sAdhibhUtAdhiyaj~naM mAM cheti 
saMyojanenAdhibhUtAdisahitatvena brahmaj~nAnAdanyadeva viShNuj~nAnamuchyata iti taditi visheShaNAdeva pratItisambhavAditi bhAvaH | yatkiJNchidityatra anyadevetyatra cha iti pratItyA jAta iti sheShaH |
nanu "sAdhibhUtAdhidaivaM mAm" iti bhagavata eva brahmatvokteH kiM tadbrahmeti prashne.ahaM brahmeti parihAro baktavyaH | "akSharaM brahma paramam" iti kathamuchyata ityata Aha || parameti || tathaiva paramAkSharaM brahmetyeva | bhavatu paramAkSharaM brahmetyuktiphalaM, paramAkSharashabdasya viShNau prasiddhatvAt | tathApyahamiti sAkShAdanuktvA evaM kathane ko heturityata Aha || aj~nAnAmiti || tadapi svasya paramAkSharatvamapi | nanu ye paramAkSharaM viShNuriti na jAnanti teShAmahaM brahmeti noktam | akSharaM brahmetyevoktam | ato brahma akSharaM cha bhagavato.anyadevetyAshaMkaiva syAnna tu paramAkSharaM brahma cha bhagavAniti j~nAnamityata Aha || punariti || satyameva shaMkA bhavatIti | sA cha "avyakto.akShara ityuktaH" ityuparyakSharasyAvyaktatvoktyA parihriyate | "avyaktaM vyaktimApannaM manyante mAm" ityavyaktashabdasya bhagavati prayuktatvAt | ataH "akSharaM brahma paramam" iti parihAre ahamityuktAdapi lAbhasambhavAt tathA parihAro yukta iti bhAvaH |
yadyakSharashabhdo viShNAvena mukhyastarhi "ye chApyakSharamavyaktam" ityatra, "kUTastho.akShara uchyate" ityatra cha akSharashabdavAchyo viShNuH syAdityata Aha || ye cheti || akSharashabdasya viShNau mukhyatve.api "ye chApyakSharamavyaktam" ityatra tAvadviShNoranyadeva akSharashabdavAchyamityevAvasIyate | "ye bhaktAstvaM paryupAsate", "ye chApyakSharam" iti bhagavadakSharayoH pR^ithaktvena tadapAsakayostAratamyasya pR^iShTatvAt | ye tvakSharamanirdeshyam", "ye tu sarvANi karmANi" ityAdinA.akSharopAsakAnAM bhagavadupAsakAnAM cha phalatAratamyasya kathanAchcha | tathA "kUTastho.akShara uchyate" ityatrApi viShNoritadevAkSharamityavasIyate" | "ahamakShararAdapi chottamaH" iti viShNorakSharAduttamatvakathanAt mukhyArthAsambhave gauNAN^gIkArasyanyAyyatvAt | prakR^ite tu bAdhakAbhAvAdviShmuvaShayatvameveti bhAvaH |
nanvadhiyaj~nabrahmaNo.api viShNutve tatra brahmAhamevetyanuktvA adhiyaj~no.ahameveti kimarthamuchyate | kAraNavisheShamantareNoktibhedAsaMbhavAt | ato.adhiyaj~na eva viShNurna brahmetyata Aha || adhiyaj~na iti || brahmAdhiyaj~nayorubhayorviShNutve.api brahmAhamevetyanuktvA.adhiyaj~no.ahameveti kathanaM yujyate | "sAdhiyaj~naM mAm" iti bhagavatA svasyAdhiyaj~nasAhityenoktatvAt adhiyaj~no 
bhagavato bhinna evetyAshaMkA prAptA | tannivR^ittyArthatvAdahamevetyukteH | tadityuktyA brahmaNo bhagavadanyatvashaMkAprAptAvapi mAmityanena tasyAH prAj~nabuddhimapekShya nirastatvena trAhamevetyuktyabhAvAditi bhAvaH | etena "evaM bahuvidhA yaj~nA vitatA brahmaNo mukhe" ityuktatvAdadhiyaj~naprashnaparihArau prAptishUnyAviti cha nirastaM bhavati | bhagavAnevAdhiyaj~nashchet kathaM tatsAhityaM prAguktamityata Aha || tasyaiveti || bhagavata evAdhiyaj~natve.api tatsAhityaM yujyate | adhiyaj~nasya sarvaprANidehagatarUpAntaratvAditi bhAvaH | anena deha ityasyAbhiprAyo varNito bhavati |
atra pramANaM darshayan bhagavata eva brahmatve kathaM tadityuktirityAshaMkAM cha piraharan shlokadvayaM smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || prANinAmiti || brahmaNaH sarvagatarUpAntaratvAt tadityuktiryukteti bhAvaH | taistaiH sarvaprANibhiradhikayAjyatvAdadhiyaj~no, bR^iMhitatvAt brahmetyarthaH | bhUtAdhikatvata ityatra bhUtapadena pR^ithivyAdIni | puruprANA.ataH puruShAkhyeti sheShaH | "ShakAraH prANa AtmA" iti shruteH | nanu "adhiyaj~naH kathaM ko.atra" ityatra kuto.adhiyaj~naH kathaMpUpa iti prashnaH kasmAnna parihR^ita ityata Aha || kathaMrUpa iti || tallakShaNoktyeti || "kaviM purANam" iti bhagavallakShaNokyetyarthaH | bhagavallakShaNoktyA kathamadhiyaj~nasvarUpaprashnaH parihR^ita ityata uktam || ahameveti || "adhiyaj~no.ahameva" ityadhiyaj~nasya bhagavadabhinnatvenoktatvAdityarthaH || 4 ||
prayANakAle cha kathaM j~neyo.asItyasya kimarthaM kathambhUtaH kena prakAreNa smartavyo.asItyarthaH | tatra kimarthaM smartavyo.asItyasya parihAra uchyate "anteti" | tatra madbhAvapadasya anyathApratItinirAsAyArthamAha || madbhAvamiti || anyathA taM tamevaitIti vAkyasheShavirodha iti bhAvaH | nanvantakAle smaraNAdeva tatprApteH sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvaM kimarthamuchyata ityata Aha || sadeti || na tatprAptyarthaM sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvamuchyate | kintu smaran tyajatItyuktaM sAkShAdantakAlasmaraNaM sadA tadbhAvabhAvitAnAmeva bhavatIti sAkShAdantakAlasmaraNopAya evochyata iti bhAvaH | nanu antakAla eva mahatA prayatnena bhagavatsmaraNasya kartuM shakyatvAt kiM sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvenetyata Aha || na chediti || sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvAbhAve mahatA prayatnena smarato.apyanyaviShaya eva prArabdhakarmavashAt smR^itirbhavati | tatashcha tatprAptireva bhavati | yathA khalu mahatA prayatnena samAdhiM kurvato.api prArabdhakarmavashAt tataH skhalanaM bhavati | ataH sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvena bhAvyamiti bhAvaH | yadi prArabdhakarmavashAdantakAle brahmasmR^itirna bhavet tarhi j~nAninAmapi prArabdhakarmabhAvAdantakAle brahmasmR^ityabhAvena mokShAbhAvaH prasajyata 
ityata Aha || aparokSheti || aparokShaj~nAninAM smaran tyajatItyuktaM sAkShAdantakAlasmaraNaM bhavutyevAto nAmokShaH | tasyAprArabdhapUrvottarakarmanAshAshleShasadbhAvAt prArabdhakarmaNAM parimitatvena bhogenAvasAnasambhavAditi bhAvaH |
evaM vyAkhyAne bhagavadvAkyasammtimAha || prayANeti || nanvevaM sati antakAlasmaraNasya prArabdhakarmAvasAnameva kAraNaM, tatkAraNatayA.aparokShaj~nAnaM cheti prAptam | tathAcha kiM sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvenetyata Aha || yukteti || satyaM sAkShAdantakAlasmaraNasya prArabdhakarmAvasAnameva kAraNam | katkAraNatvAdaparokShaj~nAnaM cheti | tathApi sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvaM cha antakAlasmaraNakAraNaM bhavatyeva | aparokShaj~nAnasAdhanatvAt | sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvasyAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanatvena yuktachetasa ityuktatvAditi bhAvaH | anena yuktachetaso mAmAshritya yatanti ye te tadbrahma viduriti yojanA sUchyate | yannityasmaraNaM bhagavadaparokShaj~nAnasAdhanamuktaM tadbhaktyAdiyuktameva tathA | na svayameveti smR^ityA.a.aha || bhaktyeti || 5 ||

kena prakAreNa smartavyo.asItyasya parihAra uchyate  " yadakSharam " iti | tatra pUrvamantakAlasmaraNasya sadA tadbhAvabhAvitatvaM sAdhanamuktvA brahmacharye tathA kathamuchyata ityato brahmacharyapadaM tatparatayA vyAchaShTe || mana AdInAmiti ||  " tatte padaM saN^graheNa pravakShye " ityatra tatsmaraNaprakAraM pravakShya ityarthaH || 11 ||

brahmAdIn prAptAnAmapi punarjanmAbhAvAt kiM vishiShyAbhidhIyate mAmupetya punarjanma nAmuvantIti | ata uchyate  " AbrA्meti " | tatrA.ajanAnnajanirbhuvIti vachanAt janalokAdisthitAnAmapi janmAdyabhAvAt kathaM brahmabhavanamArabhya punarAvR^ittiruchyata ityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || niyamIditi || atra janmapadaM maraNasyApyupalakShakam || aMsalayAviti || aMshena bhUmau jananaM, layAnte cha jananaM, tadAdau maraNaM chetyarthaH | aMshasya maraNaM chAstItyAha || tatrApIti || aMshato.avatIrNatve.api naitadayuktam | muktasyaiva mukhyatayA jananAdyabhAvAt janAdAvalpajananAdibhAvAdetadvAkyasya cha tadarthatvAdityuktaM bhavati || 16 ||

brahmaNo dinamuchyate " ityAdau yugasahasramatrasya viriJNchadinAditvenoktatvAt kathaM sahasrapadaM tato.api bahvarthamityata Aha || brahmaNa iti || nAtra chaturmukhasyAhorAtramuchyate, yena sahasrapadaM tato.api bahvarthaM na syAt | kintu parabrahmaNo dvirarArdhAtmakamahorAtramiti bhAvaH | kuto brahmapadena parabrahmetyaN^gIkR^itya tadahorAtraparatvamuchyate, viriJNchAhorAtraparatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || avyaktAditi || evaM vAkyasheShasadbAve.api kuto nAsya viriJNchAhorAtraparatvamityata Aha || na hIti || AhanIti || tadavasAna ityarthaH | evaM na aharAgame sarvavyaktiprabhava ityapi draShTavyam | nanu kathaM bhagavato.ahorAtrasadbhAvaH | kAlakR^itavikArAbhAvAt |  " paranAmanimeShakAnte " ityAdau dviparardhakAlasya nimeShatvenoktatvAchchetyAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || nityasyeti || nirvikArasyetyarthaH | upachAre bIjamapravR^ittyeti | rAtrAviva pralayakAle pravR^ittyAbhAvAdanhIvAnyadA pravR^ittisadbhAvAt pralayAdikAlo rAtryAditvenopacharyata ityarthaH || 17-22 ||
bhagavantaM prAptAnAmapunarAvR^ittiH, anyeShAM punarAvR^ittirityuktam | tatra punarAvR^ittimatAmanyeShAM cha kena pathA़.a.agamanamityata uchyate  " yatra " iti | yatra yanmin kAle mR^itA anAvR^ittiM gachChanti, yasmiMshcha punarAvR^ittiM gachChanti, yasmaMshcha punarAvR^ittiM gachChanti taM kAlaM vakShyAmItyanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || yatreti || nanvagnijyotirdhUmAnAm akAlAbhimAninAmapi mArge mamyatvena vakShyamANatvAt kathaM pratij~nAvAkye yatra kAle taM kAlamityuchyata ityata Aha || agnIti || agnijyotirdhUmAnAM gamyatayA vakShyamANAnAmiti sheShaH | gamyatayA vakShyamANeShu kAlAbhimAninAM bAhulyAt alpasalilayutapayasI payaHpadasya salilopalakShakatvavat kAlapadasyetaropalakShakatvAditi bhAvaH |
nanu  " te.archiShamabhisambhavanti " ,  " archirAdinA tatprathiteH " ityAdau jyotiShaH prathamaprApyatayoktatvAt kathamatra joyatiShaH prathamamagneH prAptiruchyate | kutashchAharAdipadasya devatAviShayatvamityAshaMkAM smR^ityaiva pariharati || agniriti || evaM smR^itisamAkhyAnAdukta evArtho nAharAdikAle mR^itAnAmapunarAvR^ittyAdiriti samarthitam | vipakShe bAdhakaM chAha || tatkAleti || 
yadyatrAharAdikAlamaraNe apunarAvR^ittyAdi syAditi vivakShA bhavettarhi agnijyotirdhUmakathanasyAhaN^gatiH syAt | na hyaharAdAviva agnichyotirdhUmoShu maraNaM nAmAstIti bhAvaH | itashcha na pratIto.artha ityAha || atheti ||  " ya evaM vidvAnudagayane pramIyate devAnAmeva mahimAnaM gatvA.a.adityasya sAyujyaM gachChatyatha yo dakShiNe pramIyate " iti shrutAvuttarAyame kR^itasya j~nAnino.apunarAvR^ittyA brahmaprAptiM, dakShiNAyane mR^itasya karmiNaH punarAvR^ittyA chandraprAptiM choktvA punarj~nAnina uttarAyaNe dakShiNAyane vA mR^itasyApunarAvR^ittyA brahmaprAptiruchyate | ata uttarAyaNe mR^itAnAM punarAvR^ittirdakShiNAyane mR^itAnAM punarAvR^ittiriti niyamAbhAvAnnAnyo.artha iti bhAvaH | 
mahimAnaM pUjAm | maha pUjAyAmiti dhAtaH |  " AdityAchchandramasam " iti shruteH brahmamArge.api sUryAchandramasoH vidyamAnatvAt sUryAchandramasoH mahimAnamApnotIti yuktam | atra j~nAnina uttarAyaNe mR^itasya brahmaprAptikathanaM phalAdhikyAbhiprAyamiti j~nAtavyam | atra smR^itiM chAha || vidvAniti |. yatra tatretyasyAharAdiShu vA rAtr.hyAdiShu vetyarthaH || 23-26 ||

eke tu shuddhasvarUpatvAdInAM nityAbhivyaktAnAmeva visheShANAM chaitanyaikyaM, na tu kartR^itvAdInAmiti manyante | nAn nirAkaroti || visheSheti || shuddhasvarUpatvAdInAmeva chaitanyaikyaM na tu kartR^itvAdInAmiti devaividhyaM kiM yatkiJNchiddhetubalena kalpyate tadvinA vA? nAdyaH | tadadarshanAt | na dvitAyaH | rakartR^itvAdInAmapyaikyopapattau vR^ithA dvaividhyakalpne kalpanAgauravaprasaN^gAt | aprAmANikapramANaviruddhakalpanaprasakteshcha | yadi kalpanAgauravAdidoShAnaN^gIkR^ityApi kartR^itvAdInAM bhinnatvamuchyate tarhi shuddhasvarUpatvAdayo.api visheShA bhinnA evetyatiprasaN^gaH syAt | parasya doShabhayAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | evaM chetane visheShAderatyantAbhedaH samarthitaH | tannyAyenAchetane.api yAvad.hdravyabhAvino visheShAdervisheShiNA.atyantAbhedo draShTavyaH |
ayAvad.hdravyabhAvivisheShasya yau bhedAbhedAvuktau tau samarthayati || naikatvamiti || ekatvaM nAnAtvaM cha nAstItyakte.anirvachanIyatvashaMkA syAt | tannirAsAya niyamAdityuktam | ata ekaikasyAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | anubhavAdantathA gatyabhAvAchcha naikatvam, nApi nAnAtvamiti sambandhaH | nanu chetane.api bhedAbhedasadbhAvena chetanAchetanayorekaprakAratvAt achetana iti kiM vishiShyAbhidhIyata ityata Aha |. eka iti || ahaM madabhinno ghaTAderbhinna iti chetane bhinnapratiyogikAveva bhedAbhedAvanubhUyete | achetane tvekapratiyogikAveva | ato na chetanAchetanayorekaprakAratetyarthaH | kathamachotane bhedAbhedAvanubhavasiddhAvityataH tantvAdyavayavebhyaH paTAdyavayavino bhedAbhedasadbhAve.anubhavakathanena tantvAdInAM paTatvAdivisheShairbhetAbhedasadbhAve.anubhavaH pradarshita eva bhavatIti manvAna Aha || ekamiti || tantUnAM paTarUpeNaikatvasya parasparaM bhedasya chAnubhavAderakaikatantoH paTena bhedAbhedAvanubhUyete | ekaikatantoH paTenAtyantAbhede.anyonyabhedAnubhavAyogAditi bhAvaH | gatyantarAbhAvaM chAha || tantubhya iti || yadyekaikatantoH paTo.atyantabhinnastarhyekaikatantubhyaH paTaH pR^ithag dR^ishyata | na chaitadasti | nApyekaikatantunA paTo.atyantAbhinnaH | yathAsvasaMsthAnavisheSheNAvasthitaikaikatantubhAve paTAbhAvAnupapatteriti bhAvaH | sarvAvayavasamudAyasya svayamabahutvAt tadbhAve.avayavyabhAvAbhAvAt saMsthAnavisheSheNAvasthitAnAmevAvayavatvAt avayavinA.atyantAbhedo draShTavyaH | yathA.a.atmagatAnAM kartR^itvAdivisheShANAM bahutve.apyekenA.atmanA.atyantAbhedaH tathA bahutvepi tantUnAM ekena paTenAtyantAbhedaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || na cheti || kimannoktasya vyabhichArashchochyate utAtmagatavisheShadR^iShTAntena jaDe.apyantAbhedasAdhanamAtram? nAdyaH | atra kartR^itvAdInAM bahutvAbhAvAt | vyavahAravisheShasya svanirvAhakavisheSheNaivopapatteruktatvAt | nApi dvitAyaH | kartA.ahaM bhoktA.ahamityekaikavisheShavishiShTasyAtmano bhedAnubhavenaikaikavisheShasyApi kevalAbhedAnubhavAt | ekaikasmiMshcha tantau paTapratyayAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | kimachetane paTAdAvantyAvayavinyeva avayavAvayavinorbhedAbhedAviti ? || tasmAditi || pUrvAparAdibhAgabhedena aMshAvagamAdaupAdhikAMshasya nirastatvAdityarthaH |

vastuni guNakriyAdInAmayAvad.hdravyabhAvivisheShANAM svasadbhAvadashAyAM bhedAbhedAveva yuktau | nIlaM phalamiti teShAM sAmAnAdhikaraNyena bhAvavyavahR^itarabhedasyAN^gIkAryatvAt | vastuni vidyamAne.api kadAchinna nIlaM phalamityabhAvavyavahR^iterbhedasyApyaN^gIkAryatvAt | atyantAbhede vastuni sati tadvinAshAsambhavAditi bhAvaH vinAshAnantaraM tu bheda eveti j~nAtavyaM, svayamasato.abhedAyogAt | nanu yathA chetane suptyAdAvavidyamAnAnAmapi balaj~nAnAdInAmatyantAbhedastathA atrApyatyantAbheda eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || chetana iti || supto.ayaM balavAnityAdivyavahArabalena suptyAdAvapi balAdInAM shaktirUpeNAvasthAnasiddheH | yukto.atyantAbhedo, na tu shyAmatAdInAm | teShAmatyantochChedAdityarthaH | shyAmatAdInAmapi shaktirUpeNAvasthAnaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || na cheti || manyAmahe nIsatvAdInAM shaktirUpeNAvasthAnaM yadi balAdInAmiva shaktirUpAbhiprAyeNa teShAM vyavahAro bhavet | na hi pIte chUtaphale nIlamiti vyavahAro.astIti bhAvaH |
yaduktaM visheShabalAdekaM pUpaM harerbahuvyavahAraviShayatAM yAtIti tadbhavedyadi rUpAbhedaH pramANAvasito bhavet |  " abhAvo yatra " ityuktatvAt | na cha tatpramANamupalabhyata ityata Aha || ekameveti || yaduktamachintyaishvaryayogato durghaDamapyetad ghaTata iti tadayuktam | tathAsati paramaishvaryabalena jIvAbhedAderapi ghaTanApAtAdityata Aha || parameti || yatkalyANaguNAtmakaM tatsarvaM pratItyA durghaTamapi harau paramaishvaryayogato ghaTata ityevAN^gIkriyate na tu jIvaikyAdikamapIti | tathA sati paramaishvaryasyaivAnupapatteriti bhAvaH || 1-14 ||
dR^iShTavishvarUpo dR^iShTAnuvAdavyAjena stauti   "pashyAmi " iti | tatra kamasarUpAsane sthitaM brahmANamityalpArthatvApratItinirAsAya kamalAsanasthapadaM vyAchaShTe || kamaleti || kathaM brahmaNo brahmaNi sthitatvamityato rudrasyeshapadoditasyedaM visheShamiti bhAvenAha || rudramiti || bhavedidaM vyAkhyAnaM yadi rudrasya brahmaNi sthitatvaM bhavet, tadeva kuta ityata Aha || viShNumiti || 15-18 | |  "dyAvApR^ithivyoH " ityatra tvayetyuktyaivekeneti siddhatvAt kimarthaM punarekenetyuchyata ityatastasya sArthakyamAha || dyAvApR^ithivyoriti ||  "anAdimadhyAntam " iti parimANAnantyamuchyata ityanyathApratIti sambhavAt kimarthamuchyate kimarthamuchyate prAyo bhItA ityata Aha || arjunAditi || etadvachanabalena lokatrayashabdasya tatra sthitavishvarUpadarshanayogyapratibandhakahInabhaktaviShayatvAt bhagavataH kiJNchidugratvAttaddarshanAM bhayasyApi sambhavAt  "dR^iShTvA.adbhutaM " ityAdivAkyamupapannamiti bhAvaH |  "pashyAmi devAMstava dehe " ityuktatvAt  "amI hi tvA surasaN^ghA " iti pArokShyeNa nirdiShTA muktAH | tatrAmuktA ityapaunuruktyamiti bhAvaH | bhavedapunaruktiryadyetat muktaviShayaM syAt | tadeva kutaH? parokShanirdeshasyAmukteShvapi sambhavAditi chenna |  "tvAM vishanti " iti svechChayaiva bhagavatpraveshokteriti bhAvenAha || vishaMtIti || tathApi kuto muktaviShayatvamasyetyata Aha || pravesha iti || 21-25 ||
nanu dhR^itarAShTraputrAdInAM bhagavanmukhapraveshonmukhacheShTA.abhAvAt kathaM  "amI cha tvA dhR^itarAShTrasya putrAH " ityAdyuchyata ityata Aha || anyati || bhagavanmukhapraveshAnunmukhacheShTAnAmapi bhagavanmukhacheShTayaiva tatra praveshAdupachAreNa vishantIti prayogo yujyate | pralayodakapraveshAnunmukhacheShTAnAM prajAnAM tachcheShTayaiva tatra praveshe  "praviShTA udakaM prajAH " iti prayogavadityarthaH | bhagavanmukhacheShTayaiva tatra praveshashchet dhArtarAShTrasenAyA eva bhavet | bhagavanmukhAnAM tadabhimukhatvAt | ataH  "sahAsmadIyaiH " ityayuktaM syAdityata Aha || seneti || nanu yuddhopakrama eva chUrNitottamAN^gatayA.anyairadR^iShTAH kathamarjunena mayA tathA sandR^ishyanta ityuchyate  "kechidbilagnAH " ityAdinetyata Aha || ye tviti || tanminneva muhUrte mariShyamANAnAmevAtra grahaNAd.h yuddhopakrama evaivamuktiryuktA | vishIrNatvenApatitasya sUkShmadR^iShTigocharatvAdanyeShAM tathA darshanaM cha yuktam |  "divyaM dadAmi te chakShuH " ityAderarjunasya divyadR^iShTitvAdanyAdR^iShTadarshanaM cha yuktamiti bhAvaH | anyeShAM tadadarshane dR^iShTAntamAha || yatheti || divyadR^iShTitvAdarjunasyAnyadR^iShTadarshane dR^iShTAntamAha || yatheti || etachcha viShNudharme vistareNoktam || 26-30 ||
 "AkhyAhi me ko bhavAn " ityatra ko devo bhavAniti pR^ichChatItyanyathApratItinirAsAyA.aha || visheSheti || guNAdeH svayamevoktatvAt kiM punaH prashnenetyato visheShetyuktam | svaj~nAtaviShaya ityarthaH | svarUpaviShaya eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || viShNuriti pUrvameva j~nAtatvAt visheShaguNakarmAdiviShaya evAyaM prashno na svarUpamAtraviShaya ityarthaH || 31 ||
parihAre guNAderanuktatvAt nAyaM tadviShaya ityataH kAlashabda eva guNAdivAchIti bhAvena smR^ityaiva taM vyAchaShTe || kAla iti || 
kalitAH svasambaddhAH | kala bandhane, kala saMharaNe, kala j~nAne, kala vidrAvaNa itadi paThanti | ugrarUpaH kimarthamiti prashnaparihArAyoktaM  "lokakShayakR^it " ityAdi | tadupapadyate  "R^ite.api " iti | tatra yudhiShThirAdInAmapyurvaritatvAt kathaM tvAmR^ite sarve mariShyantItyuchyata ityata Aha || apIti || nAtrArjunamekamR^ite sarve mariShyantItyuchyate | kintu arjunabhrAtR^inashvatthAmAdIMshcha vinA | apipadena teShAM samuchchitatvAditi bhAvaH | 32-33 ||

vAyuryamo.agnirityAdyarjunastutivAkye vAyvAdishabdAnAM bhagavati yogavR^ittiM smR^ityaiva darshayati || vAyurti || vabayorabhedAd vakAro balavAchI | ayapaya gatAviti dhAtoH Ayushabdo j~nAnavAchI | idi paramaishvarya iti dhAtuH ||39-41 ||
 "asatkR^ito.asi vihArashayyAsanabhojaneShu |eko.athavA.api " ityatra yadyapyahaM tvameka eva | tathApi lokavyavahArAnusAreNa kShAmaya ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || eka iti || tarhyanvayo nopapadyata ityatastaM darshayati || apIti || sarvottamatvenAsatkArAyogyo.apyasatkR^ito.asItyevochyate | nAnyat | arjunasya bhagavadaikye mAnAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | ekashabdaH kathaM sarvottamavAchItyata Aha ||eka iti || ekatvAd.h eH, karotIti ka ityarthaH | anyanirapekShatayA hi kartA sarvottamaH || 42-45 ||
 "tenaiva rUpeNa bhava " ityarjunaprarthanAvAkye vishvarUpaM vihAya pUrvatanaM gR^ihANetyuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || tenaiveti || yadA rUpAntaraM pratIyate tadA vishvarUpatyaga eva kiM na syAt, kiM tadgopanenetyata Aha || paJNchAnanamiti | narasiMharUpe.api gopitavishvarUpatvokterna rUpantarapratItau vishvarUpatyAga iti bhAvaH || 46 ||
bhaktyatishayotpAdasAya vishvarUpadarshanasya daurlabhyamuchyate  "mayA " iti | tatra  "tejomayaM vishvaM " iti vishvAtmakatvaM bhagavadrUpasyochyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAya vishvashabdaM smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || vishveti ||  "yanme tvadanyena na dR^iShTapUrvaM " ityarjunetarairvishvarUpasyAdR^iShTatvamuchyate ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || tvaditi || nAtra vishvarUpalasyArjunetarairadR^iShTatvamuchyate | pratyutetaH pUrvaM kenApi na dR^iShTamityanuktvA tvadanyenetyuktatvAt tainaivetaH pUrvam indrasharIreNa dR^iShTamityevochyate ityarthaH | tarhi brahmAdibhirapi na dR^iShTamityapi nAshaN^.hkanIyam | tvadanyenetyarjunAdadhamavivakShayoktatvAdityAha || tvaditi || naitAvat.arjunAdhamairna dR^iShTamiti kalpanIyam | adhamairapyarjunavanna dR^iShTamityabhiprAyeNaivAdR^iShTatvasyoktatvAdityAha || tairiti || bhavedevaitad vyAkhyAnaM yadi vishvarUpaM brahmAdibhirindreNArjunAdadhamaishcha dR^iShTaM, indreNa chArjunavadeva dR^iShTaM, arjunAdadhamaintadvanna dR^iShTamityetatsidhyet, tadeva kuta ityata Aha || vishvarUpamiti || indrasyAdhikadarshatve.alpadarshitve vA vishiShya tvayendrasharIreNa draShTamityuktirna nambhavati | Adhikye.anukterAdhamye niShedhasya chAdarshanAt || 47 ||
yadyanyeShAmapi vashvarUpadarshanamatrAbhipretaM syAttarhi  "na vedayaj~nAdhyayanairna dAnaiH " ityuttaravAkyavirodha ityata Aha || vedeti || nottaravAkye.arjunAdanyeShAM vishvarUpadarshanAbhAva uchyate | kintu tvadavaraistvadvanna dR^iShTamityukteH svatastathA darshanAbhAve.api vedAdisAdhanaistathA tairdR^ishyatAmityAshaMkya tvadavarairvedAdisAdhanairapi tvadvanna draShTuM shakyata ityevochyata iti bhAvaH | vishvarUpasyArjunAdanyenAdR^iShTatvamevArthaH kiM na syAditi chenna | udAhR^itasmR^itivirodhAt | atrApi "dR^iShTvA.adbhutaM pUpaM ",  "dR^iShTA lokAH " ityAdipUrvavAkyavirodhaH syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || 48-49 ||
 "svakaM rUpaM darshayAmAsa " iti kR^iShNarUpasya vishiShya svIyatvokteH yaduktaM vishvarUpasya sAkShAdIshvarasvarUpatvaM tadayuktamityata Aha || svavaditi || nAtra svakashabdena kR^iShNarUpasya svakIyatvamuchyate, yena vishvarUpasya svakIyatvaM na syAt | kintu svavat svakIyavat kriyate pradarshyata iti vyutpattyA svakIyatayA pradarshanIyatvamevetyarthaH | nanUbhayorapi bhagavadIyatayA pradarshyamAnatvAt kR^iShNarUpasyaiva kuto visheShoktirityata Aha || vishvarUpamiti || satyamubhayaM pUpaM bhagavadIyatayA pradarshyata, 
iti, kintu j~nAninAmeva | aj~nAninAM tu kR^iShNarUpameva bhagavadIyatayA pradarshyate | na tu vishvarUpamato.aj~navivakShayA visheShoktiryukteti bhAvaH | ata evAlpaj~nAnivivakShayA svavadityuktam | kimarthamevaM vyAkhyeyam? vishvarUpaM bhagavadIyameva kiM na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti ||
kR^iShNarUpavishvarUpayoH svakIyatvAsvakIyatvapratItinirAkaraNaprasaN^gena paramaM pUpaM darshayAmAseti vishvarUpasya paratyoktyA kR^iShNarUpasyAparatvaM smR^ityaiva nirAkaroti || pareti || anyathA svabhAvataH | tarhi vishvarUpa eva paratvaM viduShAmapi kathaM dR^ishyata ityata Aha || vyaktiriti || vishvarUpe  paratvavyAktirnAvatArarUpeShu || atastathA dR^iShTiryukteti bhAvaH | iyaM cha vyaktiralpaj~nAnivivakShayochyate | na tu brahmAdimahAj~nAnivivakShayaTA | teShAM kR^iShNAdAvapi paratvasya pratIterityAha || aj~neti || 50
