nanu  "dR^iShTvedaM mAnuShaM rUpaM " iti kR^iShNarUpasya mAnuShatvokteH kathaM nAvaratvamityata Aha || kiJNchiditi || anyathodAhR^itavAkyavirodhaH syAdityarthaH || 51 ||
nanu  "sudurdarshamidaM rUpaM " ityatra apyasya rUpasya nityaM darshanakAN^kShiNa eva vartante, na tu pashyantItyuktatvAt kathamarjunAduttamairadhamaishcha vishvarUpasya dR^iShTatvamuchyata ityatastadvAkyaM yathAvadyojayati || ya iti || anena yanmama rUpaM dR^iShTavAnasi, asya rUpasya nityaM darshanakAN^kShiNo ye devAste.api yaddR^iShTantastadidaM sudurdarshamiti yojanAsUchitA bhavati | anyathoktavirodha iti bhAvaH || 52 ||
iti shrImadAnandatirthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitayAM nyAyadIpikAyAM ekAdasho.adhyAyaH || 11 ||
|| atha dvAdasho.adhyAyaH ||
 OM|| etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || sAdhaneti || mokShasAdhanayoravyaktabhagavadupAsanayormadhye prAguktabhagavadupAsanasyAdhikyanirNayo.asmin adhyAye kriyata ityarthaH | nanu bhagadupAsanasyevAvyaktopAsanasyApi yadi mokShasAdhanatvaM kvachiduktaM syAttadA "evaM satatayuktAH" iti sandihya prashno yujyate | na cha tadastItyataH kathaM prashna ityata Aha || shriya iti || yaH puruShaH shrIsamArAdhanArthaM jAto.asau tadarthameva gR^ihAnnirgato bhavati sa shriyaM upadeShTrabhyo gurubhya eva svasya vayo dhatte | evaM shriyamupAsInAH puruShA amR^itatvaM yAnti | tasmin gurushiShyAkhye mithune samIhitAni satyAni bhavantItyarthaH | kiM shriya upAsanaM svAtantryeNaiva mokShasAdhanamityataH shrIprasAdamutpAdya tato bhagavatprasAdadvAreNaiveti bhAvena smR^itimAha || shrIriti || shrIprasAdasya bhagavatprasAdotpAdakatvaM kuta ityataH shriyo.atimAnamAha || avyaktamiti || evambhUtA chet shrIstarhi tatprasAdaH svayameva puruShArthahetuH kiM na syAt? IshvaraprasAdasAdhanatvaM tasya kimarthamuchyata ityata Aha || tasyA iti || shriyo.api viShNoH paramatvAnna tatprasAdasya svAtantryeNa puruShArthasAdhanatvaM, kintu viShNuprasAdatvenaivetyarthaH | viShNoH mahadbrahmabhUtashriya uttamatve hetumAha || ya iti || evaM shrutipurANavAkyebhyo viShNUpAsanasyevAvyaktopAsanasyApi mokShasAdhanamiti shaMkayottamasAdhanaM pR^ichChatItyarthaH |
yadi bhagavadupAsanasyeva shriya upAsanasyApi mokShasAdhanatvaM pratIyeta tarhi tadviShaya eva prashnaH kartavyaH | avyaktopAsanaviShaye kimarthaM kriyata ityata Aha || kUTastha iti || "kUTastho.akShara uchyate" ityuparitanavAkye chitprakR^itAveva prayuktakUTasthAkSharashabdayoratrApyavyakte prayuktatvenAvyaktaM chitprakR^itireva | ataH chitprakR^ityupAsanasya mokShasAdhanatvapratItyA.avyaktopAsanaviShaye prashno yukta eveti bhAvaH | etena "ityAdishrutibhyaH", "avyaktopAsanAt" ityasyApyanavadyatvaM sidhyati | nanvavyaktAdishabdAnAM parabrahmaNi mukhyatvAdatra tatkiM vivakShitaM na syAdityata Aha || anyatheti || yadyatrAvyaktashabdena parabrahmochyeta tarhi tvadupAsakAvyaktopAsakAnAM madhye ka uttama iti bhagavato.avyaktasya cha bhedenArjunaprashno.anupapannaH syAdityarthaH | kuto.anupapanna ityato.arjunenaiva bhagavataH parabrahmatvasyoktatvAdityAha || paramiti |
anye tvatrAvyaktapadena yatkiJNchichChUnyAparanAmakaM nirguNaM brahmochyata iti manvAnAH tadupAnakeshvaropAsakayoH ko.adhika iti prashnArthaM kalpayitvA.avyoktopAsakAnAmevAdhikyaM parihAre kathyata iti vadanti | tAn pratyAha || ye tviti || "te me yuktAtamA matAH" iti bhagavatA svopAsakanAmuttamatvamuktvA "mayyeva" iti madupAsakAnAmevottamatvAt madupAsaka eva bhaveti sphuTamuktatvAdavyaktopAsakAnAmAdhikyaM vadatAmapalApakatvameva | tatashcha sAhasikatvAt "aho naShTA ete" iti shokaviShayatvameva na tu parihAraM vaktaM prativAditvamityarthaH |
nanu cheShTAvatyAH shriyo.achalatvam "achalaM dhruvam" iti kathamuchyata ityataH smR^ityaiva tadghaTayati || neti || "anirdeshyamavyaktamachintyaM paryupAsate" iti vyAhatam | anirdeshyAvyaktAchintayasyopAsanAyogAdityataH anirdeshyatvAdikamupAsyatvAvirodhena smR^ityaiva ghaTayati || sUkShmatvAditi ||
madupAsakA evottamA ityuchyate "mayi'' iti | tvadupAsakAnAmivAvyaktopAsakAnAmapi mokShasadbhAvAt kathaM teShAmuttamatvamityato.avyaktopAsakAnAM mokShamaN^gIkR^itya sahetukaM svopAsakAnAmuttamatvamuchyate "ye tvakSharam' iti | tatrochyamAnabhagavatprAptiH na kevalashAkteyAnAmiti bhAvena mayItyAdikaM shrutyaiva vyAchaShTai || aviShNuj~nairiti || atra "dhyAyIta nityadA" ityantena parItyupasargAbhiprAya ukto bhavati | "tena tuShTA"ityanena "te prApnuvanti mAmeva" ityasyAbhiprAya ukto bhavati | evamavyaktopAsanasya mokShasAdhanatve.api na tadevottamaM mantavyamiti bhAvenAha || tathApIti || upAsate shriyA saheti sheShaH | anena "mayyAveshya" ityuktArthaM bhavati | avyaktopAsakAnAmapi mokShasadbhAve kathaM bhagavadupAsakAnAmuttamatvamityata Aha || yata iti || anena "kleshaH" iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | anena uktaprakAreNa paryupAsanam indriyagrAmAtiniyamanaM, sarvatra samabuddhitvaM, 
sarvabhUtahiteratvAdisuShTvAchAramantareNa avyaktaprasAdAbhAvAt paramashraddhAmAtrayuktAnAM suShTvAchArAderaunye.api bhagavatprasAdasambhavAt kleshAdhikayaM j~nAtavyam | itashcha bhagavadupAsanamevottamamityAha || viShNuneti || shriyA saha bhagavadupAsane dvayorapi paramaprasAdasambhavenAchirAt mokSho bhavati | pR^ithagavyaktopAsanapakShe tu kiJNchidbhagavadupAsanaM kR^itvA bahukAlaM pR^ithak shriyamupAsya punaH shriyA saha nirantaraM bhagavadupAsanaM kartavyam | tato muktiriti chireNaiva bhavatItyato.api bhagavadupAsanamevAdhikamiti bhAvaH | anena "ye tu sarvANi" ityetaduktArthaM bhavati | hetudvayenoktaM viShNUpAsanasyAdhikyamupasaMharati || tasmAditi || teShAmAdhikyaM cheti sheShaH ||
ye nityayuktAste yuktatamA ityayuktam | ekArthatvAdityata Aha || yukteti || nityuyuktapadaM nityodyuktArthamiti cha draShTavyam | nanu 'ye tu sarvANi'ityatrAnanyayogena bhagavadupasanasyottamatvamuchyate | ataH kathaM shriyA sahitabhagavadupAsanasya AdhikyakathanaparatayaitadvyAkhyAyata ityAshaMkAM pramANavAkyenaiva pariharati || viShNoriti || nAtrAnanyayogapadena anyopAsanasmbandho niShiddhyate | kintvanyasya bhagavadadhInatvaM tatparivAratvaM vinopAsanam | ato yuktaM prAjInavyAkhyAnamiti bhAvaH | nanu yadi bhagavadupAsakAnAmivAvyaktopAsakAnAmapi mokShashravaNAt tadupAsanaviShaye kimuttamamiti prashnaH kriyate tarhi 'j~nAtvA shivaM shAntimatyantameti', 'hariM haraM viraJNchaM cha j~nAtvA muchyeta saMsR^iteH' ityanyadevatopAsanasyApi mokShahetutvashravaNAt tadviShaye kimiti prashno na kriyata ityAshaMkAM siMhAvalokananyAyena pariharati || antavaditi || anyadevatopAsanAyA mokShasAdhanatvasya pUrvameva niShiddhatvena shrutyAdau taduktAvapi tasyAnyArthatvaM kalpayitvA.avyaktopAsanaviShaya eva prashnaH kR^ito nAnyadevatopAsanaviShaya iti bhAvaH | tarhi nAmAnyato bhagavadanyopAsanasya mokShasAdhanatvasya pUrvameva niShiddhatvenAvyaktopAsanasyApi tadabhAvaprAptestadvachanAnAmapyarthAntaram akalpayityA kimiti tadviShaye prashnaR^i kiyata ityata uktam || lakShmyA iti || sAmAnyato bhagavadanyopAsanasya mokShasAdhanatvamiShedhe.api lakShmyAH bhagavadatipriyatvenAnyebhyo visheShasadbhAvAt tadupAsanasya mokShasAdhanatvasambhavena niShdhasya tadatiriktopAsanaviShayatvaM kalpayitvA.arjunenAnyopAsanaviShayaprashnamakR^itvApyavyaktopAsanaviShaya eva prashnaH kR^ita iti bhAvaH |
madupAsanasyAdhikatvAttadeva kuru | tadalAbhe mAM jAnIhI | tadabhAve chAbhyAsayogena mAM jAnihI | tadabhAve cha matkarmaparo bhava | tadashaktau cha madyogamAshritaH karmaphalatyAgaM kurvityuchyate- 'mayi' iti | tatra matkarmakR^ittvameva madyogaH | ataH kathametadityataH smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || vAShNavAnIti || sarvakarmANi vaiShNavAni karotIti yojanA | viShNuviShayatayA karotItyarthaH | archAmArjanaM pratimAsnApanam | Adipadena dhyAnaM cha grAhyam | tadyogamAtravAn tatkarmatvopAyamAtravAn | anena madyogamiti matkarmatvayogamiti vyAkhyAtam | yadi bhagavatkarmatvaM kAmayate tarhyeva tadyogo bhavati | na tu kAmyenAnyopAsanAdinetyarthaH | anena 'sarvakarma' ityuktArthaM bhavati | bhagavadupAsane.api tAratamyamAha || asamyagiti || dhyAnAlAbhe j~nAnaM, tadalAbhe.abhyAsa ityetatsamarthyate-'shreyo hi' iti | tadanena vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | j~nAnapUrvadhyAne.api sakAmAnniShkAmamevAdhikamityAha || tasmAt || iti | tatra hetumAha || tasmAditi || anena 'dhyAnAt' ityetad vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | nanvatra tyAgAchChAntiH phalamuchyate | ataH kathamuchyate tasmAnmuktirityata Aha || shAntiriti || nanvatra karmaphalatyAgamAtrasyaiva dhyAnAdhikyamuchyata iti kiM neShyate? j~nAnapUrvaM dhyAnasAhityaM kimuchyate? ityato vA.a.aha || shAntiriti || atra tyAgasya shAntipadoditamuktihetutvamichyate | na cha tatkevalatyAgagrahaNe yuktam | 'saMnyAsastu mahAvAho duHkhamAptumayogataH' ityuktatvAt | j~nAnapUrvakadhyAnasahitatyAgasya 
tatsambhavAt sa evatra vivakShita iti bhAvaH || 4-15 ||
'ye tu sarvANi karmANi ityAdi prapaJNchyate-'adveShTA' iti | tatra 'sarvArambhaparityAgI' ityetadanyathApratItinirAsAya chaturdhA vyAchaShTe || avaiShNaveti || uktArthAnupapAdayati || sarveti || sarvakarmaphalatyAgamityanena sarvArambhaphalaparityAgena sarvArambhaparityAgItyuktaM siddhyati | mayItyanena sarvAmbhAbhimAnatyAgena sarvArambhANAM bhagavati samarpaNena cha sarvArambhaparityAgItyuktaM siddhyati | 'mayi' iti vAkyasya smR^ityaiva tathA vyAkhyAtatvAt | AdipadagR^ihItena 'sarvadharmAn parityajya' ityAdinA.avaiShNavArambhaparityAgena sarvArambhaparityAgItyuktaM siddhyati | tasya tathA sayuktikaM vyAkariShyamANatvAt | nanu 'sarvArambhaparityAgI' ityasya 'shubhAshubhaparityAgI' iti prapaJNchyamAnatvAt avaiShNavArambhapirityAgItyAdikaM kiM vishiShyAbhidhIyata ityatastatsmR^ityaiva uktAviruddhatayA vyAchaShTe || bhaktimiti || upalakShaNe chaitat | tatsAdhanatayA vaiShNavArambhAMshcheti j~nAtavyam | 'samaduHkhasukhaH', 'harShAmarShabhayodvegairmuktaH' ityetanniyamapratItinirAsAya smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || prAya iti || tathochyate sukhAdiShu samo harShAdivarjita uchyeta | evaM chedalpavaiShamyAdervidyamAnatvAt kathaM tadabhAvoktirityata Aha || yatheti || mukhyArtha eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || na hIti || nanu harShasya guNatvAt kathaM tatparityAgo.apekShitatayochyata ityato harShashabdasya heyArthatAM smR^ityaiva darshayati || hR^itiriti ||  manasa iti sheShaH | nanu 'adveShTA' ityAdAvadveShAdimatAM priyatvamAtramuktvA ' ye tu dharmyAmR^itam ' ityatra shraddhAdimatAmatipriyatvaM 
kiM nimittamuchyata ityata Aha || vyastenet ||  ' adveShTA ' ityAdau yat pR^ithak pR^ithak sAdhanamuktaM tattanmAtreNa priyatvamuktam |  ' ye tu ' ityatrAdveShTetyAdiprAguktasamastasAdhanenAtIvapriyatvam | vyastAt samastasyAdhikyAditi bhAvaH | nanu  ' adveShTA ' ityAdAvadveShAdisAdhanena priyatvamuchyate,  ' ye tu ' iti bhaktyA.atIva priyatvamuchyata iti kiM na syAta bhakteH sarvasAdhanottamatvAdityata Aha || bhaktiriti || adveShAdikathane.api bhakteruktatvAt nAyaM vibhAgo yukta iti bhAvaH |  ' yanmAnnodvijate lokaH ' iti vyastasAdhanakathane bhakteranuktatvAt kathaM bhaktistu vyasteShvayuktaivetyuchyata ityata Aha || yasmAditi || 17-19 ||
dharmyAmR^itapadasya durgamArthatvAdarthamAha || dharmeti || 20 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM dvAdasho.adhyAyaH || 12 ||
|| atha trayodasho.adhyAyaH ||
etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || sarveti || yat prathamaShaTke prAchuryeNa j~nAnasAdhanamuktaM, yachcha dvitIye bhagavatsvarUpaM nirUpitaM,  ' na tvevAhaM ' ityAdau yajjIvasvarUpaM pradarshataM,  ' bhUmirApo.anala ' ityadau yat kShetramabhihitaM tadviprakIrNatayoktaM sarvaM buddhyArohArthaM saN^kShipyAsminnadhyAye pradarshayatItyarthaH | sarveShAmadhyAyAnAmarthAn saN^kShipati saN^kShipya darshayatIti sarvArthasaN^kShepaH |
tatra  ' tat kShetraM yachcha ' iti pratij~nAtam | bhagavajj~nAnasyaiva mokShahetutvAt kShetraM bhagavatsvarUpaM chobhayaM kimarthamuchyata ityAshaMkA tAvatparihriyate  ' idaM ' iti | tatra  ' saN^ghAtashchetanA ' iti kShetravikAratvenoktasharIrasya kathaM samastakShetratvamuchyata ityAshaMkAparihArAya shrutyaitadvyAchaShTe || hiMseti || jIvasya svato nityatvAt dehAditayA pariNataitadupaghAtadeva chIvo hiMsita ityatuchyate | avyaktAdikaM hiMsAhetujIMvasya bhavati | shrR^i hiMsAyAmiti dhAtorhiMsAhetutvAt shar | pareNeryatvAdIramiti sharIramityarthaH | kShi nivAsagatyoriti dhAtoH | avyaktAdItyanena mahAbhUtAnItyasyArtha ukto bhavati | taddhikArAH kShetravikArAH | anena  ' ichChAdveSha ' ityuktArthaM bhavati | vikAritvaM cha na chidrUpechChAdInAmiti bhAvenAha | chidrUpeti || anena svayamachidrUpA iti labhyate | vartanta iti sheShaH | kimeteShAM sadA mishratayA.avasthAnamityataH saMsAra eva na sarvadeti bhAvenAha || vikAreti || muktau dveShaduHkhAbhAvAt kathaM chinmAtrechChAdisaMyuto muktaH syAdityata Aha || muktishcheti || AsurI daivI cheti sheShaH | tarhi daivamuktau dveShAdyayogAdAsuramuktau cha sukhAdyayogAdadhikaM saN^.hkaTamevetyataH pratyekamichChAdyasheShAsambhave.api vibhAgena tatsambhavAdavirodha iti bhAve.anAha || chinmAtreti || yatra syurutyuttaratrApi sambaddhyate | ichChAdiShvapaThitA.api viShNubhaktirdveShasya paThitatvena tatpratiyogitayA gR^ihyate |
 ' etadyo vetti ' ityetajjIvaviShayatayA pratItinirAsAya vachanAntareNa vyAchaShTe || kShetraj~na iti || yaH kShetraM jAnAti sa sarvo.api kShetraj~naH, ato viShNuriti kiM vishiShyochyata ityata Aha || na hIti || kimayaM svayaM kShetrAntarbhUtaH san tajjAnAtItyapekShAyAmAha || asAviti || anena  ' na sattat ' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | sarvAsannihitatvAt kathaM sarvaj~nAnaM 
harerityata Aha || sa iti || etena  ' bahirantashcha ' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | viShNoH sarvajIvAbhinnatvAt kathaM teShu sthitirityata Aha ||vilakShaNashcheti || kathaM vailakShaNyamityata Aha || sarvata iti || keshAdiShu pANyAdishaktimattvaM yuktiviruddhamityataH pratItatvAnna yuktiviruddhamiti bhAvenAha || kR^iShNeti || anena  ' sarvataH ' ityuktArthaM bhavati | kA nAma bhagavatpANyAdishaktirityata Aha || sarveti || vettItyetat karmaNo.apyupalakShakam | anena  ' sarvendriyaguNa ' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | sarvendriyaguNA AbhAsyanate.anu yante.aneneti | bhagavataH pANyAdimattve shrutyAdAvanindriyatvoktiH kathamityata Aha || sa iti || anena  ' sarvendriyavivarjitaM ' ityuktArthaM bhavati | j~nAnAdiguNasadbhAve kathaM tasya nirguNatvoktirityata Aha || guNairiti || kuta evaM nirguNatvashruterarthAntaraM kalpyate sarvathA guNarAhityameva kiM na syAdityataH tasya sarvakalyANaguNamUrtimattvena pramANasiddhatvAdityAha || sarveti || anena  ' nirguNaM ' ityuktArthaM bhavati | hareH pANipAdAdimattve.acharatvoktiH kathamityata Aha || anyatheti || kvachichcharatvokteH kathaM vikAritvAbhAva ityata Aha || chara iti || anena  ' acharaM charameva cha ' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | kathaM sarvagatasya charaNamityato na tasya sarvagatatvameva kintvaNutvaM madhyamatvaM chAstItyAha || vyApta iti || anena  ' sarvamAvR^itya tiShTati ' ,  ' hR^idi sarvasya viShThitam ' ityAdyuktatAtparyaM bhavati | taddUre tadvantika ityAdau viruddhadharmoktyeshvarasya niHsvabhAvatvokteH kathamuktaM yuktaM syAdityatastadghaTayati || sarvagatvAditi || anena  ' dUrasthaM ' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | vyAptatvANutvAdInAM vastvantare sahAnavasthAnAt kathaM harau saha sthitirityatata Aha || ananteti || anantAvyayashaktitve.api virodhinaH kathaM te.atira santItyata Aha || na cheti || kShetraj~nanAmno jIve prasiddhyabhAvAchcha nAtrAsAvuchyata ityAha || na cheti || kvachit sadbhAve.api bhAvaH | na cha viShNAvapi kShetraj~nanAmno na prasiddhiriti vAchyam | uktavachana eva prasiddhatvAt | vachanAntare.api 
tatprasiddhiM darshayati || kShetraj~na iti || manaso vibhUtIrmanaso vikArAn | mAyArachitAH nimittabhUtasvechChArachitAH | 
itashcha  ' etadyo vetti ' ityetanna jIvaparamityAha || ata iti || yato.atra na jIvo vivakShito.ata eva etadyo vettIti bhagavadabhiprAyeNa | sAmAnyataH kShetraj~nashabdasya vyutpAditatvAt jIvasyApi kiJNchitkShetraj~nAnasadbhAvAt tsaya kShetraj~natvaprAptestannirAkaraNAya kShetraj~naM mAmityuktamityarthaH | jIvasya kShetraj~natvanirAkaraNAya kShetraj~naM mAmityuktamiti kuta iti chet? kim  ' etadyo vetti ' ityasyeshvaraparatvamabhyupagamyedamuchte uta jIvaviShayatvam? pakShadvayaM dUShayati || anyatheti ||  ' etadyo vetti ' ityasyeshvaraparatvamaN^gIkR^itya  ' kShetraj~naM mAM ' ityasya jIvavyAvartakatvAnaN^gIkAre parameshvarasya  ' etadyo vetti ' ityanenaiva kShetraj~natvasiddheH kShetraj~naM mAmiti punastadvachanasya vaiyyarthyaM syAt |etadyo vettItyasya jIvaparatvamaN^gIkR^itya kShetraj~naM mAmityasaya javavyAvartakatvAnaN^gIkAre vaktavyasya jIvakShetraj~natvasyaitadyo vettItyuktenaiva pUrNatvAt kShetraj~naM mAmiti nirarthakaM viruddhArthaM cha syAditi bhAvaH | 
etadyo vettItyasya jIvaparatve.api nottaravAkyavaiyyarthyam | jIvasya kShetraj~natvamuktvA IshvarasyApyuchyata iti kShetraj~natvenoktajIvasya kShetrasya cheshvaraikyamuchyata iti sArthakyopapatteH | pratyutaivamanabhyupagamyeshvarasyaiva kShetraj~natvasiddherityata Aha || bhedeti || jIvasya kShetraj~natvamuktvA tasyeshvarabheda uchyata ityAdiyojanAmanaN^gIkR^ityeshvarasya kShetraj~natvAN^gIkAre.apyetadyo vettIti sArthakameva | kShetraj~nanAmaniruktyartatvAdityarthaH | kShetraM jAnAtIti kShetraj~na iti kShetraj~nanAmanirukteH prasiddhatvAt kShetraj~naM chApi mAmityetAvataivAlaM kiM niruktyetyata Aha || sarveti ||  ' kShetraj~naM chApi mAM viddhi ' ityevokte kShetra cha j~nashcheti kShetraj~na iti vyutpattyA jaDajIvAtmakatvamIshvarasyaivochyata iti pratItiH syAt | tannirAkaraNAya prasiddhA.api vyutpattiruchyate | na cha prasiddhavyutpattiM parityajyaivaM vyutpattyA shaMkAprAptireva nAstIti vAchyam | jaDajIvAtmakasya sarvasyApIshvareNAbhedamaN^gIkurvatAM tathA pratItisambhavAditi bhAvaH |
Ishvarasya kShetraj~nanAmaniruktiH, jIvasya tadabhAva ityetatsarvasya etadyo vettIshvarastaM kShetraj~naM prAhurityAdivAkya eva IshvaravAchipadaprakShepeNa vaktuM shakyatvAt tadarthaM pR^ithag vAkyakalpane gauravamityata Aha || kShetraj~namiti || nottaravAkye jIvavyAvR^ittyarthameva svasya kShetraj~natvamAtramuchyate | yena gauravaM syAt | kintu jIvavyAvR^ittyarthamishvarasyAsphuTamuktaM kShIyate.atra IshvareNeti kShetramityarthasUchAnAya svasya kShetre sthitishchochyata iti bhAvaH |
yaduktametadyo vettIti jIvasya kShetraj~natvamuktvA kShetraj~naM chApIti IshvarasyApi taduchyate.ato na vaiyyarthyamiti tannirAchaShTe || tatpakSha iti || etadyo vettItyasya jIvaviShayatvapakShe kShetraM jAnAtIti kShetraj~na iti vyutpatterjIva iva Ishvare.api sAmyena etadyo vettItyuktyaiveshvarasyApi kShetraj~natvaM siddhyatyeva | ataH kShetraj~naM chApIti vAkyaM vyarthameveti bhAvaH | kShetraj~natayoktajIvasya kShetrasya 
cheshvarAbhedakathanAya kShetraj~naM chApi mAM viddhIti sArthakamityuktaM dUShayati || sarveti || yadi kShetraj~naM chApi mAM viddhIti sArthakamityuktaM dUShayati || sarveti || yadi kShetiraj~naM chApi mAmityatra kShetrakShej~narUpasya sarvasyAbhedo vivakShitaH syAttarhi sarvakShetraM kShetraj~naM chApi mAM viddhIti vaktavyam | sarvakShetreShviti saptamIprayogo.anupapannaH syAditi bhAvaH | tarhi kShetraj~nasyaiveshvarAbhedo.atrochyatAm | tathAtve bAdhakAbhAvAdityata Aha || na cheti || yadi kShetraj~natayoktajIvasyeshvarasya chaikyamAtra vivakShitaM syAttarhi kShetraj~no.ahaM chaika eveti vaktavyam | na tu kShetraj~namanUdyeshvaratvavidhAnaM yujyate | jIvamanUdya mAM viddhIti vidhAtumasyeshvarasyApi jIvavat kalpitatvena visheShAbhAvAditi bhAvaH || 3 ||
 ' tatkShetraM yat ' ityuktatvAt  ' yatashcha yat ' iti punaruktirityata Aha || yatashcheti || tarhi  ' sA cha yA ' iti vaktavyamityatastatpratij~nAntaramiti bhAvenAha || sa cheti || keyamanumatirityata Aha || anusAriNIti || kAryotpAdasyeti sheShaH | anenAnumantR^ishabdArtho.apyukto bhavati | atra pramANamAha || preraNeti ||  ' yatashcha yat ' ,  ' sa cha yaH ' iti pratij~nAdyayaM chettarhi tadubhayamuttaratrochyate | na chobhayoktiH shrUyata ityata Aha || upadraShTeti || atra pramANamAha ''upadraShTA.anumantA '' ityAdinA.anumanturuktatvAt taddharmatayA.anumatirapyuktaiveti bhAvaH |  ''yatprabhAvashcha '' iti pratij~nAtaM kutrochyata ityata Aha || j~neyamiti || nanu chaitanyasyAvikAritvAt kathaM vikAreShu chetanA paThyata ityata Aha || chetaneti || nanu mahAbhUtAnItyAdinoktAnAM saN^ghAtasya kShetratvAta kAryatvaM kathamuchyata ityAshaMkAM pariharan uktarthaM pramANamAha || suN^ghAta iti || 7 ||
j~neyaM vaktuM j~nAnamuchyate  ''amAnitvaM '' iti | tatra tattvaj~nAnArthadarshanapadasyAsphuTArthatvAt tadarthamAha || tattveti || nanvamAnitvamityAdinA j~nAnasAdhanaM tattvaj~nAnArthadarshanamiti j~nAnaM choktvopasaMhAre katham  ''etajj~nAnamiti proktaM '' ityuchyata ityata Aha || j~nAyata iti || proktamityatra j~nAnashabdeneti sheShaH | uktamityuchyata iti vA || 12 ||
nanu  ''anAdimatparaM brahma '' ityatrAnAdItyetAvatA pUrNatvAt anAdimaditi kimarthamuchyata ityata Aha || anAdIti || na chAtra 
bhAShyavirodhaH tatroktasya matupo mukhyArthasyAnaN^gIkAre bhAShye doShasyoktatvAt | atra punastamaN^gIkR^ityaiva prayojanAntaraM matupA chinotIti || paraMbrahma na sattannAsaduchyata ityetat pramANavAkyenaiva vyAchaShTe || mukhyata iti || kathaM mUrtAmUrtayoH sadasachChabdavAchyatvaM, kathaM cha bhagavatastadvilakShaNatvamitta Aha || mUrtamiti || paraM amUrtam || 17 ||
j~nAnagamyamiti j~nAnaviShayatvamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyaha || svayameveti || atra svaj~neyatvamevochyate, na tu paraj~neyatvam | na cha bhagavataH svaj~neyatvAbhAvaH | svayamiti tasyoktatvAdityarthaH | anyaj~neyatvamarthaH kiM na syAditi Aha || anyeti || j~nAnaM j~neyamiti j~neyashabdenaikasyAM kriyAyAM kartR^ikarmaNoraikyavirodhAnneshvarasya j~neyatvamuktamiti badatAM vAdinAM matanirAsAya svaj~neyatvamevochyate | na tvanyaj~neyatvam | tasya 'j~neyaM yattat pravakShyAmi ' ityupakramavAkya evoktatvena punaruktiprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | svaj~neyArthatve prabhAvoktiriyaM kathamityata Aha || kartR^ikarmeti || aghaTitamapyekasyAM j~nAnakriyAyAM kartR^irmabhAvamAtmani Ishvaro ghaTayatItyevamabhiprAyeNedamuchyate | ato bhavati prabhAvoktiriyamiti bhAvaH |
Ishvarasva j~neyatve pramANAntaraM chAha || svavettA svatantravettA | tasya vedanaM cha svatantram | kasya vettetyata Aha || sveneti || yachcha tasya vedanaM svatantramuktaM tadapi na tasmAdbhinnamityAha || vittishcheti || kiM svenaiva vedya ityata Aha || vedyashcheti || kvachiditi kimarthamuchyate, sarvathA parairvedyaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || taditi || yathA.anyeShAM bhagavajj~nAne tatprasAdasApekShatA tathA bhagavato.api svavedanAdo parasApekShatA nAstIti svAtantryaM vivR^iNoti || sveti || tena svavettR^itvAdinA | tathAhi- svaH svatantraH prakAsho yasyAsau prakAshashcheti svaprakAshaH | parasya vettA vedyashcha syAditi na svaprakAshashabdArthakathanam | jIvAnAmapi svaprakAshatvAt kathameka ityuchyata ityata Aha || jIvAnAmiti || jIvAnAM svatantratvettR^itvAbhAvAdeka iti yuktamiti bhAvaH || 18 ||
uktamupasaMhR^ityata tajj~nAnaM stUyate itIti || tatra madbhAvapadamanyathApratItinirAsAya vyAchaShTe || madbhAvAyeti || 19 ||
yatashcha yat sa cha ya iti pratij~nAtaM vaktuM prakR^ityAdisvarUpamuchyate  'prakR^itimiti ' | tatra prakR^itiM puruShaM chetyuktamiti sheShaH | ubhAvikyuktasya pulliN^genAnvayAya vyutkramaH | anenobhAvityetat pR^ithagvAkyamityuktaM bhavati | ubhe apIti saN^grahashcha | vikArAMshcha guNAMshchetyatra vikArAdInAM prakR^itiH svatantraM kAraNamityanyathApratItim ichChAdayo vikArA ityuktatvAd guNashabdArthameva vadan nirAkaroti || vikArANAmiti || upadraShTA.anumantA chetIshvarasyaiva svAtantryasya vakShyamANatvAt na prakR^iteH svAtantryaM, kintUpAdAnatvamevetyarthaH | nanvichChAdivat sattvAdiguNAnAmapi vikAratvAd vikArAMshcha guNAMshcheti pR^ithaguktiH kinimittetyata 
Aha || guNAnAM cheti || sattvAdiguNAnAM vikAratve.api vikAnAMshcha guNAMshcheti pR^ithaguktiH sattvAdInAmalpavikAratvAdichChAdInAM tato.adhikavikAratvAttadvivakShayA yuktetyarthaH |
 'kAryakAraNakatrR^itve ' iti shlokamachetanaprakR^itijIvaviShayatvapratItinirAsAya chetanaprakR^itIshvaraviShayatayA pramANenaiva vyAchaShTe || svadeheti || viShNutattvamAvR^ityeti || viShNoryathAsthitimaj~nAyitvetyarthaH | viShNutattvAj~nasyaiva bandhakarmasambhavena dehendriyahetutvAdaj~nAnahetuchitprakR^iterjIvasya sharIrendriyahetutvam | IshvaraparatayottarArdhaM vyAchaShTe || jIvasyeti || sarvakattR^itvAdIshvarasya bhogashaktikartR^itvaM kiM vishiShyochyata ityata Aha |. sarveti || yathA sarvapAlo.api vikuNThapo vishiShyochyate, sthAnAntarasyeva viNThasya pAlakAntararahitatvAt tathA sarvakartA.api hariH keShAJNchidbhoktR^itvAdInAM kartA vishiShyochyate | kAryAntara iva bhoktR^itvAdAvanyeShAM pravR^ittyabhAvAdityarthaH | visheSheNa svakarmaNA kevalena svakarmaNA | etena bhagavataH kAryakAraNakartR^itvahetutve.api chitprakR^iterbhoktR^itvapradAne svapravR^ittimapekShya kAryakAraNakartR^itve.adhikapravR^ittiriti kAryakAraNakatR^itve hetutvoktiriti sUchitaM bhavati |
etadubhayaM gItAyAmeva sUchitamityAha || parameshvarasyeti || parameshvarasyaiva kAryakAraNakartR^itve hetutve.api chitprakR^itestaduktiryuktA | bhoktR^itvadAne tasyA alpapravR^ittitvena tadapekShayA kartR^itve.adhikapravR^ittimattvAt | tathA parameshvarasya sarvakartR^itve.api vishiShya bhoktR^itvadAnoktiryuktA | bhoktR^itvadAne chitprakR^ityAdInAmanyatra pravR^ittimapekShyAlpapravR^ittitvena bhagavata evAdhikaprava-ttitvAdityetatsUchayitumasya shlokasya pUrvottarArdhayoruchyata ityuktamityarthaH | kathamanenaitatsUchitamityata Aha || kartR^itve.apIti || bhoktR^itvApekShayeti || svasyA bhoktR^itvadAne pravR^ittyapekShayetyarthaH | adhikapravR^ittiH kAryakAraNakartR^itva iti sheShaH | bhoktR^itve heturuchyate | visheSheNeti sheShaH |
 'puruShaH prakR^itistho hi ' ityatreshvara uchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || puruSha iti || Ishvarasya  'puruShaH sukhaduHkhAnAM ' iti puruShashabdena prakR^itatvAt kathamatra jIve puruShashabda ityata Aha || ubhayoriti || yadyapyatra puruShashabdeneshvaraH prakR^itastathApyatra puruShashabdasya jIvaviShayatvagrahaNaM yuktam |  'prakR^itiM puruShaM chaiva ' ityatra puruShashabdeneshvaravat jIvasyApi pirakR^itatvAt | anyathA  'ubhau ' ityasya vaiyyarthyAditi bhAvaH | astu jIvaH prakR^itastathApi samIpaprakR^itaM parityajya dUraprakR^itagrahaNaM nopapannamityata Aha || yatheti || samIpaprakR^itatve.apIshvarasya tatparityAgaMna dUraprakR^itajIvagrahaNamupapadyate | asya puruShasya prakR^itijaguNabhoktR^itvapratIteH | 
Ishvarasya tadayogAt, jIvasya tadyogyatvAt | yathAyogyamevArthAshrayaNasyopapannatvAditi bhAvaH | ubhayoH prakR^itatve jIvamAtragrahaNaM kathamityato vA.aha || yatheti || 21 ||
yadyatra puruShapadaM jIvaparaM tarhi punaruktiH syAt | jIvasya  'kAryakAraNakartR^itve ' ityanenoktakAryakAraNasaMbandhasyaiva prakR^itisthapadenokteH | sukhaduHkhAnAM bhoktR^itve ityanenoktasukhaduHkhAdibhogasyaiva  'bhuN^kte prakR^itijAn guNAn ' ityuktatvAdityata Aha || kAryeti || kAryakAraNasaMbandhasya sukhAdibhogasya cha prAguktatve.api tanmithyAtvavAdinAM nirAsAya  'puruShaH prakR^itistho hi ' ityuktatvAnna punaruktidoSha iti bhAvaH | nisAkaraNasya pramANasApekShatvAt tadanuktoktAbhidhAnamAtreNa kathaM nirAkaraNamityata Aha || hIti || atra kAryakAraNasambandhasya sukhAdibhogasya cha hishabdenAnubhavaprasiddhikathanena tanmithyAtvavAdinAmanubhavavirodhasya tarshitatvAt naitaduktAbhidhAnamAtramiti bhAvaH |
ahaM sukhIduHkhItyAdyanubhavasya bhrAntitvasambhavAt sukhAdibhogasya mithyAtvAN^gIkAre kathaM tadvirodha ityata aha || na hIti || sukhAdiviShayAnubhavo na bhramaH AntarArthAnubhavatvAt | AntarArthAnubhavasya bhramatvArshanAditi bhAvaH | bAdhakAbhAvAchcha nAyamanubhavo bhrama ityAha || na cheti || nanvAtmAdau jainAdInAM madhyamaparimANatvAdij~nAnasya bhramatvadarshanAt kathamAntarArthAnubhavatvAdabhratvamuchyata ityAshaMkAM pariharan vyAptimAha || sharIramiti || nAtrA.antarAnubhavatvameva hetuH | yena vyabhichAraH syAt | api tvaparokShatvavishiShTam | aparokShAnubhavasya cha vahireva bhramatvadarshanAdAntarAnubhavasya tadabhAvaH siddhyati || jainAdInAM chAnumAnAdinaiva madhyamaparimANatvAdibhrama iti bhAvaH | bAdhakAbhAve.api sukhAdyanubhavasya bhramatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || tatrApIti || yatra bahirarthAnubhavasya bhramatvaM tatrApi balavatpramANavirodhAdeva tat kalpyate | ataH sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya bAdhakAbhAvenAbhramatvaM yuktamiti bhAvaH |
itashcha na sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya bhramatvena sukhAdermithyAtvaM vAchyamityAha || sAkShIti || sAkShiyanubhavasidhdhasyApi sukhAderbhrAntikalpitatve sarvaM mithyA, AtmA satya iti vyavasthA.api na siddhyati | etadvyavasthAyA api sAkShyanubhavasiddhatvena mithyAtvApAtAditi bhAvaH | bhrAntitvamabhrAntitvamiti || bhrAntikalpitatvamabhrAntikalpitatvamityarthaH 
| sarvaM mithyA AtmA satya iti vyavahArata evAsti, na tu paramArthataH | atastadasiddhirnAniShTetyata Aha || vyavahArata iti || vyavahArata eveyaM vyavasthA.astItyapi na siddhyati | sAkShiNo.aprAmANye tatra pramANAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | kiJNcha sAkShyanubhavasyAprAmANye stambhAdau sthANvAdimanovR^ittirbhrAntiH | stambhAdimanovR^ittirabhrAntirityapa na siddhyati | sAkShiNa eva j~nAnasya bhrAntitvAbhrAntitvagrAhakatvAt | tadasiddhau cha vyavahAramAtraM cha na siddhyatIti bhAvenAha || bhrAntiriti || etena sarvaM mithyA AtmA satya iti vyavasthA vyavahArato.astItyetadAgamAdinA siddhyatItyetadapi nirastam | AgamAdiprAmANyasyApi sAkShigrAhyatvAt |  'sAkShisiddhasya ' ityAderekagranthatve bhrAntirityasya sAdhyAbhidhAnaparatayA tachCheShatvaM j~nAtavyam | 
yaduktaM sukhAdiviShayasAkShyanubhavasya na bhrAntitvaM, bAdhakAbhAvAditi tadayuktam | 'vimuktashcha vimuchyate ' ityAdipramANasadbhAvAdityata Aha || anubhava iti || nAnena sukhAdiviShayasyAnubhavasya bhrAntitvaM siddhyati | tatsvarUpaprAmANyayoH siddhyabhAvAt | sAkShyanubhavasyaiva tatsAdhakatvAt | tasya cha bhrAntitvAbhidhAnAditi bhAvaH | na cha sukhAdiviShaya eva sAkShyanubhavasya bhramatvaM, pramANasvarUpAdAvabhramatvamiti yuktam | visheShapramANAbhAvenAnAshvAsAt | sAkShyanubhavasya bhramatve.api pramANasvarUpapramANye lokavyavahArAdeva setsyata ityAshaMkyAha || vyavahArata iti || na lokavyavahArataH pramANasvarUpAdisiddhiH | lokasya cha tadvyavahArasya chAsiddheH | sAkShiNa eva tadgrAhakatvAt | tasya cha bhrAntitvAN^gIkArAditi bhAvaH | sAkShiNo bhrAntitve.api vyavahAravyavahartR^isiddhiH pratItita eva bhaviShyatItyAshaMkya pariharati || pratItita iti || bhavet pratItyaiva vyavahArAdisiddhiH yadi saiva siddhyet | na cha tatsAdhakaM vaktuM shakyata iti bhAvaH | sAkShiNa eva pratItisiddheH kathaM tatsAdhakAbhAva ityAshaMkya pariharati || svata iti || na sAkShiNA pratItisiddhiH | tasya sukhAdau bhrAntitvAN^gIkAreNa pratItyabhAve.api pratItirastIti bhramo.ayamiti shaMkAkuNThitashaktitvAditi bhAvaH |
itashcha na sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya bhramatvamityAha || sveti || sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya bhramatvAN^gIkR^itAvAtmAbhAvo.api syAt | AtmasAdhakAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | nanvahamiti pratyakShata evAtmopalabhyate | ataH kathaM tatsAdhakAbhAva ityata Aha || svayamiti || nAhamityanubhavenAtmasiddhiH, anubhavasya sukhAdau bhrAntitvAbhyupagemenAtmanyapi bhramatvashaMkAvArakAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | niradhiShThAnabhramAsambhavAt sukhAdi्ramAnyathAnupapattyA.adhiShThAnabhUtAtmasiddhirityata Aha || nirAlambana iti || nAnena tarkeNAtmasiddhiH | etattarkAnubhavasyApi sukhAnubhavavat bhramatvashaMkAyAH prasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | shrutirAtmani pramANamityata Aha || taditi || yachChrutiH pramANamAtmanyuchyate tachChrutiprAmANyasAdhakAbhAvenApramANyasyApi vaktuM shakyatvAt na tenAtmasiddhiriti bhAvaH | shruteH prAmANyAnubhavAt kathamaprAmANyamityata Aha || pramANatveti || nAnubhavena shruteH prAmANyasiddhiH | 
sukhAnubhavavadasyApyaprAmANye pramANatvabhramatvasambhavAditi bhAvaH | sAkShisiddhasyetyAdyuktamupasaMharati || itIti || evamuktaprakAreNa sAkShyanubhavasya bhramatve sarvaM mithyA AtmA satya iti vyavasthAdi kiJNchidapi na siddhyatItyarthaH |
sukhAdyanubhavo bhrama ityarthasAdhakashruteH prAmANyAsiddherna tayA sukhAdyanubhavasya bhramatvasiddhirityuktam | atha tasya shrautAnubhavasyApi bhramatvopapattyA sukhAdyanubhavasyAbhramatvameva bhavati | na tu tena tasya bhramatvasiddhiH | parasparaviruddhayoranyataraniShedhasyetaravidhinAntarIyakatvAditi bhAvenAha || bhrama iti || ito.api na sukhAdyanubhavasya bhramatvamityAha || sukheti || yadi lasukhAdyanubhavo bhramastarhi yat prachChannaM nairAtmyamatamaN^gIkR^itaM tatparakaTitaM syAt | sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya AtmasvarUpatvAdityarthaH | sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasyAtmarUpatvaM bhavanmata eva nAsmanmate | kintu manovR^ittirUpatvamevetyato.apasiddhAnta ityAha || na hIti || nanvastu sukhAdyanubhavasya bhramatvamAtmasvarUpatvaM cha | tathApi kathamAtmAbhAvaprasaN^ga ityata Aha || bhramasyeti || sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasya bhramatve.avidyAkAryatvaM syAt | bhramasyAvidyAkAryatvAN^gIkArAt | tathAchAtma no.apyavidyAkAryatvaM syAt | sukhAdiviShayAnubhavasyAtmasvarUpatvAt | avidyAkAryatve chAtmano mithyAtvaM durnivAramiti bhAvaH |
astvevamAtmano yuktyA durghaTatvam | tathApi na tadbAdhakam | AtmanaH pramANasiddhatvAt | na hi pramANasiddhasya yuktyA durghaTatvamAtreNa bAdho.astItyAshaMkya pariharati || durghaTatvamiti || yadyAtmanaH prAmANikatvAdyuktyA durghaTatvamapi na bAdhakamityuchyate tarhi sukhAdInAmapi durghaTatvaM sughaTatvaM vA.astu | na tadbAdhakaM, pramANasiddhatvAditi vaktavyamityarthaH | yuktyA durghaTatvamastu | na tadbAdhakamiti kathamityata Aha || na hIti || aN^gIkR^itya chedamuktam | yuktyA durghaTatvamaparihR^itya tasyAbAdhakatvAbhyupagame.atiprasaN^gaH syAdityAha || durghaTatvamiti || yadi yuktyA durghaTatvaM na bAdhakamityAtmAstitvaM durghaTatayA.aN^gIkriyate tarhyAtmano.avidyAtvaM durghaTamapyaN^gIkriyatAmavisheShAdityarthaH | prAmANikasyaiva yuktyA durghaTatvaM na 
bAdhakamityuchyate | na chAtmano.avidyAtvaM prAmANikaM, yena yuktyA durghaTatvamabAdhakaM syAdityata Aha |. atIti || nAtmano.avidyAtvamaprAmANikam | kiJNchichchetanaM kiJNchidachetanamityaN^gIkAre gauravaprApteH | sarvasyAchetanatvAN^gIkR^itereva jyAyastvamiti yuktisiddhatvAditi bhAvaH | na kevalaM prAmANike yuktyA durghaTatvamabAdhakam | kintu yadaN^gIkAre pramANAvirodhastatraiva | Atmano.avidyAtvaM pramANaviruddhamato yuktyA viruddhatvaM tatra bAdhakamevetyata Aha|| na cheti || atmano.avidyAtvaM vadatAM pratipakShiNAmuktarItyA na ko.api pramANavirodho.astIti bhAvaH | nanvevamanubhavabalena kAryakAraNasambandhasya sukhaduHkhAdibhogasya cha satyatvaM vadatA bhagavatA.anubhavasya bhramatvamabhyupagachChatAM matamevaM kimiti na nirAkR^itamityAshaMkAM pariharannuktamupasaMharati || ata iti || anubhavabhramatvasya sphuTamuktarItyA anantadoShaduShTatvapratIterna svayaM bhagavatA tannirAkR^itiH kR^iteti bhAvaH |
puruShaH prakR^itistha ityuktam | tatra svataH shuddhasya jIvasya prakR^itisthatve kiMkAraNamityata uchyate 'kAraNam ' iti || tatra paramAtmano jIvabhAvena sharIrasambandhAdyuktau shuddhasya kiM kAraNaM sharIrasambandhAderityataH saguNatvaM tatkAraNamuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyA.aha || asyeti || 22 ||
atra jIvasya sharIrasambandhe sattvAdiguNasaN^gaH kAraNamuchyate, na tu paramAtmanastatra saguNatvam | paramArthatastadanupapatteH | tanmithyAtvasya dUShitatvAditi bhAvaH | kiM jIvasya sattvAdiguNasaN^gaH sadasadyonijanmasu svatantrakAraNamuta nimittamAtram? nAdyaH | jaDatvena tadanupapatteH | dvitIye svatantrakAraNaM vAchyamiti shaMkAparihAratvena shlokamavatArayati || svatantreti || kathamanena hareH svatantrakAraNatvamuchyata ityataH pramANavAkyena shlokaM vyAchaShTe || sarvebhya iti || upari upari vartamAnaH, uttama iti yAvat | svAnukUlyena svAtmano.avikShepakatayA | matyA buddhipUrvakam | svAtantryaM tatra hetutvenaivoktam | paramatvAdityanena paramAtmetyuktArthaM bhavati | upadraShTetyAdau sarvatretishabdAnvayonAnumantR^itve hetvabhidhAyakatvaM draShTavyam | dehinonya ityanena parashabdo vyAkhyAto bhavati | nanvanumantuH prAgdehasthitatvenAnuktatvAdapyukto dehe.asminniti kathamuchyata ityata Aha || mAmiti ||  ' kShetraj~naM chApi mAM viddhi sarvakShetreShu bhArata ' iti prAganumanturdehagatatvenoktatvAdapyukto dehesminnityuktiryukteti bhAvaH | nanUpadraShTR^itvAdikamanumantR^itve hetutvenochyatAm | anumanturdehasthatayoktatvaM kimarthamuchyata ityata Aha || teneti || ko.ayamanumantetyato dehe.apyukta ityanenAhamevAnumanteti darshayati || dehasthatvenAtmanaH kathitatvAditi bhAvaH || 23 ||
'prakR^itiM puruShaM chaiva' ityAdyuktArthaM bubhutsAtishayotpAdanAya tajj~nAnaphalamuchyate-'ya enaM' iti | tatpramANavachanenaiva vyAchaShTe || dvividhamiti || j~nAtvA parokShataH | 'sarvathA vartamAnaH' ityasya pramAdAdanyAyena vartamAno.api niyatamokSha ityarthaH | paramapuraShAdidarshane kiM sAdhanamityata Aha || anAdIti || kathaM nAnAtvamityata Aha ||tatreti || svayamiti || svapratibhayA || tatheti || uktaprakAradvayena | anena 'dhyAnena' ityuktAkteM bhavati | 'kiJNchit' ityuktyAteShAM dhyAnAtiriktasAdhanasadbhAve.api tasyAlpatvAdanuktirityuktaM bhavati | R^iShayo.antaHprakAshA ityAdau R^iShINAmantardarshananiyamokteH kechanetyuktiH kimarthetyata Aha || kechiditi || R^iShyantaraviShayA shrutiriti bhAvaH | 'devAH' ityanena 'anye sAN^khyena' ityuktArthaM bhavati | krameNa kAlakrameNa | 
devAnAM dhyAnAbhAve darshanaM bhavati chettarhi darshanavirodhidhyAnaM kimarthaM te kurvantItyata Aha || yeShAmiti || sAN^khyaM pratibhA yogo darshanopAyo yeShAM te sAN^khyayogAH | 'pratibhA spaShTatAkramAt' ityuktam | tatra sarvottamapratibhA deveShu kasya mukhyetyata Aha || brahmeti || kechidityanena 'karma' iti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | atrApi shravaNapratibhayolpatvaM draShTavyam | anya ityanena 'anye tu' ityuktArthaM bhavati |
R^iShidevarAj~nAM pratibhoktA | tatra kimeteShAmekavidyaiva pratibhA.asti, atha tAratamyenetyapekShAyAmAha || R^iShIniti || brahmaNaH pratibhApramANamAha || brahmaNa iti || tarhi tasya hareH sakAshAt shravaNaM kimarthamityata Aha || viShNoriti || prItyarthameva, na tu j~nAnArtham | keShAM tarhi j~nAnArthaM shravaNamityata Aha anyeShAmiti || mAnuShettaramiti || mAnuShANAM prAyaH shravaNAdeva j~nAnamityarthaH | nanvevaM dhyAnAdiyoginAmapi shravaNAdisadbhAve kathaM mAnuShANAM shrutaveditvaM kvachiduchyata ityata Aha || atyalpeti || evaM darshanasAdhanaM nAnAvidhamuktvA prakR^itamanusandhatte || sarva iti || 
yaduktaM dhyAnAdiyoginAmapi shravaNAdyastIti tadayuktam | tathAsati keShAJNchit 'shrutvA.anyebhyaH' iti vishiShyoktyasambhavAdityata Aha || anyeShAmiti || dhyAnAdiyoginAM shravaNAdisadbhAve.api manuShyANAM 'shrutvA.anyebhyaH' upAsate iti visheShoktiryuktA | teShAmatyalpapratibhAnatvena shravaNabAhulya.sadbhAvAditi bhAvaH | anenAtyalpapratibhAnatvAditi vivR^itaM bhavati | kathaM manuShyANAmatyalpA.api pratibhA yujyate | shrutiparAyaNA iti shravaNaikAshrayatvokterityata Aha || manuShyANAmiti || 
manuShyANAmatyalpapratibhAsadbhAve.api shrutiparAyaNA iti visheShaNaM yuktam | tatpratibhAyA mUlapramANApekShatvena svAtantryAbhAvAt prAyeNAsamyaktvAchcha | asvatantre.asAdhuni chAsattvoktidarshanAditi bhAvaH |
yaduktaM manuShyANAM piratibhA mUlapramANasApekShA prAyo na samyagutpadyate, alpA cheti tadayuktam | pANDavAdimanuShyANAmashrutArthe.api samyak bahupratibhAdarshanAdityAshaMkAM pramANenaiva pariharati || ashruteti || vishrutA vyAptA bahuletyarthaH | tallakShaNAntarANi chAha || yashcheti || yaH puruShaH svamukhaparimANenanavaparimANAdhodehavAn, yA cha strI svamukhaparimANenAShTaparimANavatI tau punaH svasvAN^guliparimANena ShaNNavatyaN^galau, svasvatAlaparimANena dashatAlau, svasvapAdaparimANena saptapAdau tau cha surottamau vidyAdityarthaH | atra tAlo nAma madhyamAN^gulyagrAt maNibandhaparyantaH kara uchyate | devottamalakShaNamuktvA devamAtralakShaNamAha || yAvaditi || tat ShaNNavatyaN^gulaM krameNa hrasadekanavatyaN^gulaparyantamuttamAvarasurAvadhikadevamAnaM bhavati | atra saptapAdaparimANaM krameNa hrasadekAN^gulonameva bhavatItyarthaH | mandharvAdilakShaNamAha || tadUnamiti || tadekanavatyaN^gulaM saptAshItyaN^gulaparyantaM krameNa hrasadgandharvAdiparimANaM bhavati | atrApi saptapAdaparimANaM krameNa hrasatpunarekAN^gulonaM bhavatItyarthaH ||manuShyalakShaNamAha || tAvaditi || saptAshItyaN^gulaM manuShyaparimANamityarthaH | asuralakShaNamAha || tata iti || saptAshIteradhastAt asuraparimANamityarthaH | devopadevAnAM mAnasya sambhUya kiyatIpvaN^gulAdupari devottamaparimANAt | ShaNNavatyaN^gulAdadho yadaShTachAN^gulaM taddevopadevaparimANaM j~nAtavyamityarthaH | R^iShyAdilakShaNamAha || deveShviti || chyavanAdInAM pR^ithvAdInAmavaradevavat parimANaM j~nAtavyamityarthaH | etallakShaNatAratamye hetumAha || yAvaditi || anenaitat svAbhAvikamiti choktaM bhavati || 25-26 ||
yaduktaM harireva sarvajIvAnAM sadasadyonijanmasu svatantrakAraNamiti tatprapaJNchyate 'yAvaditi' | tatra kShetraj~nasya hareH kShetrasaMyogo nAma jaDadehasaMyoga ityantathApratItinirAsAyAha || kShetreti || 'yAvat saJNjAyate' ityetadvivaraNarUpe 'mama yoniH' ityuttarAdhyAyagatavAkye lakShmInArAyaNasaMyogAtsarvabhUtasambhavasyoktatvAt atrApi kShetrapadena shrIrevochyata iti bhAvaH | avyaktatatve prasiddhaH kShetrashabdaH shrIvAchItyetatkuta ityataH shriyaH shretrashabdavAchyatvaM, prasaN^gAt mahAbhUtAnItyAdyuktAhaN^.hkArAdishabdAnAM cha devatAvAchitvaM pramANena darshayati || avyaktamiti || sarasvatyAdInAmapi shrIshabdavAchyatvAt  tadvyAvR^ittyarthamAha || sadeti || kiM jaDAvyaktAbhedAt tachChabdavAchyetyata Aha || nirdoSheti || kathaM tarhi avyaktAdipadavAchyatvamityata Aha || sA hIti || na vyajyata ityavyaktam | viShNurasyAM nivasatIti kShetram | mahAguNeti mahadbrahma, jIvottameti pradhAnamuchyata ityarthaH | atra mahato.anuktatvepyAdikAryatvAt grAhya eva | kriyAH uddishya | uktaM vivR^iNoti || jIveti || shabdAdi bodhayatIti buddhirityarthaH | tatsuto.aniruddho.api || sparshayatIti sparshaH | hR^iJN haraNa iti dhAtoH rasAharaNahetutvAt jihvetyarthaH | AghrAtergandhAghrANahetutvAt | vachanAt vachanapravartakatvAt | hAnilAbhayornimittatvAt | sana lAbha iti dhAtuH | kvachidviShNoH pAdadevatvokteH viShNunetyuktam | yaj~nashambhU cha na hariharAvityuktam || shachIti || padanAt gatipravartakatvAt | pada gatAviti dhAtuH | nirAvR^ityA pratibandhAbhAvena | vAtIti vAyuH | adanAdagniH | prathanAd vistR^itatvAt pR^ithivI | janmalayahetutvAt jalamityarthaH | pR^ithu vistAra iti dhAtuH | utpattilayayorjalAdhInatvadarshanAt tanniyAmakadevatAyAstatsiddham | shabdanAdityAdeH shabdAdipravartakatvAditvAtyarthaH | mukhyavAyuH sukhanAt sukhamityAdi draShTavyam | sA shrIreva | evaM sarasvatIvadvAyoH patnIvirdhR^itirmatetyarthaH |
shrIrevechChetyuktam | tadupapAdayati | ichCheti || yadyavyaktachetanechChAdishabdaiH lakShmyAdidevatA uchyante tarhi kvachidavyaktamuktvA 
punashchetanAdikaM kathamuchyata ityata Aha || sthAneti || avyaktapadoktashriyaH chetanAdipadena punaruktiryuktA | aibhimAnyamAnasthAnabhedena rUpabhedAdityarthaH | evaM devatAntare.api draShTavyam | kathaM tarhi jaDapadArtheShvavyaktAdishabdAH pravartanta ityata Aha || etairiti || avyaktAdinAmakadevatAbhimanyamAnatvAt jaDAnAmavyaktAdishabdavAchyatvamiti bhAvaH | kShiNoti nAshayati | kShitiM kR^itvA trAti svanivAsanimittena rakShati | kShINam adhamam || visheShavikR^itisthitA iti || mahadAdibhyo.atishayena vikAritayA.avasthitA ityarthaH | ghaTAdAvapyetadeva vikArashabdapravR^ittinimittamityAha || visheShAditi || vigatamityAdeH atrAntimakArye nAshaM vinA kAryAntarotpAdakatvaM nAstItyarthaH | abhimAninAmapIchChAdishabdavAchyatvAt kathaM vikAratvamityata Aha || taditi || sambandho niyamyaniyAmakabhAvaH |
yaduktaM chetanAchenataM sarvaM kShetramiti, taduktam | chetanasya 'idaM sharIraM' ityuktasharIratvAnupapatteH | hiMsAheturityAdinirvachanasya tatrAsambhavAdityata Aha || yasyeti || chetanasya kShetratve.api na tasyoktasharIratvAsambhavaH | 'yasyAtmA sharIram' ityuktatvAt 
| uktaniruktyasambhave.api bhagavattantratvena sharIratvopapatteriti bhAvaH | 'yAvatsaJNjAyate kiJNchit sattvaM'ityatra sattvashabdo jIvavAchIti 'mama yoniH' iti vAkyasyodAharaNenaiva sUchitam | tatra sattvashabdasya jIvavAchitve pramANamAha || sattvamiti || tayoranya iti yaduchyate sa jIva iti vaktavye sattvamiti shrutyochyate | sattvashabdena jIvagrahaNe tasyAnAditvAt saMjAyata ityuktajananaM na yujyata ityata Aha || janIprAdurbhAva iti || 27 ||
parameshvarasya sarvasharIrasthAtvamuktam | tarhyadhiShThAnatAratamyAttasya tAratamyaM duHkhisahAvasthAnAt duHkhaM cha syAdityata uchyate-'samaM' iti | tatra 'vinashyatsvavinashyantam' ityayuktam | jIvAnAM vinAshAbhAvAt | na cha tasyAchetanaviShayatvam | chashabdAdyabhAvAdityata Aha || jIveShviti || evaM vijAnanneva j~nAnItyuktam | tajj~nAnaphalamuchyate 'samaM' iti | shlokadvayaM smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || duHkheti || na hinastItyasyArthaH 'sa eva' iti || 28-29 ||
IshvaraH sadasadyonijanmasu karmAnapekShyaiva kAraNaM chettarhi tasya vaiShamyAdi syAt | karmApekShAyAM svAtantryaprachyutiH | tathA tasyApi DanakasadbhAvAchcha na svAtantryamityata uchyate-'prakR^itya' iti | tatra prakR^itireva katrIM na paramAtmetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || prakR^ityeti || svayameva prArabhyeti || pUrvakarmAdikaM svayameva prabodhyetyarthaH | abhiprAyaM vakti || viShNoriti || karmasApekShatve.api na bhagavataH svatantryaprachyutiH | yAvatA.asau svayameva pUrvakarmAdikamudbodhya tadapekShyedAnIM karmANi kArayati | na tu karmAdikaM viShNorudbodhakamiti bhAvaH | kuta etadityata Aha || pUrvamiti || astu karmAdi harirudbodhayati, na tu ddharimudbodhayatIti | tathApi harestadapekShatvAdasvAtantryamityataH karmAdisattAyA api bhagavadadhInatvAt tadapekShAyAmapi nAsvAtantryamiti bhAvena karmAdisattAyA bhagavadadhInatve pramANamAha || dravyamiti || kuta evamarthakalpanetyata uktarthe smR^itisamAkhyAM darshayati || svayamiti || nanvatra IshvareNetyashravaNAt kathamayamarthaH syAdityata Aha || teneti || 'samaM pashyan hi sarvatra samavasthitamIshvaram' iti Ishvarasya prasatutatvAt teneshvareNetyanukte.api siddhyatItyarthaH | kimanayA kalpanayA?  prakR^itereva kartR^itvaM neshvarasyetyevArthaH kiM nasyAdityata udAhR^itaH smR^itivirodhastAvat vAkyAntaravirodhaM cha darshayati || ahamiti || teneshvareNetyatra sUchitaM chetyAha || prakR^ityeti || chashabdena kathametatsiddhyatItyata Aha || prakR^iteneti || uchyamAnakriyAyAH prakR^itakartR^itvamIrayedityarthaH |
Ishvarasya kartR^itvAbhidhAyakavachanavirodhAnnArthAntarakalpanA yuktetyuktam | prakR^iteH kartR^itvasya shrutyAdiviruddhatvAchcha nAsau yuktetyAha || prakR^iteriti || tvadR^ite dUre.api kiJNchana kenApi na kriyata ityarthaH | itashcha nArthAntarakalpanA yuktetyAha || kevaleti || IshvarasamuchchachArthashchashabda ityataH kevaletyuktam AtmAnamakartAramityatra pareNeshvarasyAkartR^itvAN^gIkArAt na tatsamuchchayArthashchashabda iti bhAvaH | itashcha neshvarasyAkartR^itvametadarthaM ityAha || tata eveti || ito.api nArthAntarakalpanA yuktetyAha || ahamiti || atra yAvatsaJNjAyata itIshvarasya sarvakartR^itvaM prakR^itamiti tenApIshvarAkartR^itvavyAkhyAnaM viruddham | na cha vAchyaM pUrvavAkye.api prakR^itereva kartR^itvaM kShetraj~nasya tatsaMyogAt kartR^itvopachAra iti | mama yonirmahadbrahmetyAdinA uttarAdhyAye.anyathaitadvAkyArthasya vakShyamANatvAdityarthaH | ito.api na prakR^itereva kartR^itvamiti asyArtha ityAha || achetanamiti || kathaM svoktivirodha ityata Aha || ichCheti || ichChApUrvakriyAsvIkAro hi kartR^itvam | tathA shruteH | achetanaM nAmechChArahitam | ato.achotanaM cha karoti cheti vyAhatiriti bhAvaH | nanu prakR^iteH svatantrakartR^itvAbhAve.api pariNAmarUpaM kartR^itvamaN^gIkriyata eva siddhAntinA.api | atantadartho.ayaM shlokaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || vikAreti || yadyapi prakR^iteH pariNAmarUpaM kartR^itvamaN^gIkR^itaM, tathApi na tadartho.ayaM shlokaH | atra sarvakarmaNAM prakR^ityaiva kriyamANatvokteH | etadarthatve cha parameshvarAdikarmasu prakR^itivikAratvAbhAvAt sarvasha iti padasyArthasaN^.hkottaprApterityarthaH |parameshvarAdikarmaNaH prakR^itivikAratvAbhAvaH kuta ityata Aha || achetaneti || 30 ||
na kevalaM bhagavataH sarvaprerakatvAdij~nAnamAtreNAlam | kintu tasya sarvAdhAratvAdyapi j~nAtavyamityuchyate- " yadA " iti | tat tirohitArthatvAt pramANavAkyenaiva vyAchaShTe || eketi || bhUtapR^ithagbhAvasya paramAtmasthatvoktyA pR^ithagbhUtAnAM tatsthatvamabhipretam | 
tadevAtroktam || 31 ||
sarvachetanAchetanAtmakatvAt paramAtmanaH kathaM bhUtAnAM tataH paR^ithagbhAva ityata uchyate- " anAditvAt " iti | tatra paramAtmano.akartR^itvapratItiM cha nirAkartuM sharIrasthapadaM vyAkhyAti || sharIrastha iti || sharIrasthashabdasya kuto jIvavAchitvamityataH tatparayogaM darshayati || svapneneti || nanu jIvavadIshvarasyApi sharIrasthiteH jIvasyaiva tatpadavAchyatvaM kutaityata Aha || sharIrastha iti || viShNorapi mayedaM sR^iShTaM, madadhInamityabhimAno.astyeva | ataH kathaM tadanabhimAna ityata 
Aha || tadgatAnAmiti || sharIrasthapadaM jIvavAchakaM chet kathaM yojanetyata Aha || anAditvAditi || iti vAchyamiti sheShaH | jIvasyApyanAditvAt kiM vishiShyeshvarasyaiva taduchyate, yenAsya jIvAbhedanivAraNe hetutvaM syAdityata Aha || sharIreti || evambhUtAdimattvAbhAve.api kathaM paramAtmano jIvAdvisheSha ityata Aha || jIvasyeti || itishabdo hetau | nanu nirguNatvaM kathamIshvarasya jIvabhede heturbhavati jagatkartR^itvAdiguNAnAm Ishvare bhAvena hetorasiddherityata Aha || sattveti || nAtra guNapadena jagatkartR^itvAdayo vivakShitAH | kintu sattvAdaya eva | tatsambandhashcheshvare nAsti, jIve.astIti bhavati heturiti bhAvaH | karoti na lipyata iti jIveshvarabhede hetvantaram | tadvyAchaShTe || sarvamiti || jIvo na karoti lipyata eveti draShTavyam | lepashcha tatphalena | nanvatra jIvAdyabhedasyAprAptatvAtkathaM niShedho yukta ityata Aha || vAdIti || yathA shUnyavAdisiddhatvAt shUnyakAraNatvasya  " taddhaika AhuH " ityAdinA niShedhaH kriyate tathA sarvAdvaitavAdiprAptatvAt advaitaniShedho yujyate | yathA cha j~nAnadvArA mokShArthaM karmabhirIshvara evArAdhya iti karmashrutyabhiprAyAparij~nAnaprAptasya kevalakarmaNaivasvargAdipuruShArthalAbho bhavatItyasya  " iShTApUrtaM " ityAdinA niShedhaH kriyate tathA bhagavatA sarvaM vyAptamiti  " sarvaM khalidaM brahma " ityAdishrutyAbhiprAyAparij~nAnaprAptasyAdvaitasya niShedho yukta iti bhAvaH | prAtItika evarthaH kiM na syAdityata uktArthe vAkyAntarasammatimAha || kurvANa iti || mR^ityAdirahita ityanenAvyayapadaM vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | Ishvarasya chetanAchetanabhinnatve shrutisammatiM chAha || sa eSha iti || 32-34 ||
adhyAyArtha upasaMhriyate || kShetreti || tatra bhUtaprakR^itimokShapadaM tirohitArthatvAt vyAchaShTe || jIvAnAmiti || mokShaM mokShasAdhanamamAnitvamityAdyuktam || 35 ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrthabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachatasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM trayodasho.adhyAyaH || 13 ||
|| atha chaturdasho.adhyAyaH ||
hariH OM|| etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || kShetreti || prAdhAnyenottarAdhyAyaiH sAdhanamevochyate | tatra bandhaprakAraparij~nAna eva tanmokShasAdhanAnuShThAnaM yujyate | bandhashcha triguNAtmakaH | ato  " yAvatsaJNjAyate " ityuktavivaraNapUrvakaM triguNavikArasthitiM tadatyayopAyaM cha darshayatyanenAdhyAyeneti bhAvaH |  " kAryate hyavashaH karma " ityAdau traiguNyasya saN^kShepeNoktatvAt vivichyetyuktam | 
 " paraM bhUyaH pravakShyAmi " iti pratij~nAtamuchyate  " mama yoniH " iti | tatra yonishabdasya kAraNArthatvapratItinirAsAya bhAryAdyarthatve pramAmamAha || yoniriti || sthAnaM guhyasthAnam | astvevaM yonishabdo bhAryAdyanekArthaH | prakR^itaH kimartha ityata Aha || atreti || yonishabdasyAnekArthatvAt kathamayamevArtha ityata Aha || tasminniti || 3 ||
traiguNye vivichyokte sati tarhi guNA eva sarvottamAH, na tu tato.anyaH sarvottama iti shaMkA syAt | sA nirAkriyate-nAnyamiti | atra guNAnAnameva kartR^itvaM, neshvarasyaityanyathApratItinirasAyAha || etabhya iti || aj~nasyApi puruShatvAt ko visheSho j~nAnina ityata Aha || antheti || evaM yojanAyAM  " madbhAvaM so.adhigachChati " iti vyarthaM syAt | vAkyasya tadvinaiva samAptatvAdityataH tatsArthakyaM darshayati || kathamiti || bhagavati bhAvaprAptiyogyasyaiva puruShatvaM  " puruShatve vA vistarAdAtmA " ityAdishrutisiddham | pratIta evArthaH kiM na syAdityato  " mama yoniH " ityAdi smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || mahAlakShmIriti || parA ShaDbhyo.adhikA | dguNatvAt sat, tviSha dIptAviti dhAtoH prabhArUpatvAt tvamiti sattvamityarthaH | sR^iShTyA hi raJNjanaM bhavati | kimiyaM prasiddhA pR^ithivIdevatA.asAvityata Aha || yaditi || tamu glapana iti dhatuH | glapanaM saMsAreNa glAnidAnam | amuktigA ityanena  " dehe dehinaM " ityasyArtha ukto bhavati | keShAM ko bandhiketyata Aha || sarvAniti || anena tatra sattvamityAdinA tAratamyenoktabandhatraividhyasya viShayaH pradarshito bhavati | evametAsAM sarvabandhakatvenAtisAmarthyAt sarvottamatvamiti na mantavyamityAha || etAbhya iti || viShNuM sarvottamatvena jAnanneva yato vimuchyate.ataH sa eva puruShaH | ato naitAbhyo vidyate paraH iti jAnan nR^ipashurityarthaH || 16-19 ||
 " rajasastu phalaM duHkham " ityatra duHkhashabdaH kevaladuHkhArtha ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || rajasa iti || duHkhashabdaH kathaM duHkhamishrasukhavAchItyata Aha || duHkhamiti || atra kevaladuHkhavAchI kiM na syAdityato rajaso mishraphalatve smR^itimAha || karmaNa 
iti || aj~nAnajamityanena aj~nAnamiti vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tena kevaladuHkhasya tamaHphalatvoktishchArthAntare bAdhiketi sUchitaM bhavati || 20-21 ||
guNAtyayopAyAdiprashnasya parihAra uchyate  " prakAshaM " iti | tatra svasmin prakAshaM nechChati, svagatamohaM na dveShTi, duHkhAdisAmyaM cha spR^ihAdyabhAvamAtraM, sarvArambhaparityAgashcha sarvatrodAsInatvamityanyathApratItinirAsAya pramANAntareNa tadvyAchaShTe || loketi || puruShAntare sthitaM prakAshAdi sAdhu na dveShTi | tatra mohAdyasAdhu nechChatItyarthaH | svasya prAptaprakAshatvAt mohojj~nitatvAt svasminneva tadichChAdyabhAvaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || svayamiti || mohaM dveShTi cheti draShTavyam | taM chApItyanena mAM chetyuktArthaM bhavati | sukhaduHkhAdItyasya viShNubhaktiparityAge sukhasya, anyathA duHkhasya bhAve.apItyarthaH | arthArthamityAdinA samaloShThetyAdyuktarthaM bhavati | avaiShNavetyanena sarvArambhetyuktArthaM bhavati | viShNu yAtItyanena saguNAnityAdeH tAtparyamuktaM bhavati || 22 ||
itashcha sarvArambhaparityAgIti na kevalodAsInatvamuchyate | udAsInavaditi pUrvavAkye kevalodAsInatvAbhAvasyokteH | neN^gata iti pUrvavAkye karmAbhAvasyoktatvAt kathaM kevalodAsInatvAbhAva ityata Aha || neN^gata iti || neN^gata iti na sarvapravR^ittiniShedhaH, kintu bhagavadudAsInapravR^ittiniShedha evetyarthaH | tarhi neN^gata ityanenaiva avaiShNavakarmAkaraNasyoktatvAt sarvArambhaparityAgIti punaruktirityata Aha || iti vaktIti sheShaH | neN^gata iti sAmAnyoktiriti draShTavyam | neN^gata ityalpAvaiShNavapravR^ittyabhAva uchyate | sarvArambhaparityAgIti dIrghAvaiShNavapravR^ittyabhAva uchyata ityatashcha na punaruktiriti bhAvena iN^ganArambhashabdayoH alpamahatkarmArthatve pramANamAha || iN^ganamiti || 23-25 ||
nanu guNashabdena shryAdInAM vivakShitatvAt  " saguNAn samatItyaitAn " iti tadatyayaH kathamuchyate | ashakyatvAdityata Aha || lakShmyAdibhiriti || lakShmIti shrIruchyate | smR^ityuktArthAnuvAdeva arthAntaraM chAha || taditi || ubhayatra prayogaM darshayati || yatheti || yathA dvArapAlakR^itabandhAtyayena gachChan dvArapAlamatItya rAjAnaM gachChatItyuchyate, yathA cha yo rAjAnaM gachChati sa dvArapAlamatItya gachChatItyuchyate tathaivetyarthaH | brahmabhUyAya ityasya brahmabhAvAyetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || brahmeti || 'mama yonirmahadbrahma' iti mahAlakShmyA eva brahmashabdena prakR^itatvAt atrApi saivochyata ityarthaH | pramANAntarasamAkhyAnenApyetat sAdhayati || atItyeti || guNAtItasya bhagavatprAptyAdyeva vaktavyaM, lakShmIprAptyA bhagavatprAptiH | yena taduktiH saN^gatA syAdityato.abhiprAyamAha || maditi || tatsthatva iti sheShaH | lakShmInArAyaNayoraviyogashchet guNatIto mAmApnotItyeva vaktavyam | kiM paramparoktyetyata Aha || tathApIti || yadyapi tayoraviyogastathApi lakShmIsamIpaM prApya tadanuj~nayA bhagavatprAptirbhavatIti paramparoktiryuktetyarthaH | 'sukhasyaivakAntikasya' iti tirohitArthatvAdvyAyaShTe || ekAntikasyeti || ekamevAsmAdadhikamiti gaNane.ante sthitamekAntikam | tattu mokSha eveti bhAvaH ||

karma sAttvikamanyadrAjasAdItyuchyate | tatashchaitAdR^ishameva satkarma anyadasatkarmeti sadasatkarma vivichyoktameveti bhAvaH | na cha vAchyamatraivaMvidhakarmaNaH sattvamanyasyAsattvaM svayamevochyata iti | anyathA prasaN^gAnanuguNatvaprasaN^gena sadAdishabdasya sAttvikAdyarthatvAt | etena 'aphalAkAN^kShibhiH' ityAderapyevamevAdhyAyasaN^gatiH sUchitA bhavati |
nanu 'karma chaiva tadartho.ayaM' iti sAttvikaM karmoktvA rAjasamanabhidhAya 'ashraddhayA hutaM' iti tAmasameva kimuchyata ityata Aha || rAjasasyeti || nAtra tAmasamevAsachChabdenochyate api tu rAjasamapIti bhAvaH | takuta ityato.ashraddhayetyuktAsallakShaNasya rAjase.api bhAvAdityAha || viShNivati || 'na cha tatpretya no iha' iti yadrAjasatAmasakarmaNoH phalamuktaM tadvivichya smR^ityA darshayati || sAttvikamiti ||

|| atha aShTAdasho.adhyAyaH ||
hariH OM|| etadadhyAyapratipAdyamarthaM darshayati || sarveti || yatsarveShvadhyAyeShu viprakIrNatayA puruShArthasAdhanamuktaM tanmandAnAM buddhyArohArthaM saN^kShepeNAsminnadhyAye nirUpyate | chaturdashAdyanuktaM traiguNyaM chochyata ityarthaH || 1-2 ||
'sarvakarmaphalatyAgaM' iti svoktatyAgasvarUpAvadhAraNAya prAtItikI vidvanmatavipratipattirudbhAvyate-'tyAjyam' iti | atra yaj~nadAnatapaHkarma na tyAjyaM, kAryameva taditi bhagavanmatavirodhitvAt tyAjyaM doShavaditi tyAgapakShiNo nindyA ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || manIShiNa iti || ata iti || 'kAryamityeva vatkarma' ityatra yathA karmaNi saN^gaphalatyAgena karmatyAgo varNyate, na tu karmasvarUpatyAgena, tathA tyAjyamityetadartho varNayituM shakyate | ato na tasya bhagavanmatavirodhaH | kuto.arthAntarakalpaneti chet manIShiNa ityuktatvAdeveti bhAvaH || 3-4 ||
nishchayaM shrR^iNviti pratij~nAtamuchyate-yaj~neti | tatra jyotiShTomAdiyaj~neShu hiraNyAdidAneShu yatInAM shUdrAdInAM chAdhikArAbhAvAt UrdhvaretastvAditapassu gR^ihasthAdInAm adhikArAbhAvAt kathaM sarveShAM yaj~nAdividhIyata ityata Aha || dravyeti || nAtra sarveShAM jyotiShTomAdiyaj~naH, hiraNyAdidAnAni, UrdhvaretastvAditapAMsyeva vidhIyante, kintu dravyayaj~nAdiyaj~nAH, vidAyAdidAnAni, satyavachanAditapAMsi | teShAM cha yatyAdInAmapyuchitatvAt yuktaM sarveShAM tadvidhiriti bhAvaH | 'nAgnirna yaj~naH' ityAdeH trivarNabAhyAnAM na kvApi yaj~ne.adhikAra ityata Aha || viShNviti || dravyAdiyaj~nAbhAve.api teShAM svAdhyAyayaj~ne.adhikAro.astyeva | na cha vedAnadhikAreNa tadabhAvaH | viShNunAmasvAdhyAyayaj~ne.adhikArasambhavAditi bhAvaH | teShAM kiM tapa ityata Aha || satyeti || 5-6 ||
'tyAgo hi' ityuktaM prapaJNchyate-'niyatasya' iti | tatra karmatyAgasya svayameva stUyamAnatvAt kathaM mohanimittatvamuchyata ityata Aha || saN^geti || svarUpatyAgasyApi mohanimittatvaM kutaH? yonAyamarthaH syAdityata Aha || sveti || nanu puruShArthasAdhane|pi karmaNi duHkhasAdhanamiti mithyAj~nAnena tatsvarUpaparityAgasya rAjasatvakathanAt kathaM tAmasatvamityata Aha || mohamiti || nohaM vineti || paratrApIdaM duHkhasAdhanamiti mithyAj~nAnaM vinetyarthaH | duHkhashabdena sharIrAyAsa uchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || duHkheti || kevalamiti || sharIrAyAsadvArA prAptaM na chetyarthaH | sharIrAyAsa evArthaH kiM na syAdityata Aha || kAryeti || na kevalamanyathA punaruktiprasaN^gAdatra duHkhashabdo mAnasaduHkhArthaH | kintu tathA vachanAchchetyAha || duHkhamiti || arthavisheShavivakShAyAmevaM j~neyam | tadabhAve dvayamapi shabdadvayenochyata iti bhAvaH || 8-9 ||
sAttvikatyAgI punarnirUpyate-' na dveShTi' iti | tatra kathaM sAttvikatyAgino.akushalakarmAdveShaH kushalakarmAsaN^gashchochyate | 'kAryamityeva' ityuktivirodhAdityataH pramANAntareNa tadvyAchaShTe || na dveShTIti || puNya iti || tatphala iti yAvat || tameva stauti || ya iti || samyagityanena modhAvItyAdyuktArthaM bhavati | tadarpaNenetyanena tyAgItyuktArthaM syAt | tasyetyanenAniShTamityasya tAtparyamuktaM bhavati | kiM tasya sarvathA bandhakaM karma na bandhAya bhavatItyata Aha || bahulaM chediti || bahulaM chet sarvatyAginAmapyatyalpadoShakaraM kiyatparyantamityata Aha || yAvaditi || 10-11 ||
'aniShTamiShTaM mishraM cha' ityatra bandhakaM karmaphalaM tyAgina iShTamityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || anyeShAmiti || tyAgina eveShTaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || asyeti || na tyAgino bandhakaM karmaphalamiShTam | tyAgitvAdeva 'yastu karmaphalatyAgI' iti karmaphalechChAtyAgina eva tyAgitvenoktatvAditi bhAvaH | bhavedevaM yadi 'aniShTamiShTaM mishraM cha' ityatra bandhakakarmaphalaM vivakShitaM syAt | na chaivamabandhakakarmaphalasyApi grahaNe bAdhakAbhAvAdityatastyAgino bandhakakarmaphalasyaivAbhAve.atyAgino 
bandhakakarmaphalabhAve pramANamAha || j~nAnAderiti || tyAgimAtrasya j~nAnabhaktyAdeH | tasyaivAparokShatastattvasaMvettuH mokShabhogyAnandAtishayAt | tadR^ite j~nAnAdikamR^ite | anena 'bhavatyatyAginAM' ityuktArthaM bhavati | bhavatyatyAginAM pretya na tu tyAginAmityatyAginAM pratiyogitvena tyAgina eva vaktavyAH | saMnyAsinastu kimityuchyanta ityata Aha || kevaleti || atyAgipratiyogitayA saMnyAsikathanaM nAnupapannam | svArthe phalechChAbhAve.api paropakArArthaM kArIryAdikevalakAmyakarmakaraNasti tyAginAm | tadapi nyAsinAM nAstItyetAvanmAtravisheShavattvAt tyAgibhyo visheSho nyAsinAmityarthaH | etAvAneva chedvisheShaH tat kiM tayo- sAmyam? yena tyAgiShu vaktavyeShu nyAsinAmuktirityata Aha || tyAgitvamiti || karmaphalechChAbhAvo dvayorapi sama ityarthaH | tyAgibhyo nyAsinAmukta eva visheSha ityetat kuta ityata Aha || pareti || 12 ||
karmaNyabhimAnatyAgo.api saMnyAsa iti bhAvena karmakAraNAnyuchyante-'paJNcha' iti | tatra sAN^khyakR^itAntapadena paramasAN^khyasiddhAnta evochyate, na tu prasiddhasAN^khyameva | atra daivashabdeneshvarasya gR^ihItatvAt paramasAN^khyasya cha seshvaratvAt prasiddhasAN^khyasya nisIshvaratvAt, tathA paramasAN^khyasya vaidikatvenAtropAdAnasambhavAt anyasyAvaidikatvena tadasambhavAditi bhAvena tayoH seshvaratvAdau pramANamAha || kathitamiti || 13 ||
adhiShThAnapadasyAtra vivakShitamarthamAha || adhiShThAnamiti || 14-16 ||
tajj~nAnaM stUyate-'yasya' iti | etachcha sarvAnahaN^.hkArAdimatAM samamityanyathApratItinirAsAya vachanAntareNaiva vyAchaShTe || svAtantryamiti || Atman Atmani || lakShamyAdeshcha svAtantryaM vettItyanuShajyate | tadarthaM lokahananArtham | tadarthaM jAtatvenaivAlaM, kimIshvarasyAtantryAdij~nAnenetyata Aha || aj~na iti || lokAn hanti chediti sheShaH | tarhi j~nAnenaivAlaM, kiM tadarthaM jAtatvenetyataH parokShAparokShaj~nAninorapi tadarthamajAtayorlokahanena vibhAgena bAdhakAmaha || aparokSheti || parokShaj~nastadarthajAto yadi lokAn hanti tarhi kiJNchiddoSheNa lipyata ityarthaH | aparokShetyuktyA j~nAnaM chAparokShamapekShaitamiti sUchitam | parotraAnena tadarthaM jAtatvenaivAlaM, kimaparokShaj~nAnenetyato vA.a.aha || parokSheti || atra tadarthaM jAtaiti grAhyam | nanu sarvoShAmapyasvatantratvenAhantR^itvAt asyaiva na hantIti kiM vishiShyochyata ityata Aha || asvAtantryeti || bhAvo.asya nAstItyanyasya bhAvo.astIti hetorna hantIti visheSho yukta iti yojyam | na hantItyuchyata ityato na paunaruktyam | nanu buddheralopo nAma svAtantryAbhimAnaparityAgaH | ataH punaruktirityata Aha || buddhiriti || bhavedevaM, 'yasya nAhaN^.hkR^ito bhAvo' 'buddhiryasya na lipyate' ityanayorarthabhedo yadi svAtantryAbhimAnaphalarAgayorubhayorapi bandhakatvaM syAt | tadeva kuta ityata Aha || svAtantryamiti || 17 ||
'daivaM chaiva' itIshvarasya karmasu prerakatvamuktam | tatpreraNAsvarUpaM nirUpyate-'j~nAnam' iti | tatsmR^ityopapAdayati || samprerayituriti || preraNAyA bhagavaddharmatvAt kathaM j~nAtR^itvAdItyata Aha || seti || preraNAyA j~nAnAdirUpabhagavatsvarUpatvena tathAtvamupapadyata ityarthaH | preraNAyAstadA tadA jAyamAsAyAH kathaM bhagavatsvarUpatvamityata Aha || svarUpeNeti || na preraNA tadA tadotpadyate || kintu bhagavatsvarUpatayA sarvadA vidyamAnaiva vyaktirUpeNa jAyate | ato bhagavatsvarUpatvamupapannamiti bhAvaH |
yo.aya preraNAyA vyaktirUpo visheShaH so.api nAnitya iti shaMkanIyam | tasya nityapreraNArUpatvena sadA vidyamAnasyaiva visheShato jAyamAnatvAdityAha || visheSho.apIti || evaM visheShasyApi visheShastasyApItyanavasthA syAdityata Aha || svanirvAhakateti || bhavedanavasthA, yadi preraNAyA bhinno visheShastasyApi tathetyaN^gIkriyate | na chaivam | sA preraNA svarUpameva svAtmAnaM visheShatayA visheShitayA nirvahati | sa visheSho.apyevamityaN^gIkArAdityarthaH | etad dR^iShTAntenopapAdayati || vishiShTavaditi || tadeva vivR^iNoti || visheShyasyeti || asti tAvad visheShyavishiShTayoravipratipanno.abhedaH | dharmadharmibhedavAdinA.api tasyAN^gIkR^itatvAt | na cha visheShyavishiShTayornirvisheShAbhedaH | tathAsati j~nAtR^idevadattashabhdayoH paryAyatvApatteH | na chaivaM visheShyasyApi visheShAN^gIkAreNAnavasthA.asti | visheShyavastunastadvisheShANAM cha svanirvAhakatvAt | evaM IshvarapreraNAyA visheShastasyApi visheSha ityaN^gIkAre na kashchiddoSha iti bhAvaH | bhavedetadvisheShyavishiShTayorabhedasiddhau, sa eva kuta ityata Aha || j~nAturiti || visheShyavishiShTayorbhedAnubhavAbhAvAt abhedAnubhavasadbhAvAchcha na bheda iti bhAvaH | visheShyavishiShTayorabhede.anubhavAntaraM cha darshayati || pashyAmIti || ma iti visheShyamuchyate | visheShaH samutthita iti tasyaiva vishiShTatvam |
visheShaNayuktaM vishiShTam | tadvisheShaNaM nirUpayati || visheShuNamiti || visheShAkhyaM yathA 'yastuno.astitvaM', phalasya nIlatvam' 
iti | itahadatyantabhinnaM daNDAdi | tadubhayamapi visheShaNamiti kasmAduchyata ityata Aha || visheShamiti || aNayet gamayet | nanu daNDAdivisheShaNaM vastuni daNDatvAdivisheShaM gamayati, visheShaH kiM gamayedityata Aha || visheSheti ||
pUrvoktakarmakAraNAni saN^kShipyatrochyante-'karaNaM' iti | tatra karmasaN^grahakathanaM kvopayujyata ityatastadanUdya madhyamapadalopisamAso.ayamiti bhAvena vyAchaShTe || saN^graha iti || kathamadhiShThAnAdipaJNchakasya karaNAditritvamityata Aha || adhiShThAnasyeti || nanu pUrvAnuktakarmaNo.atra kathanAt kathaM teShAmayaM saN^kShepaH syAdityata Aha || karmeti || 18 ||
sAttvikaj~nAnAdisAdhanAnuShThAnAya guNabhedA uchyante-'j~nAnam' iti | tatra, guNAH saN^khyAyante.asminniti guNasaN^khyAnapadena prasiddhasAN^khyashAstramuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || evamiti || prasiddhasAN^khyashAstramevAtra kiM na syAdityata evamityuktam | evaM sarvagatasyeshvarasya sarvato bhedAdiviShayaM j~nAnaM sAttvikamityAdi guNasaN^khyAne prochyata iti hyatrochyate | tachcha paramasAN^khyashAstragrahaNa evopapadyate, na nirIshvarasAN^khyagrahaNa iti bhAvaH || 19 ||
tatra pratij~nAtaM j~nAnatraividhyamuchyate-'sarva' iti | tadapratItyAdi nirAsAya smR^ityaiva vyAchaShTe || astitvAditi || pR^ithaktvenetyantena sarvabhUteShviti saptamyA abhiprAyo.apyukto bhavati | viShNorityAdinA avibhaktamityuktArthaM bhavati | tAratamyenetyanena vibhakteShviti dvedhA vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | atha bhUtashabdena bhavatIti jaDaM chochyata ityabhiptetya vibhakteShvityasyArtha uchyate || jaDebhya iti || tebhyo jaDebhya ityanena saptamyartha ukto bhavati || samyagiti || viShNuH sarvottamaH jIvAstadadhInaj~nAnAdimantaH, jaDaM tadrahitamityato viShNvAdInAM bheda ityarthaH | anenaikamityuktAbhiprAyaM bhavati || 20 ||
viShNorityanena pR^ithaktvenetyuktatAtparyaM bhavati | sAttvikaj~nAnasyApi viShNoranyathra yathArthatvenoktatvAt kathaM rAjasatvamasya syAdityata Aha || yadIti || mishratattvavit sandigdhatayA bhagavatsvarUpaM jAnannityarthaH | anyathetyanena yattvityuktArthaM bhavati | yatkiJNchidekaM kR^itsnaM jAnAtIti chAdau draShTavyam | jAnAtItyantena kArye kR^itsnavat saktamityasya tAtparyamuktaM bhavati | 
kR^itsnamakAryatvAdiguNapUrNaM brahma yathA viShayIkaroti brahmeti tathetyarthaH | sa evetyanena kArye kR^itsnayat saktamityasya kR^itsnapadamakhilajagadviShayamaN^gIkR^itya artAntaramuktaM bhavati | eketyanena ekasmin kArye kR^itsnavatsaktamityuktatAtparyaM bhavati | yuktItvanenAhaitukamityasya yuktirAhityachcha tathA manyata ityarthaH | alpetyanenAlpamityuktArthaM bhavati | alpasamyagj~nAnaM ityarthaH | bhrAntasyApyadhiShThAnAdi viShayasambagj~nAnavattvAt | atattvArthamityanenAtattvArthavadityuktArthaM bhavati | yathAvasthitAkArAd viparItAkAramityarthaH | tattvArthaj~nAnavarjanAditi || yathAsthitAkAraj~nAnAbhAvAdityarthaH |
nanu sarveShu bhUteShu pR^ithaktevena yajj~nAnamityetadeva nAnAbhAvAn pR^ithagvidhAnityuchyate | ataH punaruktideSha ityata Aha || pR^ithaktveneti || vyAkhyAnavyAkhyeyabhAvAt na punaruktideSha iti bhAvaH | nanu sarveShu bhUteShu pR^ithaktvAj~nAnaviShayasya sAttvikatvenoktatvAt kathaM rAjasatvamatrochyata ityata Aha || sarveti || na kevalaM sarveShu bhUteShu pR^ithaktvaviShayaM sAttvikaj~nAnamuktam | kintu tadgateshvaramapR^ithaktvena sarvottamatvena cha viShayIkurvat | tadabhAvAdbhUteShu pR^ithaktvaviShayatve.apyasya rAj~nasatvaM yuktamiti bhAvaH | anena yadIti smR^itirvivR^itA bhavati |
'yattu kR^itsnavadekasmin kArye saktaM j~nAnaM tadahaitukaM, atattvArthavadalpasajj~nAnayuktam' iti niyatamevAtaH taduktau punaruktirityata uktaM vivR^iNvannAha || ekasyeti || yasya kasyachidekasya nAstItyantamuktArthaHvivaraNam | na pUrvoktasyaivAhaitukatvAdivisheShaNAni vidhIyante, yena punaruktiH syAt | kintvahaitukatvAdInAM svayameva tAmasAnAmuktavisheShaNayogitayA atitAmasatvaj~nApanAya uktavisheShaNAnyuchyanta iti bhAvaH | sadasadvailakShaNyAdyavidyamAnAkArakalpanAyuktamityarthaH | evameShAM padAnAM sAmAnAdhikaraNyamaN^gIkR^ityaiva punaruktiM parihR^ityAnekAdhikaraNa tayA.api tAM pariharati || ekasminniti || kArye sarvaM jagaditi, saktamekasmin kArye sarvaM jagaditi chaitAni padAni yojyAnIti vA na punaruktiriti samyaddhyate | nanvevaMvidhaj~nAnasya kvApyabhAvAt tasya tAmasatvakathanaM kathaMmityata Aha || mAyeti || 21-22 ||
guNabhedena karmatraividhyamuchyate-'niyataM' iti | tatra niyatapadena svavarNAshramochitamAtramuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || mayIti || viShNoH sarvottamatvaj~nAnapUrvakaM tadbhaktyA tadarpaNabuddhyA kriyamANameva karma niyatamityatrochyate | na tu svavarNAshramochitatvamAtram | kutaH? 'mayi sarvANi karmANi' iti bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnapurvakaM tadarpaNabuddhyA karmakaraNaM vidhAya 'ye me matamidam' iti tasya mokShAdhanatvokteH | 'ye tvetat' iti tadakaraNe pratyavAyasya chokteH | yatkaraNe phalaprAptiH, yadakaraNe pratyavAyaH tasyaiva niyatatvAditi bhAvaH | bhavatu bhagavadarpaNabuddhya kriyamANaM karma niyatam | tasya bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnAdipUrvakatvaM kutaH mayi sarvANi karmANi ityatra tadanukterityata Aha || adhyAtmeti || sarvAdhike paramAtmani chetaH adhyAtmachetaH | apekShitatayA j~nAyata iti sambaddhyate | bhavedetat, yadyadhyAtmachetaseti padaM bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnArthaM syAt | tadeva kuta ityata Aha || ye tviti || mayi sarvANi iti shlokArthAnuvAdarUpe ye tu sarvANi ityanmin shloke.adhyAtmachetaseti padasya 'matparAH' ityAdinA bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnatatsmaraNAdyarthatayA vyakhyAtatvAt bhavedevaitatpadaM tadarthamiti bhAvaH | ahaM paraH sarvottamo yeShAM te matparAH | na cha vAchyametachChlokasya tachChlokAnuvAdarUpatvaM kuta iti | 'evaM satatayuktA ye ' ityarjunena prAguktaprakArAnuvAdena pR^iShTasya bhagavatastathaiva parihArokteryuktatvAt | samAkhyAvashAchcha etachChlokArthAnuvAditvaM vij~nAyate | kimetanniyatatvaM karmaNa eva sAttvikatve prayojakamuta j~nAnAdInAmapItyata Aha || evamiti || bhagavadarpaNAdikaM chAtra draShTavyam || 23-25 ||
guNabhedataH kartustraividhmuchyate- 'mukta ' iti | tatra kartA chedanahaMvAdIti kathamityata Aha || sarvasyeti || kartA.apyahameva karteti sAttviko na vadati | tena svakartR^itvAdeH sarvasya bhagavadadhInatayA nishchitatvAdityarthaH || 26-27 ||
nanu sAttvikasyApi prakAkR^itatvadIrghasUtritvayoH sadbhAvAt kathaM tattAmasasyaivochyata ityataH tatpadadvayasyArthaM smR^ityaiva darshayati || bhagavaditi || smaranniti | chintayannityarthaH | pashchAt kuryAmiti chintanaM sAttvike.api samamityata Aha || prApteti || yasya karmaNo yaH kAlo vihitaH tasmin kAle prApte.api pashchAt kuryAmiti chintayan dIrghasUtrItyarthaH | anena alasAdapyasya vailakShaNyaM sUchitam | saH prAptakAlaM karma udAsta eveti | nanvevaM cheddIrghasUtritaH stabdhAdInAM utkR^iShTatvAt kathaM tAmasatayA gaNanamityataH gaNanamityataH pramANavAkyenaiva tAmaseShveva tAn vibhajyAha || alasa iti || ayukto bhagavadarpaNAdiyogarahitaH | stabdho nAma AtmasambhAvanayA kvApyanataH | naikR^itiko nIchakarmA | shaTho gUDhadveShI | trividhatAmasAnAM phalamAha || durnaratvamiti || 29-30 ||
 'buddheH ' iti pratij~nAtamuchyate- 'pravR^ittiM ' iti | tatra  'yayA darmamadharmaM ' ityuktaddhyorekaprakAratvAt kathaM rAjasatAmasatvamityataH tadvibhAgaM vAkyAntareNa darshayati || kiJNchiditi || anena  'ayathAvat ' iti niyamena yathAvannetyuktaM bhavati |  'yogena ' iti upAyabalenetyalpArthapratItinirAsAya tad vAkyAntareNa vyAchaShTe || vaiShNava iti || anena yogena yuktyeti pUritaM bhavati | dhR^itishched vyabhichArashUnyaivAto.avyabhichAriNyeti vishiShyAsyA eva kimuchyata ityata Aha || vihiteti || na 
chAtrAvyabhichAritvamaskhalitatvamiti bhAvaH | yayA svapnamityuktamAtraM yayA na muJNchati sA tAmasIti pratItinirAsAyAha || svapnamiti || sarvaniShiddhaM bhagavad.hdveShAdi | bhagavad.hdveShAdeH vR^iddhAniShiddhatvena tAmasatvAt tadviShayadhR^iterapi tAmasatvamiti bhAvaH | vR^iddhaniShiddhatve.api kutastAmasatvamityata Aha || taditi || nanu bhagavad.hdveShAdeH kaishchana vR^iddhairvihitatvAt kathaM tanninditatvamityata Aha || mahAtmAna iti || ye bhagavad.hdveShAdividhAyakA na te vR^iddhAH, kintu bhagavantaM bhajanta eva | tathoktatvAdityarthaH || 35-36 ||
 'sukhaM ' iti pratij~nAtamuchyate- 'abhyAsAt ' iti | tatra  'AtmabuddhiprasAdajaM ' ityasya svamanaHprasAdajamityanyathApratItinirAsAya smR^ityaivArthamAha || viShNoriti || jAtamiti sheShaH | manaHprasAdo nAma manasaH svato.api prAyo viShayAgati H || 37-39 ||
sarvajIvAnAmapi guNatastraividhyamuchyate- 'na tat ' iti | tatra sattvasyApi guNavisheShatvAt kathaM guNabaddhatvamuchyata ityata Aha || sattvamiti || nanu guNAtItaM sattvaM nAstItyetAvatA pUrNatvAt pR^ithivyAM divIti visheShoktiH kimarthetyata Aha || muktAnAmiti || muktAnAM guNabaddhatvAbhAvAt guNAtItaM sattvaM nAstItyukte teShAmapi tatprasaktestadvyAvR^ittyarthaM pR^ithivyAmityAdivisheShoktiryuktetyarthaH |

ityarthaH | paramahaMsAH shikhAyaj~nopavItahInAH ekadaNDinaH | yaj~nopavItanAn ekadaNDI shikhArahito haMsaH | tridaNaDI shikhAyaj~nopavItavAn grAmaikarAtriH bahUdaH | tridaNDI shikhAyaj~napavItavAn yAvajjIvaM putradattAnnAdaH kuTItakaH | adhikaM kramAditi sambaddhyate | tat paramahaMsAnAmapi samaM kimityata Aha || dharmA iti || shamo dama ityAdau brAhmakarmatayoktA ityarthaH | karmabAhulyAd haMsAdInAM rAjasatve devAdInAmapi tadbhAvAd rAjasatvaM syAdityata Aha || devAderiti || kuto netyata Aha || na hIti || karmaNi manashchalatu mA vA, tathApyasti tAvad vahulaM karma | ato haMsAdivadrAjasatvameva devAderityata Aha || anyeShAmiti || na haMsAdiShvapi karma svarUpata eva rajo.anumApakam | kintu chittachalanahetutvenaiva | devAdikarmaNastu tadabhAvAnna rAjasatve liN^gatvamiti bhAvaH | karmaNaH svarUpata eva rajo.anumApakatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha || yadIti || bhagavatsmaraNahetukarmaNaH sattvAnumApakatvadarshanAnna karma svarUpata eva rAjasatvAnumApakamiti bhAvaH | ata eva prAyaH syAdityuktam |
paramahaMsAdarvAg gR^ihasthAntAnAM yat krameNa karmabAhulyamuktaM talleshato vibhajya darshayati || dharmeti || haMsAdiShu karmabAhulyakramo.aneyato draShTavyaH | chaturvidhayatito brahmachAriNaH samidAdichChedanamagnipUjA shrAddhakaraNamiti visheShaH | brahmachArito gR^ihasthasya dArasaN^graho visheShaH | apatyAnutpAdanaM, grAmabhavavastusevAbhAvaH, pashvahiMseti gR^ihasthAd vanasthasya visheSha ityarthaH ra| grAmyasaMtyAgoktyA vanasthasya brahmachArto.api karmAlpatvamuktaM bhavati | itarat svochitaM yaj~nAdi |
rAjasasAttvikeShu bhAgavateShu varNabhedenAnekaprakAreShu viprasvarUpamuktam | kShatriyAdisvarUpaM rAjasarAjasAdisvarUpaM cha vAkyAntareNa darshayati || sAttvikA iti || rAjasasAttvikeShviti draShTavyam | sattvarAjasA iti || samasattvarAjasA ityarthaH | atisvalpasattvAdhikyeneti || tamaso.apyatisvalpatayA sattvamadhikaM yathA tathaivetyarthaH | kShatriyAdimAtrasyaivaM sthitiH kimityata Aha || ya iti || varNabAhyA bhAgavatAshchet kimityata Aha || sattveti || yaH pulkaso.api bhAgavato.asau rAjaseShvapi sattvAdhika ityarthaH | rAjasasAttvikAnuktvA rAjasarAjasAdInAha || traividyeti || kAlato bhAgavatAn jAyamAnAn vyavachChinatti || traividyamAtrA iti || sarvAdhikya iti || sarvaprakAreNAdhikye iti gamayitavyam | sAttvikaprabhedamAha || pitR^igandharveti || shreShTA evetyanena pitR^igandharvapUrvakAH sAttvikatAmasAH, munayaH sAttvikarAjasAH, devA sAttvikasAttvikA ityuchyante |
devAn vibhajyAha || devA iti || kramottarA iti || sAttvikasAttvikeShu bR^ihaspatyAdayastAmasAH, indro rAjaso, brahmAdirudrAvasAnAH sAttvikA ityuchyante | viriJNchAdIn vibhajyAha || shiva iti || uttarottarA iti || sAttvikasAttvikeShu rudrasya tAmasatvaM, sarasvatyA rAjasatvaM, brahmaNaH sAttvikatvamuktaM bhavati | evaM chedviriJNchaH kimuchyata ityata Aha || sattveti || tasmAduktarItyA guNanibandhanameva teShAM tAratamyaM kimityata Aha || muktAviti || guNAbhAve.apyuktaprakArAvasitanukhakrameNaiva tAratabhyopapattiriti bhAvaH | 'narAdhamAstAmaseShu sAttvikAH ' ityuktam | te kIdrashA ityatastadvivR^iNoti || viShNAviti ||  
'rAjasAstu sarAstatra viprA rAjasasAttvikAH ' ityuktam | tatra  'ye tu bhAgavatA varNAH ' iti vachanAntarabalena rAjasasAttvikAnAM bhAgavatatvaM grAhyamiti sUchayan bhAgavataviprANAM rAjasasAttvikatvamevetyanyathApratItinirAsAya anuktaM pUrayati || rAjasAnAmiti || rAjasasAttvikeShu vAkyadvayenoktaM varNabhedaM buddhyArohArthamegIkR^itya darshayati || rAjasastheti || anena  'viprA rAjasasAttvikAH ' ityAdi prAguktarItyA vivR^itaM bhavati | rAjasasAttvikA na sAdhAraNaviprAdayaH | api tu bhAgavatA eveti vAkyAntarAnusAreNoktaM hetvantaraM chAha || sattveti || rAjasasAttvikAnArabhya hiraNyagarbhAvasAnAH sarve.api hi mokShayogyAH | guNAntarApekShayA yeShu sattvAdhikyAnmokShayogyatA cha bhAgavatAnAmeva | ato rAjasasAttvikAdayaH sarve.api bhAgavatA eveti bhAvaH | sattvapradhAnatve.api kuto mokShayogyatetyata Aha || sattvAditi ||  'rajastamashchAbhibhUya sattvaM bhavati ' ityadhikaguNasyetarAbhibhavena svaphalapradatvasyoktatvAt sattvapradhAnye rajastamasorabhibhavena mokShasAdhanaj~nAnasya sambhavAt sattvAdhikye mokSho bhavati | j~nAnasya sattvaphalatAyA uktatvAditi bhAvaH | atra sphuTArthaM vAkyAntaraM chAha || sattvAdhika iti || sattvAdhiko rAjasasAttvikAdiH | tamauttaro narAdhamAdiH | rajobhUyAn traividyaH | samaH ekaprakAreNa guNatrayo.aj~naH || 41 ||
brAhmaNetyuktaM prapaJNchyate- 'shamaH iti | tatra shamAdayo brAhmaNasyaivetyanyathApratItinirAsAya tat pramANAntareNa vyAchaShTe || shama iti || anena brAhmaNe taduktirAdhikyavivakShayetyuktaM bhavati | tapo brahmacharyAdi | shauchaM shuddhiH | kShAntiH krodhAsamutthitiH | ArjavaM manobAkkAyakarmaNAmavaiparItyam | j~nAnaM sAmAnyataH | vij~nAnaM visheShataH | AstikyaM dharmAdau  'astyevAnena mama
