shamAdInAM sAthAraNatve.api kShatriyasya shauryAdayaH sarve.api visheShadharmAH kiM na syuH brAhmaNasyAdhyApanAdimAtraM, shUdrasya shushrUShAmAteraM cha svadharmaH kiM na syAt? ityatasteShAM sAdhAraNyaM pramANena darshayati || shauryamiti || etena kShatriye shauryAdyuktirAdhikyaviShayeti choktaM bhavati | satAmadhyApanaM cha shushrUSheti sambandhaH | shUdrasyAdhyApanaM vinA kimuktaM bhavatItyata Aha || tasmAditi || shushrUShAyAH sarvadharmatvAdityarthaH | satAmiti sambaddhyate | shauryAdInAM sAdhAraNatve kShatriyAdInAM ke visheShaguNA ityata Aha || eta iti || sAdhAraNatayoktebhyo.anye yuddhe.apalAyanaishvaryAdaya ityarthaH | naisargikA asAdhAraNAH | kimete puMsAmasAdhAraNA eva dharmA niyatyA bhavantItyata Aha || syAditi || eteShAmasAdhAraNatvAdavashyAnuShTheyatvamiti cha nAshaN^.hkanIyamityAha || balAditi || yathA brAhmaNasya jIvanArthaM yAjanamityAdi | evamasAdhAraNyenAtmIyatvAbhAve.api tyAjyatvaM cha na mantavyamityAha || anisarga iti || yathA brAhmaNasya jIvanArthamadhyApanamityAdi | uktasyApavAdamAha || yAjaneti || asvAbhAvikAH shubhA api sAdhAraNA eva vardhanIyAH | na tu viprAdyasAdhAraNA yAjanAdaya ityarthaH | shauryAdInAmasAdhAraNatvoktyA yuddhe.apalAyanamaishvaryaM cha kShatriyasya visheShadharmAvityuktam || tasyApavAdamAha || apalAyanamiti || viprakShatrArthamiti visheShoktyA sAmAnyataH kShatriyasyaiva siddhyati | tato noktavirodhaH |
yathA kShatriyaikadharmatayoktaM yuddhe.apalAyanaM kAraNavisheShAdanyeShAmapi syAttathaivaishvaryamapyanyadharmaH syAt kim? ityataH tatsvarUpanirUpaNapUrvakaM tasya kShatriyetareShvavR^ittiM pramANena darshayati || prasahyeti || prasahya vittaharaNAdi keShAmityataH tadvadanUnakAryaH kShatriyetarairityasya vyAvartyamAha || sarva iti || tarhi kiM brAhmaNAdibhirvidharmiNAM shAsanameva na kAryamityata Aha || aN^gAdIti || shiShyo nAma kIdR^isha ityata Aha || shiShyashcheti || tarhi putrAdInAmashAsanaprasaN^ga ityata Aha || putreti || anisargashiShyasvarUpaM taditi bhAvaH | na kevalaM brAhmaNAdeyaiH shiShyA eva shAsyAH kintu gurvAdayo.apItyAha || gurava iti || shikShaNIyeShu bhAveShviti || shikShaNIyArthaviShaya ityarthaH | na kevalaM gurvAdaya eva shAsyAH kintvaj~nAtA apItyAha || pApamiti || atra sarvatra aN^gAdyahAnikR^iddaNDaH shiShyeShu guravashcha deshakAlAnusArata iti visheShoktyA kShatriyAdvisheSho draShTavyaH | pApaM charanto vAraNIyA ityuktam | yadi svottamavirodhAkhyaM mahApApaM kuryustarhi kiM kAryamityata Aha || taditi || kiM sahasA tyAjyA evetyata Aha || yatheti || svottamaviroddhAro gurvAdayaH kiM sarvathA tyAjyA evetyata Aha || viShNAviti || tachChikShAprakAramAha || shikShayanniti || viShNau paramabhaktaH svottamavirodhetarapApamAcharati chet kiM kAryamityata Aha || mahAnta iti ||
prasaN^gAdviprAdInAm ApaddhakmAn smR^ityA darshayati || Apatsviti || kShAtriyasya vipradharmAcharaNe visheShamAha || kShatriya iti || bhikShetarahiraNyAdipratigrAhI syAdityarthaH | shaudraM tu dharmamAcharediti sambaddhyate | na shUdrastu viprakShatriyayordharmamAcharedityuktam | tarhyApatsu tena ko dharma AshrayaNIya ityata Aha || shUdra iti || shUdrasya vaishyadharmatve visheShamAha || shUdra iti || vedAkSharAdishravaNAdimAn na bhavedtyarthaH | kShatriyo brAhmamApatsu, tadApatsu vishAM dharmamAcharedityuktam | tato.apyApadi kiM kAryamityata Aha || atyApadIti || viprakShatriyeShu shUdradharmaM shushrUShaNaM charannityarthaH | na kevalaM kShatriyaH shUdradharmaM charan na dupyatItyeva, kiM tarhItyata Aha || yeShviti || yadi kShatriyasya svadharmakR^itAvApado bhavanti tarhi tasya sAnubandhAt svamino balAdhikye.api dharmArthaM tamanabhibhUya yeShu karmasu niyuktaH svaminA.api yAchyaH syAnna tu svayaM yAchitA | tAni shaudrANyapi karmANyarthAdyarthaM sevamAnasya viprAdidharmopajIvanAdipi varo dharmo bhavatItyarthaH | tatra svAmyanabhibhavAdapi svAminA yAchyatvaM visheSheNa dharmakAraNamityAha || prabhuNeti || vipradharmAdyAshrayaNe paropajIvanAbhAvAt shUdradharme dadbhAvAt kathaM sAnubandhAt prabhorbalAdhikyAdau satyapi tato.asya varatvamityata Aha || bAhvoriti || sarvasya tadIyatvAnna paropajIvanamiti bhAvaH || 48 ||
 'sve sve karmaNyabhirataH saMsiddhiM labhate ' ityuktasyaiva itthambhAvAntaramuchyate- 'asakta ' iti | tatra naiShkarmyasiddhipadasya mokShArthatvapratItinirAsAyArthamAha || naiShkarmyeti || sarvapadamaprArabdhaviShayam || 49 ||
asaktetyAdinA naiShkarmyasiddhisAdhanavivaraNapratij~nApUrvakaM tadanantaraphalamuchyate- 'siddhiM ' iti | tatra naiShkarmyasiddhyanantaraM cha yenopAyena paraMbrahmApnoti taM prakAraM nibodhetyanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || vakShyamANeti || atra yathA yena vakShyamANaprakAreNa vartamAno neShkarmyasiddhiM prApto bhUtvA mahAlakShmIM prApnoti taM prakAraM nibodhetyevochyate | na tu naiShkarmyasiddhyanantaraM parabrahmaprAptisAdhanaM nibodhetyarthaH | brahmashabdasya lakShmIvAchakatvameva kuta ityata Aha || mameti || atra brahmapadena parabrahmaiva kiM na syAdityata Aha || brahmeti || etadbrahmaprAptyanantaramapi parabrahmaiva kiM na syAdityata Aha || brahmeti || etadbrahmaprAptyanantaramapi bhaktyAdilAshravaNAt lakShmItattvamevedaM, na tu paraM brahmetyarthaH | bhavedetadyadi naiShkarmyasiddhiM prAptasya lakShmIprAptyanantaramapi bhaktyAdilAbho.asti, na tu parabrahmaprAptyanantaramiti siddhyati | tadeva kuta ityata Aha || sarveti || pApapadam aprArabdhAniShTakarmaparam | nanvaparokShaj~nAnino hi naiShkarmyasiddhiH | tatkathaM tadanantaramapi j~nAnAdilAbhaH? tathAtve muktAvApi tatprasaN^gAdityata Aha || aparokSheti || purA dehatyAgAt | aparokShaj~nAnAnantaramapi j~nAnAdivR^iddhirbhavedeva | na chAtiprasaN^gaH | pramANAnuguNena muktau tadabhAvopapatteriti bhAvaH || 50-52 ||
yaduktaM naiShkarmyasiddhisAdhanaM nibodhetyevochyate, na tu tadanantaraM brahmaprAptisAdhanamiti | tadayuktam | buddhyA vishuddhayetyAdisAdhanamuktvA brahmabhUyAya kalpata ityuktatvAt | anyathA naiShkarmyasiddhiM prApto bhUtveti vaktavyatvAdityAshaMkAM pariharan brahmabhUyapadasyAnyathApratItinirAsAyArthamAha || vimuchyeti || j~nAnAnantaraM lakShmIprAptau sAdhanAnAmanAvashyakatvAt naiShkarmyasiddhiM prApto bhUtvetyatrAbhipretameveti bhAvaH || 53-55 ||
 'yataH pravR^ittiH ' ityuktameva vishiShyate- 'sarva ' iti | tatra madvyapAshrayashchet yatheShTato niShiddhAnyaniShiddhAni vA sarvamarmANi kurvANaH shAshvataM padaM prApnotItyanyathApratItinirAsAya tadvyAchaShTe || vihitAnIti || madvyapAshraya iti || mayyeva samarpayannityarthaH | pratItArtha eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || na hIti || nAtra yatheShTato niShiddhAniShiddhakarmAcharaNe tAtparyaM kalpyam | tathAsati bhagavadAshrayasya vihitAkAraNe.apyatra tAtparyaprasaN^gAt | niShiddhakaraNavihitAkaraNayoH samAnatvadityarthaH | atra bhagavadAshritasya vihitAkaraNe.api tAtparyaM syAdevetyata Aha|| mAmiti || yadyatra bhagavadAshritasya vihitAkaraNe.api tAtparyaM tarhi bhagavadAshritasyaivArjunasya  'mAmanusmara udhya cha ' ityAdau vihitayuddhAkaraNe  'atha chettvamimaM dharmyaM ' ityAdau prAk pratyavAya uktaH | tadvirodhaH syAditi bhAvaH 
| pratItArthAnaN^gIkAre.apishabdavaiyyarthyamityata Aha || apIti || 55 ||
yadi bhagavadAshritatayA vihitakarma kurvato kurvato muktistirhi traividyasyApi syAt | tasyApi vihitakarmANi kR^itvA bhagavadarpaNasadbhAvena bhagavadAshritAvishiShTatvAdityAshaMkAparihArAya shlokamavatArayati || bhagavaditi || bhagavadAshritatraividyayorvihitakaraNAdisAmye.api mokShabhAvAbhAvAvupapadyeti | vihitAsheShakarmANi chetasA bhagavati saMnyasya bhagavadAshritaH karoti | na tathA traividya iti tayoshchaitasaiva visheShasadbhAvAditi bhAvaH | matpara iti traividyAdbhAgavatasya visheSha uchyate | tatra bhagavati tAtparyavAnityarthAN^gIkAre tat traividyasyApi samam | ahaM paraH sarvottamo yasyetyabhyupagame vA vasyuni vikalpAyogAt tadapi traividye samamityata Aha || sa eveti || paraH sarvaprakAreNeti sheShaH | bhAvaH sarvadeti cha draShTavyam | 
evaM chenmachchitta iti punaruktiH syAt | na hi bhagavatsarvottamatvabhAvAdanyat tachchitvamastItyAshaMkAparihArAya tadarthamAha || tatreti || tatra bhagavati | traividyAd bhAgavatasya visheSha iti sheShaH | tarhi buddhiyogamupAshrityeti punaruktiH syAt | bhagavati buddheryogo hi buddhiyoga ityata Aha || buddhIti || buddherj~nAnasya yogaH pratyAhArAdyupAya ityarthaH | atha chettvamahaN^.hkArAdityabhyupagamyoktam || 57-58 ||
taduktAkaraNamashakyaM cha tavetyuchyate-'yadi' iti | tatra prakR^itipadena svabhAvAdyuchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || prakR^itiriti || IshvarechChAyAH prakR^itishabdavAchyatvaM kuta ityata Aha || prakR^itiriti || prasaN^gAdatroktArthamanyatrApyatidishati || eSheti || atra prakR^itishabdaH parameshvarechChAvAchI kutaH? svabhAvAdyartha eva kiM na syAdityata Aha || tasyA eveti || prakR^itistvAM niyokShyatItyatra prakR^iteH jIvAniyoktR^itvamuchyate | tachcheshvarechChAyA eva mukhyamiti saivAtrochyata iti bhAvaH | nanu svAbhAvajenetyetadvivaraNAtmakottarashloke prakR^itishabdasya svabhAvArthatva grahaNAt kathaM netyata Aha || svabhAveti || jIvamiti seShaH | neyaM prakR^itiruttaratra svabhAvapadenochyate, kintvasyA jIvaniyoge sAdhanatayA svabhAvAdyuttaratrochyata iti bhAvaH | ito.apyatreshvarechChaiva prakR^itishabdArtha ityAha || tadeveti || etadvivaraNAtmakottarashlapoke bhagavadichChAyA eva sarvaniyoktR^itvasyoktatvAchcha atra prakR^itipadaM tadarthamiti bhAvaH | mAyetIshvarechChaivochyate || 59-61 ||
IshvaraH sarvabhUtAnAmityAdau bhagavateshvarasya pArokShyeNa nirdiShTatvAdayamIshvaro bhagavato.anya iti pratItinirAsAyAha || nishchiteti || parokShyeNokteH anyathA.apyapapatterna tanmAtreNeshvarasya bhagavadatiritaktatvaM kalpyamiti bhAvaH | itashcha tanna kalpyamityAha || maditi || atra tameva sharaNaM gachCha ityanyavyAvR^ittyA IshvarasharaNaprAptimuddiShyopasaMhAre 'manmanA bhava' ityAdinA svasharaNaprAptyupadeshAchcha na bhagavaditaro.ayamIshvaraH | anyathA vyAhateriti bhAvaH | sthAnaM prApsyasi shAshvataM' ityuktaM shAshvatasthAnaM kimityata Aha || shAshvatamiti || sarvasthAnAnAM pralaye vinAshAt kathaM vaikuNThAdeH shAshvatatvamityata Aha || shrIreveti || 63 ||
'idaM tu te guhyatamaM' iti pratij~nAya yajj~nAnAdipadoditaM guhyatamaM tattvamuktaM tadevAtra sarvaguhyatamaM iti punaruchyata ityanyathApratItinirAsAyAha || tattveti || nAtra 'iti guhyatamaM' iti vAkyasheShAdupasaMhR^itatvaM j~nAtavyam | tarhi kimatra guhyatamamuchyata ityata Aha || atreti || nanu 'etadbuddhvA buddhimAn syAt' iti sAdhanasArasyopasaMhR^itatvAt kathamatra taduktirityata uktam || tattveti || na tatra sAdhanasArasyopasaMhArarUpeNa bhagavatsarvottamatvaj~nAnaprashaMsA kR^itA | kintu tajj~nAnamAtreNa mokShasadbhAvAt kimasya mahimA varNanIya iti bhagavatprashaMsArthameveti bhAvaH | tatroktaguhyatamasyAtrAnuktatvevarNanIya iti vyarthamityata Aha || manmAnA iti || sAdhanasArasya prAguktatvAt tadapekShayA bhUya ityupapadyata iti bhAvaH | tarhi punaruktiH syAdityataH sAdhanasAropasaMhAra ityuktam | nanu 'manmanA bhava' ityAdinA.anyavyAvR^ittipUrvakaM svabhajanasyAtropadiShTatvena bhagavatsArvottamatvamevoktamiti kathaM tattvasArakathanaM netyata Aha || arthata iti || satyamatra viShNvAdhikyamuktamiti | tathApyanyabhajananirAsapUrvakaM svabhajanopadeshAnyathAnupapattyaivoktam | na tu mukhataH | ato nAtra tattvasArakathanamiti bhAvaH || 64-65 ||
anyabhajananirAsattyAtra akR^itatvAt kathamarthato.api viShNvAdhikyamuktamityata Aha || aneti || anyadharmAn sarvAn parityajya manmAna bhavetyevaM prakAreNa sarvadharmAn parityajyeti vachanaM manmanA ityAdyuktasheShatvena hi vartate | ato.anyavyAvR^ittipUrvakaM svabhajanamatropadiShTameveti bhAvaH | nanvatra manmanA ityAdyuktasarvadharmAn parityajya mAmekaM sharaNaM vrajetyupadishyata iti kiM na syAdityata Aha || mAmiti || 'mAmekaM sharaNaM vraja' ityanenanApi manmanA ityAdyuktasyaiva vyAkhyAyamAnatvAdanyathA.arthakalpane manmanastvAdikaM parityajyAnutiShThasya cheti vyAhatoktiH syIditi bhAvaH vyarthamidamuktavyAkhayAnamityato nigamanAtmanetyuktam | manmanA bhavetyAdinA kimuktaM bhavati mAmekaM sharaNaM vraja iti vyAkhyAnatvaM draShTavyam |
bhavedetadyadi bhagavanmanastvAdikaM sharaNAgatiH syAt, tadeva kuta ityata Aha || sarvottamatveti || atra yathAsambhavaM manmanA ityAdyuktArthenaikArthatvaM draShTavyam | trividhA manovachanasharIrabhavA | svabhAvataH na phalAntarApekShayA | mokShaphalapradetyanena 
mAmevaiShyasItyuktArthe bhavati | mAmekamiti sarvadharmAnityasya vyAkhyAnaM draShTavyam | 'ahaM tvA sarva ityarthaH | nanvarjunena svoktamadyApi nAN^gIkR^itam | tatkathaM bhagavatA tadbodhanaM samApyata ityAshaMkAM 'yathechChasi tathA kuru' iti yatheShaTAcharaNamanuj~nAyata ityanyathApratItiM parAkurvan pariharati || yatheti || bhagavaduktAnusaraNamarjunena kR^itamityatraivoktatvAt 
tataH prAgeva tajj~nasya bhagavataH tadbodhanoparamo yukta iti bhAvaH || 73-78 ||
atha samApitagrantho.ayaM bhagavAnAchAryaH svapratipAditaprakArameva vAsudevaM namati || nama iti || svasvarUpaparij~nAnasyApi kaivalyAdyakhilapuruShArthahetutvAt svakR^itAM granthanirmANarUpaparicharyAM keshave samarpayan tadAha || yasyeti || atha tameva harimAdaravisheShAt punaH stauti || niHsheSheti || bhUtirmahAlakShmIH |
shrImadAnandatIrthAryahR^idayAmalamandiraH |
indirAramaNaH prItiM yAtu dInadayAparaH ||
iti shrImadAnandatIrithabhagavatpAdAchAryavirachitasya shrImadbhagavadgItAtAtparyanirNayasya TIkAyAM jayatIrthamunivirachitAyAM nyAyadIpikAyAM aShTAdasho.adhyAyaH || 18 ||
